if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
task.wait(0.1)

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
-- INSTA RESET (mvps_priv1 method)
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
local function _newGUID()
    local hex = "0123456789abcdef"
    local t = {}
    for i = 1, 32 do t[#t+1] = hex:sub(math.random(1,16), math.random(1,16)) end
    return table.concat(t, "", 1, 8) .. "-" .. table.concat(t, "", 9, 12)
        .. "-" .. table.concat(t, "", 13, 16) .. "-" .. table.concat(t, "", 17, 20)
        .. "-" .. table.concat(t, "", 21, 32)
end

GUID = GUID or _G.SXE_RESET_GUID or _newGUID()
resetRemote = nil
instaResetCooldown = false

-- Hook FireServer para capturar el remote RE/* del juego
local _mvpsOldFS; _mvpsOldFS = hookfunction(Instance.new("RemoteEvent").FireServer, function(self, ...)
    local args = {...}
    local arg1 = args[1]
    if not resetRemote and self.Name:sub(1, 3) == "RE/" then
        resetRemote = self
    end
    if #self.Name == 67 and arg1 and typeof(arg1) == "string" then
        if string.find(arg1, "StopTrying") then return end
    end
    return _mvpsOldFS(self, ...)
end)

do
    local _Players     = game:GetService("Players")
    local _RS          = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    local _Workspace   = game:GetService("Workspace")
    local _StarterGui  = game:GetService("StarterGui")
    local _newcc       = newcclosure or function(f) return f end
    local _LocalPlayer = _Players.LocalPlayer

    local _resetRemotes    = {}
    local _TargetRemote    = nil
    local _rawFS2          = nil

    local _ResetConfig = {
        RemoteKeywords   = {"reset","kill","die","suicide","respawn","clear","death","damage","reavatar"},
        BlacklistedRemotes = {"AdminReset","StaffReset","ModReset"},
    }

    local function _scanForRemotes()
        table.clear(_resetRemotes)
        task.spawn(function()
            local areas = {_RS, _Workspace}
            local pg = _LocalPlayer:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
            if pg then table.insert(areas, pg) end
            local count = 0
            for _, area in ipairs(areas) do
                local queue = {area}
                while #queue > 0 do
                    local cur = table.remove(queue, 1)
                    count = count + 1
                    if count % 150 == 0 then task.wait() end
                    pcall(function()
                        for _, child in ipairs(cur:GetChildren()) do
                            if child:IsA("RemoteEvent") or child:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
                                local nl = child.Name:lower()
                                local match = false
                                for _, kw in ipairs(_ResetConfig.RemoteKeywords) do
                                    if nl:find(kw, 1, true) then match = true; break end
                                end
                                if match then
                                    local bl = false
                                    for _, b in ipairs(_ResetConfig.BlacklistedRemotes) do
                                        if child.Name:find(b, 1, true) then bl = true; break end
                                    end
                                    if not bl then table.insert(_resetRemotes, child) end
                                end
                            elseif child:IsA("Folder") or child:IsA("Configuration") or child:IsA("Model") or child:IsA("Tool") then
                                table.insert(queue, child)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end)
    end

    -- Hook secundario para capturar ToolActivationController heartbeat remote
    pcall(function()
        local seen = {}
        local capturing = true
        local function handleFire(self, ...)
            if not capturing then return end
            if not self:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end
            local a1 = (select("#", ...) >= 1) and (select(1, ...)) or nil
            if typeof(a1) ~= "string" then return end
            local nm = self.Name
            if type(nm) ~= "string" or not nm:match("^RE/%x%x%x%x%x%x%x%x") then return end
            local callingScript = nil
            pcall(function() callingScript = getcallingscript() end)
            local isMatch = callingScript == nil or
                (callingScript.Name == "ToolActivationController" or
                 callingScript.Name:find("ToolActivationController"))
            if isMatch then
                local c = (seen[self] or 0) + 1
                seen[self] = c
                if c >= 2 then
                    _TargetRemote = self
                    capturing = false
                    seen = nil
                end
            end
        end
        if hookfunction then
            local dummy = function(s,...) return s end
            _rawFS2 = dummy
            _rawFS2 = hookfunction(Instance.new("RemoteEvent").FireServer, _newcc(function(self, ...)
                pcall(handleFire, self, ...)
                return (_rawFS2 ~= dummy and _rawFS2 or Instance.new("RemoteEvent").FireServer)(self, ...)
            end))
        elseif hookmetamethod then
            local oldNC
            oldNC = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", _newcc(function(self, ...)
                local method = getnamecallmethod()
                if (method == "FireServer" or method == "fireServer") and self:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                    pcall(handleFire, self, ...)
                end
                return oldNC(self, ...)
            end))
        end
    end)

    task.spawn(_scanForRemotes)

    local function instantReset()
        if instaResetCooldown then return end
        instaResetCooldown = true
        _G.skipAutoTPAfterReset = true  -- no hacer auto TP tras insta reset
        local lp = _LocalPlayer
        local oldChar = lp.Character
        task.spawn(function()
            local t0 = os.clock()

            -- Primario: remote capturado por el hook inicial (resetRemote de mvps)
            while not resetRemote and not _TargetRemote and (os.clock() - t0) < 3 do task.wait() end
            local primary = resetRemote or _TargetRemote
            while primary and lp.Character == oldChar and (os.clock() - t0) < 5 do
                pcall(function() primary:FireServer("randomstring") end)
                task.wait()
            end

            -- Fallback 1: remotes escaneados por keyword
            if lp.Character == oldChar and #_resetRemotes > 0 then
                local t1 = os.clock()
                while lp.Character == oldChar and (os.clock() - t1) < 3 do
                    for _, remote in ipairs(_resetRemotes) do
                        pcall(function()
                            if remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then remote:FireServer()
                            elseif remote:IsA("RemoteFunction") then remote:InvokeServer() end
                        end)
                    end
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end

            -- Fallback 2: LoadCharacter / matar humanoid directamente
            if lp.Character == oldChar then
                pcall(function() lp:LoadCharacter() end)
                task.wait(0.3)
                if lp.Character == oldChar then
                    pcall(function()
                        local hum = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        if hum then hum.Health = 0 end
                    end)
                end
            end

            instaResetCooldown = false
            -- Limpiar flag despues de un breve delay para no bloquear TPs futuros
            task.delay(5, function() _G.skipAutoTPAfterReset = false end)
        end)
    end

    -- Redirigir el boton Reset del menu Esc
    local _resetBindable = Instance.new("BindableEvent")
    _resetBindable.Event:Connect(function() pcall(instantReset) end)
    task.spawn(function()
        for _ = 1, 12 do
            local ok = pcall(function()
                _StarterGui:SetCore("ResetButtonCallback", _resetBindable)
            end)
            if ok then break end
            task.wait(1)
        end
    end)

    -- Exponer globalmente (el hub lo llama como _G.instantReset)
    _G.instantReset  = instantReset
    _G.InstantReset  = instantReset
    _G.executeReset  = instantReset
end
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
-- FIN INSTA RESET

if _G.dxhubHubLoaded then
    if _G.dxhubHubCleanup then pcall(_G.dxhubHubCleanup) end
    task.wait(0.1)
end

local _allConnections = {}
local _loopFlags = {} -- for stopping task.spawn loops on cleanup

local function _track(conn)
    if conn and typeof(conn) == "RBXScriptConnection" then
        table.insert(_allConnections, conn)
    end 
    return conn
end

local function _disconnectAll()
    for _, conn in ipairs(_allConnections) do
        pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end)
    end
    table.clear(_allConnections)
    _loopFlags.running = false
end

_loopFlags.running = true

local function getWindowScaledPosition(guiObject)
    local GuiService = game:GetService("GuiService")
    local rbxWindowInset = GuiService:GetGuiInset()
    local absPos = guiObject.AbsolutePosition
    local absSize = guiObject.AbsoluteSize
    local x = absPos.X + absSize.X / 2
    local y = absPos.Y + absSize.Y / 2
    local y_adjusted = y + rbxWindowInset.Y
    return x, y_adjusted
end

local b64chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/'

local function getNearestPlot()
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return nil end

    local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not root then return nil end

    local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if not plotsFolder then return nil end

    local nearestPlot = nil
    local shortestDistance = math.huge

    for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
        if plot:IsA("Model") then
            local referencePart = plot.PrimaryPart or plot:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
            if referencePart then
                local distance = (root.Position - referencePart.Position).Magnitude
                if distance < shortestDistance then
                    shortestDistance = distance
                    nearestPlot = plot
                end
            end
        end
    end

    return nearestPlot
end

local function base64encode(data)
    return (data:gsub('.', function(x) 
        local r,b='',x:byte()
        for i=8,1,-1 do r=r..(b%2^i-b%2^(i-1)>0 and '1' or '0') end
        return r;
    end):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?', function(x)
        if (#x < 6) then x=x..'0' end
        if (#x < 6) then x=x..'0' end
        local c=0
        for i=1,6 do c=c+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(6-i) or 0) end
        return b64chars:sub(c+1,c+1)
    end)..({ '', '==', '=' })[#data%3+1])
end

local function base64decode(data)
    data = string.gsub(data, '[^'..b64chars..'=]', '')
    return (data:gsub('.', function(x)
        if (x == '=') then return '' end
        local r,f='',(b64chars:find(x)-1)
        for i=6,1,-1 do r=r..(f%2^i-f%2^(i-1)>0 and '1' or '0') end
        return r;
    end):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?', function(x)
        if (#x ~= 8) then return '' end
        local c=0
        for i=1,8 do c=c+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(8-i) or 0) end
        return string.char(c)
    end))
end

local QuantumClone
do
    QuantumClone = function()
        task.spawn(function()
            pcall(function()
                local character = player.Character
                if not character then return end

                local hum = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if not hum then return end

                local quantumCloner =
                    LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Quantum Cloner")
                    or character:FindFirstChild("Quantum Cloner")

                if not quantumCloner then return end

                if quantumCloner.Parent == LocalPlayer.Backpack then
                    hum:EquipTool(quantumCloner)
                end
                task.wait(0.05)
                quantumCloner:Activate()
                task.wait(0.0279)

                pcall(function()
                    local playerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
                    local toolsFrames = playerGui:FindFirstChild("ToolsFrames")
                    if not toolsFrames then return end

                    local qcGui = toolsFrames:FindFirstChild("QuantumCloner")
                    if not qcGui then return end

                    local tpBtn = qcGui:FindFirstChild("TeleportToClone")
                    if not tpBtn then return end

                    local connections = getconnections(tpBtn.MouseButton1Up)
                    if connections[1] then
                        connections[1]:Fire()
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end)
    end
end

local Settings = { StealRadius = 20, StealDuration = 0.25 }

local plotCache = {}
local plotCacheTime = {}
local cachedPrompts = {}
local promptCacheTime = 0
local PROMPT_CACHE_REFRESH = 0.1

local function isMyPlotByName(plotName)
    local currentTime = tick()
    if plotCache[plotName] and (currentTime - (plotCacheTime[plotName] or 0)) < 2 then return plotCache[plotName] end
    local plots = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if not plots then plotCache[plotName] = false; plotCacheTime[plotName] = currentTime; return false end
    local plot = plots:FindFirstChild(plotName)
    if not plot then plotCache[plotName] = false; plotCacheTime[plotName] = currentTime; return false end
    local sign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
    if sign then
        local yourBase = sign:FindFirstChild("YourBase")
        if yourBase and yourBase:IsA("BillboardGui") then
            local result = yourBase.Enabled == true
            plotCache[plotName] = result; plotCacheTime[plotName] = currentTime
            return result
        end
    end
    plotCache[plotName] = false; plotCacheTime[plotName] = currentTime
    return false
end

local function findNearestPrompt()
    local char = player.Character
    if not char then return nil end
    local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not root then return nil end
    local currentTime = tick()
    if currentTime - promptCacheTime < PROMPT_CACHE_REFRESH and #cachedPrompts > 0 then
        local nearestPrompt, nearestDist = nil, math.huge
        for _, data in ipairs(cachedPrompts) do
            if data.spawn then
                local dist = (data.spawn.Position - root.Position).Magnitude
                if dist <= Settings.StealRadius and dist < nearestDist then
                    nearestPrompt = data.prompt; nearestDist = dist
                end
            end
        end
        if nearestPrompt then return nearestPrompt end
    end
    cachedPrompts = {}; promptCacheTime = currentTime
    local plots = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if not plots then return nil end
    local nearestPrompt, nearestDist = nil, math.huge
    for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do
        if isMyPlotByName(plot.Name) then continue end
        local podiums = plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums")
        if not podiums then continue end
        for _, podium in ipairs(podiums:GetChildren()) do
            pcall(function()
                local base = podium:FindFirstChild("Base")
                local spawn = base and base:FindFirstChild("Spawn")
                if spawn then
                    local attachment = spawn:FindFirstChild("PromptAttachment")
                    if attachment then
                        for _, child in ipairs(attachment:GetChildren()) do
                            if child:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                local dist = (spawn.Position - root.Position).Magnitude
                                table.insert(cachedPrompts, {prompt = child, spawn = spawn})
                                if dist <= Settings.StealRadius and dist < nearestDist then
                                    nearestPrompt = child; nearestDist = dist
                                end
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
    return nearestPrompt
end

local function parsePetValue(text)
    if not text then return 0 end
    local lower = string.lower(text)
    local num = tonumber(lower:match("[%d%.]+")) or 0
    if lower:find("t") then num = num * 1e12
    elseif lower:find("b") then num = num * 1e9
    elseif lower:find("m") then num = num * 1e6
    elseif lower:find("k") then num = num * 1e3 end
    return num
end

local function tryCarpetEquip(maxAttempts)
    for attempt = 1, (maxAttempts or 5) do
        pcall(function()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return end
            local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not hum or hum.Health <= 0 then return end
            local carpetInChar = char:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
            if carpetInChar and carpetInChar:IsA("Tool") then return end
            local bp = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")
            if not bp then bp = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack", 1) end
            if bp then
                local carpet = bp:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                if not carpet then carpet = bp:WaitForChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet", 0.5) end
                if carpet and carpet:IsA("Tool") and carpet.Parent == bp then
                    task.wait(0.1)
                    hum:EquipTool(carpet)
                end
            end
        end)
        task.wait(0.2)
        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
        if char and char:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet") then break end
    end
end

local SAVE_FILE = "22SHub_Keybinds.json"

local fileSystemAvailable = (writefile ~= nil) and (readfile ~= nil) and (isfile ~= nil)

local function safeRead()
    if not fileSystemAvailable then return {} end
    local ok, data = pcall(function()
        if isfile(SAVE_FILE) then
            return HttpService:JSONDecode(readfile(SAVE_FILE))
        end
        return {}
    end)

    return ok and type(data) == "table" and data or {}
end

local function safeWrite(data)
    if not fileSystemAvailable then return end
    pcall(function()
        writefile(SAVE_FILE, HttpService:JSONEncode(data))
    end)
end

local function colorToTable(c)
    if typeof(c) == "Color3" then
        return {R = c.R, G = c.G, B = c.B}
    end
    return nil
end

local function tableToColor(t)
    if type(t) == "table" and t.R then
        return Color3.new(t.R, t.G, t.B)
    end
    return nil
end

local function keyName(k)
    if typeof(k) == "EnumItem" then return k.Name end
    return nil
end

local function stringToKeyCode(name)
    if type(name) ~= "string" then return nil end
    local ok, result = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[name] end)
    return ok and result or nil
end

local function loadKey(globalName, default)
    _G[globalName] = stringToKeyCode(savedBinds[globalName]) or _G[globalName] or default
end

loadKey("AutoTurretKey", Enum.KeyCode.G)

local _saveQueued = false
local _lastSaveTime = 0
local SAVE_DEBOUNCE = 10

local function queueSave()
    if _saveQueued then return end
    _saveQueued = true
    task.spawn(function()
        local elapsed = tick() - _lastSaveTime
        if elapsed < SAVE_DEBOUNCE then
            task.wait(SAVE_DEBOUNCE - elapsed)
        end
        _saveQueued = false
        _lastSaveTime = tick()
        pcall(_G.saveKeybinds)
    end)
end

task.spawn(function()
    task.wait(30)
    while _loopFlags.running do
        task.wait(SAVE_DEBOUNCE)
        if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
    end
end)

_G.autoSaveConfig = _G.saveKeybinds

-- ============================================================
-- ============================================================
_G.preTeleportSave = function()
    pcall(function() if _G.saveKeybinds then _G.saveKeybinds() end end)
    pcall(function() if _G.autoSavePositions then _G.autoSavePositions() end end)
end

-- ============================================================
-- ============================================================
local _inputHandlers = {} -- keyed by KeyCode name -> {priority, handler}
local _inputDispatcherActive = false

local function registerKeyHandler(keyCode, priority, handler)
    local name = typeof(keyCode) == "EnumItem" and keyCode.Name or tostring(keyCode)
    if not _inputHandlers[name] then _inputHandlers[name] = {} end
    table.insert(_inputHandlers[name], {priority = priority or 0, handler = handler})
    table.sort(_inputHandlers[name], function(a, b) return a.priority > b.priority end)
end

local function setupInputDispatcher()
    if _inputDispatcherActive then return end
    _inputDispatcherActive = true

    _track(UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end

        local keyName = input.KeyCode.Name
        local handlers = _inputHandlers[keyName]
        if handlers then
            for _, entry in ipairs(handlers) do
                local ok, result = pcall(entry.handler, input, gameProcessed)
                if ok and result == true then
                    break -- handler consumed the input
                end
            end
        end
    end))
end

_G.registerKeyHandler = registerKeyHandler

pcall(function()
    if readfile and isfile and isfile("22SHub_Positions.json") then
        local jsonStr = readfile("22SHub_Positions.json")
        _G.SAVED_UI_POSITIONS = HttpService:JSONDecode(jsonStr)
    end
end)

-- Autoexec fix: AdminPanel puede no existir aun al cargar
local path = nil
pcall(function()
    local pg = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui", 5)
    if pg then
        local ap = pg:WaitForChild("AdminPanel", 3)
        if ap then path = ap:WaitForChild("AdminPanel", 3) end
    end
end)

local executeAdmin = function(player, command)
    if not path then return end  -- AdminPanel no disponible
    local player_ui = path:FindFirstChild("Profiles").ScrollingFrame:FindFirstChild(player.Name)
    local command_ui = path:FindFirstChild("Content").ScrollingFrame:FindFirstChild(command)

    if not player_ui then return end
    if not command_ui then return end

    local didRun = false

    for _, v in pairs(path:FindFirstChild("Content").ScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
        if v:FindFirstChild("UIStroke") and v.UIStroke.Color == Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0) then
            firesignal(command_ui.Activated)
            task.wait(0.01)
            firesignal(player_ui.Activated)
            didRun = true
            break
        end
    end

    if not didRun then
        for _, v in pairs(path:FindFirstChild("Profiles").ScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
            if v:FindFirstChild("UIStroke") and v.UIStroke.Color == Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0) then
                firesignal(player_ui.Activated)
                task.wait(0.01)
                firesignal(command_ui.Activated)
                didRun = true
                break
            end
        end
    end

    if not didRun then
        firesignal(player_ui.Activated)
        task.wait(0.01)
        firesignal(command_ui.Activated)
    end
end

local GlobalCooldowns = {}

local function getNearestPlayer(maxDistance)
    local nearestPlayer = nil
    local nearestDistance = maxDistance

    local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
    if not localPlayer.Character or not localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        return nil
    end

    local localRoot = localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart

    for _, otherPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if otherPlayer ~= localPlayer and otherPlayer.Character and otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local otherRoot = otherPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            local distance = (localRoot.Position - otherRoot.Position).Magnitude

            if distance < nearestDistance then
                nearestDistance = distance
                nearestPlayer = otherPlayer
            end
        end
    end

    return nearestPlayer
end

local function isMyPlot(plot)
    local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
    if plotSign then
        local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
        if surfaceGui then
            local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
            if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                local text = textLabel.Text:lower()
                if (LocalPlayer.Name and text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower(), 1, true)) or
                   (LocalPlayer.DisplayName and text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true)) then
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return false
end

local function createPlotTimerBillboard(plot)
    local friendPanel = plot:FindFirstChild("FriendPanel")
    local adornPart = nil
    if friendPanel then adornPart = friendPanel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or friendPanel.PrimaryPart end
    if not adornPart then adornPart = plot:FindFirstChild("MainRoot") end
    if not adornPart then return nil end

    local existingBillboard = adornPart:FindFirstChild("PlotTimerESP")
    if existingBillboard then existingBillboard:Destroy() end

    local isMine = isMyPlot(plot)
    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "PlotTimerESP"
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 250, 0, 50)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true
    billboard.MaxDistance = math.huge
    billboard.Adornee = adornPart
    billboard.Parent = adornPart

    local timerLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    timerLabel.Name = "TimerLabel"
    timerLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    timerLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    timerLabel.TextColor3 = _G.BaseTimerESPColor
    timerLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    timerLabel.TextSize = 28
    timerLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.2
    timerLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    timerLabel.Text = "Loading..."
    timerLabel.Parent = billboard

    return billboard, isMine
end

local function isInsideAnimalPodiums(descendant)
    local parent = descendant.Parent
    while parent and parent ~= Workspace do
        if parent.Name == "AnimalPodiums" then return true end
        parent = parent.Parent
    end
    return false
end

local function updatePlotTimerBillboard(plot, billboard, isMine)
    if not billboard or not billboard.Parent then return false end
    local timerLabel = billboard:FindFirstChild("TimerLabel")
    if not timerLabel then return false end

    local timerFound = false
    for _, descendant in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
        if descendant:IsA("TextLabel") and descendant ~= timerLabel then
            if isInsideAnimalPodiums(descendant) then continue end
            local text = descendant.Text or ""
            if text:match("%d+:%d+") then
                local minutes, seconds = text:match("(%d+):(%d+)")
                local totalSeconds = tonumber(minutes) * 60 + tonumber(seconds)
                if totalSeconds == 0 then
                    timerLabel.Text = "Unlocked"
                    timerLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
                else
                    timerLabel.Text = totalSeconds .. "s"
                    timerLabel.TextColor3 = _G.BaseTimerESPColor
                end
                timerFound = true
                break
            elseif text:match("%d+s") then
                local secs = tonumber(text:match("(%d+)"))
                if secs == 0 then
                    timerLabel.Text = "Unlocked"
                    timerLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
                else
                    timerLabel.Text = text
                    timerLabel.TextColor3 = _G.BaseTimerESPColor
                end
                timerFound = true
                break
            end
        end
    end

    if not timerFound then
        timerLabel.Text = "Unlocked"
        timerLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
    end
    return true
end

local function removePlotTimerESP()
    for plot, billboard in pairs(PlotTimerBillboards) do
        if billboard then pcall(function() billboard:Destroy() end) end
    end
    PlotTimerBillboards = {}
    PlotIsMineLookup = {}
end

local function updatePlotTimerESP()
    if not _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled then return end
    local plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if not plots then return end

    local currentPlots = {}
    for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do
        currentPlots[plot] = true
        if not PlotTimerBillboards[plot] or not PlotTimerBillboards[plot].Parent then
            local bb, isMine = createPlotTimerBillboard(plot)
            PlotTimerBillboards[plot] = bb
            PlotIsMineLookup[plot] = isMine
        end
        if PlotTimerBillboards[plot] then
            updatePlotTimerBillboard(plot, PlotTimerBillboards[plot], PlotIsMineLookup[plot])
        end
    end

    for plot, _ in pairs(PlotTimerBillboards) do
        if not currentPlots[plot] then
            if PlotTimerBillboards[plot] then pcall(function() PlotTimerBillboards[plot]:Destroy() end) end
            PlotTimerBillboards[plot] = nil
            PlotIsMineLookup[plot] = nil
        end
    end
end

local function updateBaseTimerColors()
    for plot, billboard in pairs(PlotTimerBillboards) do
        if billboard and billboard.Parent then
            local timerLabel = billboard:FindFirstChild("TimerLabel")
            if timerLabel and timerLabel.Text ~= "Unlocked" then
                timerLabel.TextColor3 = _G.BaseTimerESPColor
            end
        end
    end
end

_G.toggleBaseTimerESP = function()
    _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled = not _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled
    if not _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled then removePlotTimerESP() end
end
_G.removePlotTimerESP = removePlotTimerESP
_G.updateBaseTimerColors = updateBaseTimerColors

transparentParts = {}

local function applyTransparencyToPlot(plot)
    if not _G.plotTransparencyEnabled or not plot then return end
    task.spawn(function()
        local charRoots = {}
        for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if playerObj.Character then
                charRoots[playerObj.Character] = true
            end
        end

        for _, obj in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                local shouldMakeTransparent = true
                pcall(function()
                    for char in pairs(charRoots) do
                        if obj:IsDescendantOf(char) then
                            shouldMakeTransparent = false
                            return
                        end
                    end
                    local laser = plot:FindFirstChild("Laser")
                    if laser and obj:IsDescendantOf(laser) then shouldMakeTransparent = false return end
                    local parent = obj.Parent
                    if parent and parent:IsA("Model") then
                        if parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") or parent:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            shouldMakeTransparent = false
                            return
                        end
                        local modelName = parent.Name:lower()
                        if modelName:find("brainrot") or modelName:find("dropper") then shouldMakeTransparent = false return end
                    end
                    if obj.Name:lower():find("brainrot") then shouldMakeTransparent = false return end
                end)
                if shouldMakeTransparent then
                    pcall(function()
                        obj.LocalTransparencyModifier = _G.ClearBaseTransparency
                        transparentParts[obj] = true
                    end)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

task.spawn(function()
    task.wait(15)
    while _loopFlags.running do
        task.wait(10)
        local currentTime = tick()
        for obj, timestamp in pairs(_cacheTimestamps) do
            if currentTime - timestamp > _cacheValidity * 3 then
                _espCache.brainrot[obj] = nil
                _espCache.players[obj] = nil
                _espCache.stealers[obj] = nil
                _cacheTimestamps[obj] = nil
            end
        end
        for i = #debrisScanCache, 1, -1 do
            local item = debrisScanCache[i]
            if not item.part or not item.part.Parent then
                table.remove(debrisScanCache, i)
            end
        end
    end
end)

local function isInsidePlot(plot, sizeMod)
    local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp or not plot then return false end
    
    local hitbox = plot:FindFirstChild("StealHitbox") or plot:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
    if not hitbox then return false end
    
    local hSize = hitbox.Size * (sizeMod or 0.977)
    local hPos = hitbox.Position
    local pPos = hrp.Position
    
    return math.abs(pPos.X - hPos.X) <= (hSize.X * 0.5) and 
           math.abs(pPos.Z - hPos.Z) <= (hSize.Z * 0.5)
end

local function removeTransparencyFromPlot(plot)
    if not plot then return end
    task.spawn(function()
        for _, obj in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                pcall(function() obj.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end)
                transparentParts[obj] = nil
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function updateClearBaseTransparency()
    if not _G.plotTransparencyEnabled then return end
    for part in pairs(transparentParts) do
        if part and part.Parent then
            pcall(function() part.LocalTransparencyModifier = _G.ClearBaseTransparency end)
        else
            transparentParts[part] = nil
        end
    end
end

local function applyClearBase()
    if not plotsFolder then plotsFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots") end
    if not plotsFolder then plotsFolder = Workspace:WaitForChild("Plots", 10) if not plotsFolder then return end task.wait(0.1) end
end

_G.toggleClearBase = function() end
_G.applyClearBase = function() end
_G.updateClearBaseTransparency = function() end

local function findMyPlotForBeam()
    local plots = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if not plots then return nil end
    for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do
        local sign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
        if sign then
            local surfaceGui = sign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
            if surfaceGui then
                local label = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                if label then
                    local text = label.Text:lower()
                    if text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower()) or text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower()) then
                        return plot
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function createPlotBeam()
    if not _G.rainbowBeamEnabled then return end
    local myPlot = findMyPlotForBeam()
    if not myPlot or not myPlot.Parent then return end
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character or not character.Parent then return end
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp or not hrp.Parent then return end

    if plotBeam then pcall(function() plotBeam:Destroy() end) end
    if plotBeamAttachment0 then pcall(function() plotBeamAttachment0:Destroy() end) end

    plotBeamAttachment0 = hrp:FindFirstChild("PlotBeamAttach_Player") or Instance.new("Attachment")
    plotBeamAttachment0.Name = "PlotBeamAttach_Player"
    plotBeamAttachment0.Position = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    plotBeamAttachment0.Parent = hrp

    local plotPart = myPlot:FindFirstChild("MainRootPart") or myPlot:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
    if not plotPart or not plotPart.Parent then return end

    plotBeamAttachment1 = plotPart:FindFirstChild("PlotBeamAttach_Plot") or Instance.new("Attachment")
    plotBeamAttachment1.Name = "PlotBeamAttach_Plot"
    plotBeamAttachment1.Position = Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
    plotBeamAttachment1.Parent = plotPart

    plotBeam = hrp:FindFirstChild("PlotBeam") or Instance.new("Beam")
    plotBeam.Name = "PlotBeam"
    plotBeam.Attachment0 = plotBeamAttachment0
    plotBeam.Attachment1 = plotBeamAttachment1
    plotBeam.FaceCamera = true
    plotBeam.LightEmission = 2
    plotBeam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0)
    plotBeam.Width0 = 0.7
    plotBeam.Width1 = 0.7
    plotBeam.TextureMode = Enum.TextureMode.Wrap
    plotBeam.TextureSpeed = 0
    plotBeam.Color = ColorSequence.new(_G.LineToBaseColor)
    plotBeam.Parent = hrp
end

local function resetPlotBeam()
    if plotBeam then pcall(function() plotBeam:Destroy() end) end
    if plotBeamAttachment0 then pcall(function() plotBeamAttachment0:Destroy() end) end
    if plotBeamAttachment1 then pcall(function() plotBeamAttachment1:Destroy() end) end
    plotBeam = nil
    plotBeamAttachment0 = nil
    plotBeamAttachment1 = nil
end

local function updateLineToBaseColor()
    if plotBeam and plotBeam.Parent then
        pcall(function() plotBeam.Color = ColorSequence.new(_G.LineToBaseColor) end)
    end
end

_G.createPlotBeam = createPlotBeam
_G.resetPlotBeam = resetPlotBeam
_G.toggleLineToBase = function()
    _G.rainbowBeamEnabled = not _G.rainbowBeamEnabled
    if not _G.rainbowBeamEnabled then resetPlotBeam() else createPlotBeam() end
end
_G.updateLineToBaseColor = updateLineToBaseColor

local function stripTags(text)
    if typeof(text) ~= "string" then return text end
    return text:gsub("<[^>]+>", ""):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
end

local function resetBrainrotBeam()
    if brainrotBeam then pcall(function() brainrotBeam:Destroy() end) end
    if brainrotAttachment0 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment0:Destroy() end) end
    if brainrotAttachment1 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment1:Destroy() end) end
    brainrotBeam, brainrotAttachment0, brainrotAttachment1, currentBrainrotTarget = nil, nil, nil, nil
end

local cachedHighestBrainrot = nil
local cachedHighestValue = 0
local cachedHighestName = "Unknown"

local function findHighestBrainrot()
    local highestValue, highestBrainrot, highestName = 0, nil, "Unknown"
    local myPlot = nil
    local plotsFolderLocal = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")

    if plotsFolderLocal then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolderLocal:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local text = textLabel.Text:lower()
                        if (LocalPlayer.Name and text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower(), 1, true)) or
                           (LocalPlayer.DisplayName and text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true)) then
                            myPlot = plot
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local plotOwners = {}
    if plotsFolderLocal then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolderLocal:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local plotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local ownerText = textLabel.Text
                        local ownerInGame = false
                        for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.Name:lower(), 1, true) or
                               ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                ownerInGame = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        plotOwners[plot] = { position = plotPos, ownerInGame = ownerInGame, isMyPlot = (plot == myPlot) }
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local debrisFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
    if debrisFolder then
        for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                local closestPlot, closestPlotDist = nil, math.huge
                if plotsFolderLocal then
                    for plot, plotData in pairs(plotOwners) do
                        local dx = obj.Position.X - plotData.position.X
                        local dz = obj.Position.Z - plotData.position.Z
                        local dist = math.sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                        if dist < closestPlotDist then closestPlotDist = dist closestPlot = plot end
                    end
                end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and plotOwners[closestPlot].isMyPlot then continue end
                if closestPlotDist > 300 then continue end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and not plotOwners[closestPlot].ownerInGame then continue end

                local displayNameLabel, generationLabel = nil, nil
                for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                        for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                            if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                if label.Name == "DisplayName" then displayNameLabel = label
                                elseif label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then generationLabel = label end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                if displayNameLabel and generationLabel then
                    local displayName = displayNameLabel.Text or "Unknown"
                    local genText = string.lower(generationLabel.Text or "0")
                    local petValue = parsePetValue(genText)
                    if petValue > highestValue then highestValue = petValue highestBrainrot = obj highestName = displayName end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return highestBrainrot, highestValue, highestName
end

local function updateCachedHighestBrainrot()
    cachedHighestBrainrot, cachedHighestValue, cachedHighestName = findHighestBrainrot()
end

local function getCachedHighestBrainrot()
    return cachedHighestBrainrot, cachedHighestValue, cachedHighestName
end

local function updateBrainrotBeam()
    if not _G.brainrotBeamEnabled then return end
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    local humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not humanoidRootPart then return end

    local targetBrainrot, brainrotValue, itemName

    -- Priority 1: Manually selected steal target
    if _G.SelectedStealTarget and _G.SelectedStealTarget.part and _G.SelectedStealTarget.part.Parent then
        targetBrainrot = _G.SelectedStealTarget.part
        brainrotValue = _G.SelectedStealTarget.value or _G.SelectedStealTarget.genValue or 0
        itemName = _G.SelectedStealTarget.name or "Unknown"
    -- Priority 2: Current auto steal target
    elseif _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget and _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.part and _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.part.Parent then
        targetBrainrot = _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.part
        brainrotValue = _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.genValue or _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.value or 0
        itemName = _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.name or "Unknown"
    -- Priority 3: Current TP target from CurrentStealingItemName
    elseif _G.CurrentStealingItemName and _G.CurrentStealingItemPosition then
        local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
        if debrisFolder then
            local targetName = _G.CurrentStealingItemName:lower()
            for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                    for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                            for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                                if label:IsA("TextLabel") and label.Name == "DisplayName" then
                                    if (label.Text or ""):lower():find(targetName, 1, true) then
                                        targetBrainrot = obj
                                        brainrotValue = _G.CurrentStealingItemValue or 0
                                        itemName = _G.CurrentStealingItemName
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            if targetBrainrot then break end
                        end
                    end
                    if targetBrainrot then break end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    -- Priority 4: Fallback to cached highest brainrot
    if not targetBrainrot or not targetBrainrot.Parent then
        targetBrainrot, brainrotValue, itemName = getCachedHighestBrainrot()
    end

    if not targetBrainrot or not targetBrainrot.Parent or not brainrotValue or brainrotValue < 5000000 then
        resetBrainrotBeam()
        return
    end

    local targetPrimaryPart = targetBrainrot
    if not targetBrainrot:IsA("BasePart") then
        targetPrimaryPart = targetBrainrot:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart") or targetBrainrot.PrimaryPart or targetBrainrot:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
    end
    if not targetPrimaryPart then return end

    if targetBrainrot ~= currentBrainrotTarget then
        if brainrotBeam then pcall(function() brainrotBeam:Destroy() end) end
        if brainrotAttachment0 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment0:Destroy() end) end
        if brainrotAttachment1 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment1:Destroy() end) end
        brainrotBeam, brainrotAttachment0, brainrotAttachment1 = nil, nil, nil
        currentBrainrotTarget = targetBrainrot
    end

    if not brainrotAttachment1 or not brainrotAttachment1.Parent or brainrotAttachment1.Parent ~= targetPrimaryPart then
        if brainrotAttachment1 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment1:Destroy() end) end
        brainrotAttachment1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
        brainrotAttachment1.Name = "BrainrotBeamAttach1"
        brainrotAttachment1.Position = Vector3.new(0, -8, 0)
        brainrotAttachment1.Parent = targetPrimaryPart
    end

    if not brainrotAttachment0 or not brainrotAttachment0.Parent or brainrotAttachment0.Parent ~= humanoidRootPart then
        if brainrotAttachment0 then pcall(function() brainrotAttachment0:Destroy() end) end
        brainrotAttachment0 = Instance.new("Attachment")
        brainrotAttachment0.Name = "BrainrotBeamAttach0"
        brainrotAttachment0.Parent = humanoidRootPart
    end

    if not brainrotBeam or not brainrotBeam.Parent or brainrotBeam.Attachment1 ~= brainrotAttachment1 then
        if brainrotBeam then pcall(function() brainrotBeam:Destroy() end) end
        brainrotBeam = Instance.new("Beam")
        brainrotBeam.Name = "BrainrotBeam"
        brainrotBeam.Attachment0 = brainrotAttachment0
        brainrotBeam.Attachment1 = brainrotAttachment1
        brainrotBeam.Width0 = 0.7
        brainrotBeam.Width1 = 0.7
        brainrotBeam.Color = ColorSequence.new(_G.LineToHighestColor)
        brainrotBeam.FaceCamera = true
        brainrotBeam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.15)
        brainrotBeam.LightEmission = 1
        brainrotBeam.LightInfluence = 0
        brainrotBeam.Segments = 25
        brainrotBeam.Texture = "rbxasset://textures/ui/Glow.png"
        brainrotBeam.TextureLength = 2
        brainrotBeam.TextureSpeed = 1
        brainrotBeam.Parent = humanoidRootPart
    end
end

local function updateLineToHighestColor()
    if brainrotBeam and brainrotBeam.Parent then
        pcall(function() brainrotBeam.Color = ColorSequence.new(_G.LineToHighestColor) end)
    end
end

_G.updateBrainrotBeam = updateBrainrotBeam
_G.resetBrainrotBeam = resetBrainrotBeam
_G.toggleBeamToHighest = function()
    _G.brainrotBeamEnabled = not _G.brainrotBeamEnabled
    if not _G.brainrotBeamEnabled then resetBrainrotBeam() end
end
_G.updateLineToHighestColor = updateLineToHighestColor

local function createMineESPFolder()
    if not mineEspFolder or not mineEspFolder.Parent then
        mineEspFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
        mineEspFolder.Name = "SubspaceMineESP"
        mineEspFolder.Parent = Workspace.CurrentCamera
    end
    return mineEspFolder
end

local function isHeldByPlayer(instance)
    local current = instance.Parent
    while current and current ~= Workspace and current ~= game do
        if current:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then return true end
        if current.Parent and current.Parent:IsA("Player") and current.Name == "Backpack" then return true end
        current = current.Parent
    end
    return false
end

local function getOwnerFromName(mine)
    local name = mine.Name
    if name:sub(1, 16) == "SubspaceTripmine" then return name:sub(17) end
    return name
end

local function getTopLevelMine(instance)
    local current = instance
    local topMine = nil
    while current and current ~= Workspace do
        local name = current.Name:lower()
        if name:find("subspace") or name:find("tripmine") then topMine = current end
        current = current.Parent
    end
    return topMine
end

local function getMinePosition(instance)
    if instance:IsA("Model") then
        local success, cf = pcall(function() return instance:GetBoundingBox() end)
        if success then return cf.Position end
        local part = instance:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
        if part then return part.Position end
    elseif instance:IsA("BasePart") then
        return instance.Position
    end
    return nil
end

-- Mine ESP now uses Highlight instances instead of 12-Part wireframe boxes (massive FPS improvement)

local function addMineESP(mine)
    if trackedMines[mine] then return end
    if isHeldByPlayer(mine) then return end
    local pos = getMinePosition(mine)
    if not pos then return end
    local ownerName = getOwnerFromName(mine)
    local color = _G.MinesESPColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)

    -- Use Highlight instead of 12-Part wireframe (1 instance vs 12, massive FPS save)
    local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
    highlight.Name = "MineHighlight"
    highlight.FillTransparency = 0.7
    highlight.FillColor = color
    highlight.OutlineColor = color
    highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
    highlight.Adornee = mine
    highlight.Parent = createMineESPFolder()

    local adornee = mine:IsA("BasePart") and mine or (mine:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or mine)
    local bb = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    bb.Name = "MineLabelBB"
    bb.Adornee = adornee
    bb.Size = UDim2.new(0, 250, 0, 30)
    bb.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 4, 0)
    bb.AlwaysOnTop = true
    bb.Parent = createMineESPFolder()

    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Name = "MineLabel"
    label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.Text = ownerName .. "'s Subspace Mine"
    label.TextColor3 = color
    label.TextSize = 16
    label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
    label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
    label.Parent = bb

    trackedMines[mine] = { highlight = highlight, billboard = bb }

    local conn
    conn = mine.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
        if not mine.Parent then
            pcall(function() highlight:Destroy() end)
            pcall(function() bb:Destroy() end)
            trackedMines[mine] = nil
            if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
        end
    end)
end

local function removeMineESP(mine)
    local data = trackedMines[mine]
    if not data then return end
    pcall(function() if data.highlight then data.highlight:Destroy() end end)
    pcall(function() if data.billboard then data.billboard:Destroy() end end)
    pcall(function() if data.box then data.box:Destroy() end end)
    pcall(function() if data.label then data.label:Destroy() end end)
    trackedMines[mine] = nil
end

local function updateMinesColors()
    local color = _G.MinesESPColor
    for mine, data in pairs(trackedMines) do
        pcall(function()
            if data.highlight then
                data.highlight.FillColor = color
                data.highlight.OutlineColor = color
            end
            if data.billboard then
                local lbl = data.billboard:FindFirstChild("MineLabel")
                if lbl then lbl.TextColor3 = color end
            end
            if data.box then
                for _, part in ipairs(data.box:GetChildren()) do
                    if part:IsA("Part") then part.Color = color end
                end
            end
            if data.label then
                local bb = data.label:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BillboardGui")
                if bb then local lbl = bb:FindFirstChild("MineLabel") if lbl then lbl.TextColor3 = color end end
            end
        end)
    end
end

local function scanForMines()
    if not _G.MineESPEnabled then return end
    local foldersToScan = {}
    local debrisForMines = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
    if debrisForMines then table.insert(foldersToScan, debrisForMines) end
    local plotsFolderForMines = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
    if plotsFolderForMines then table.insert(foldersToScan, plotsFolderForMines) end

    for _, folder in ipairs(foldersToScan) do
        for _, obj in ipairs(folder:GetDescendants()) do
            local name = obj.Name:lower()
            if (name:find("subspace") or name:find("tripmine")) and not trackedMines[obj] then
                local topMine = getTopLevelMine(obj)
                if topMine and not trackedMines[topMine] then pcall(function() addMineESP(topMine) end) end
            end
        end
    end
    -- Cleanup removed/held mines (Highlight auto-follows position, no manual box updates needed)
    for mine, data in pairs(trackedMines) do
        if not mine or not mine.Parent or isHeldByPlayer(mine) then
            removeMineESP(mine)
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllMineESP()
    for mine, _ in pairs(trackedMines) do removeMineESP(mine) end
    trackedMines = {}
    if mineEspFolder then pcall(function() mineEspFolder:Destroy() end) mineEspFolder = nil end
end

_G.toggleMineESP = function()
    _G.MineESPEnabled = not _G.MineESPEnabled
    if not _G.MineESPEnabled then removeAllMineESP() end
end
_G.removeAllMineESP = removeAllMineESP
_G.updateMinesColors = updateMinesColors

local STEALING_UPDATE_INTERVAL = 3
local MAX_STEAL_DISTANCE = 20

local function findStealingItem(character)
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return nil end
    local playerPos = hrp.Position
    local closestDist = MAX_STEAL_DISTANCE
    local stealingItemName = nil

    pcall(function()
        for _, obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("TextLabel") and obj.Name == "Generation" then
                local itemModel = obj:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
                if itemModel then
                    local itemPos = nil
                    local billboard = obj:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("BillboardGui")
                    if billboard and billboard.Adornee then
                        if billboard.Adornee:IsA("Attachment") then itemPos = billboard.Adornee.WorldPosition
                        elseif billboard.Adornee:IsA("BasePart") then itemPos = billboard.Adornee.Position end
                    end
                    if not itemPos and itemModel.PrimaryPart then itemPos = itemModel.PrimaryPart.Position
                    elseif not itemPos then local part = itemModel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") if part then itemPos = part.Position end end
                    if itemPos then
                        local dist = (itemPos - playerPos).Magnitude
                        if dist < closestDist then closestDist = dist stealingItemName = stripTags(itemModel.Name) end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    return stealingItemName
end

local function createStealingBillboard(character, playerName, itemName)
    for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") and child.Name == "StealingESP" then child:Destroy() end
    end
    local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or character:FindFirstChild("Head")
    if not rootPart then return nil end

    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "StealingESP"
    billboard.Adornee = rootPart
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 350, 0, 100)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 6, 0)  -- HIGHER - 6 studs up
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true

    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    frame.Parent = billboard

    local stealingLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    stealingLabel.Name = "StealingText"
    stealingLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
    stealingLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    stealingLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    stealingLabel.TextColor3 = _G.StealingESPColor
    stealingLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
    stealingLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    stealingLabel.TextSize = 20  -- BIGGER text
    stealingLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack  -- BOLDER font
    stealingLabel.Text = itemName and string.upper('STEALING - "' .. itemName .. '"') or "STEALING"
    stealingLabel.Parent = frame

    if not _G.playerESPEnabled then
        local usernameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        usernameLabel.Name = "UsernameText"
        usernameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
        usernameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 32)
        usernameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        usernameLabel.TextColor3 = _G.StealingESPColor
        usernameLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        usernameLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        usernameLabel.TextSize = 16
        usernameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        usernameLabel.Text = string.upper(playerName)
        usernameLabel.Parent = frame
    end

    billboard.Parent = character
    return billboard
end

local function createStealingHighlight(character)
    pcall(function()
        for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if (child:IsA("Highlight") or child:IsA("SelectionBox")) and
               (child.Name == "StealingESPHighlight" or child.Name == "StealingESPBox") then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)

    local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
    highlight.Name = "StealingESPHighlight"
    highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
    highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
    highlight.OutlineColor = _G.StealingESPColor
    highlight.FillColor = _G.StealingESPColor
    highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
    highlight.Enabled = true

    local success = pcall(function() highlight.Parent = character end)
    if success and highlight.Parent then return highlight end

    highlight:Destroy()
    local box = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
    box.Name = "StealingESPBox"
    box.LineThickness = 0.1
    box.Color3 = _G.StealingESPColor
    box.SurfaceTransparency = 0.7
    box.SurfaceColor3 = _G.StealingESPColor
    box.Adornee = character
    box.Parent = character
    return box
end

local function updateStealingESPColors()
    for userId, espData in pairs(trackedStealersESP) do
        if espData.billboard and espData.billboard.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                local frame = espData.billboard:FindFirstChildOfClass("Frame")
                if frame then for _, child in ipairs(frame:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("TextLabel") then child.TextColor3 = _G.StealingESPColor end end end
            end)
        end
        if espData.highlight and espData.highlight.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                if espData.highlight:IsA("Highlight") then espData.highlight.OutlineColor = _G.StealingESPColor espData.highlight.FillColor = _G.StealingESPColor
                elseif espData.highlight:IsA("SelectionBox") then espData.highlight.Color3 = _G.StealingESPColor espData.highlight.SurfaceColor3 = _G.StealingESPColor end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function addStealingESP(playerObj, itemName)
    if playerObj == LocalPlayer then return end
    local character = playerObj.Character
    if not character then return end
    local billboard = createStealingBillboard(character, playerObj.Name, itemName)
    local highlight = createStealingHighlight(character)
    if billboard and highlight then trackedStealersESP[playerObj.UserId] = { player = playerObj, character = character, billboard = billboard, highlight = highlight, itemName = itemName } end
end

local function removeStealingESP(userId)
    local espData = trackedStealersESP[userId]
    if espData then
        if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
        if espData.highlight then pcall(function() espData.highlight:Destroy() end) end
        trackedStealersESP[userId] = nil
    end
end

local function updateStealingESP()
    if not _G.stealingESPEnabled then return end
    local currentTime = tick()
    for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if playerObj ~= LocalPlayer and playerObj.Character then
            local character = playerObj.Character
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            local isStealing = playerObj:GetAttribute("Stealing")
            if isStealing and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local existingESP = _espCache.stealers[playerObj.UserId]
                if not existingESP or 
                   currentTime - (_cacheTimestamps[playerObj.UserId] or 0) > _cacheValidity then
                    local itemName = findStealingItem(character)
                    if existingESP then 
                        removeStealingESP(playerObj.UserId) 
                    end
                    addStealingESP(playerObj, itemName)
                    _cacheTimestamps[playerObj.UserId] = currentTime
                end
            else
                if _espCache.stealers[playerObj.UserId] then 
                    removeStealingESP(playerObj.UserId) 
                    _cacheTimestamps[playerObj.UserId] = nil
                end
            end
        end
    end
    for userId, espData in pairs(_espCache.stealers) do
        local playerObj = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(userId)
        if not playerObj or not playerObj.Parent or not playerObj.Character or not playerObj.Character.Parent then 
            removeStealingESP(userId)
            _cacheTimestamps[userId] = nil
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllStealingESP()
    for userId, _ in pairs(trackedStealersESP) do removeStealingESP(userId) end
    trackedStealersESP = {}
    _G.trackedStealersESP = {}
end

_G.updateStealingESP = updateStealingESP
_G.removeAllStealingESP = removeAllStealingESP
_G.toggleStealingESP = function()
    _G.stealingESPEnabled = not _G.stealingESPEnabled
    if not _G.stealingESPEnabled then removeAllStealingESP() end
end
_G.updateStealingESPColors = updateStealingESPColors
