local function addStealingChams(playerObj)
    if playerObj == LocalPlayer then return end
    local character = playerObj.Character
    if not character then return end
    local highlight = createStealingChamsHighlight(character)
    if highlight then trackedStealersChams[playerObj.UserId] = { player = playerObj, character = character, highlight = highlight } end
end

local function removeStealingChams(userId)
    local chamsData = trackedStealersChams[userId]
    if chamsData then
        if chamsData.highlight then pcall(function() chamsData.highlight:Destroy() end) end
        trackedStealersChams[userId] = nil
    end
end

local function updateStealingChams()
    if not _G.stealingChamsEnabled then return end
    for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if playerObj ~= LocalPlayer and playerObj.Character then
            local character = playerObj.Character
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            local isStealing = playerObj:GetAttribute("Stealing")
            if isStealing and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local existingChams = trackedStealersChams[playerObj.UserId]
                if not existingChams then addStealingChams(playerObj)
                elseif not existingChams.highlight or not existingChams.highlight.Parent then removeStealingChams(playerObj.UserId) addStealingChams(playerObj) end
            else
                if trackedStealersChams[playerObj.UserId] then removeStealingChams(playerObj.UserId) end
            end
        end
    end
    for userId, chamsData in pairs(trackedStealersChams) do
        local playerObj = chamsData.player
        if not playerObj or not playerObj.Parent or not playerObj.Character or not playerObj.Character.Parent then removeStealingChams(userId) end
    end
end

local function removeAllStealingChams()
    for userId, _ in pairs(trackedStealersChams) do removeStealingChams(userId) end
    trackedStealersChams = {}
    _G.trackedStealersChams = {}
end

_G.updateStealingChams = updateStealingChams
_G.removeAllStealingChams = removeAllStealingChams
_G.toggleStealingChams = function()
    _G.stealingChamsEnabled = not _G.stealingChamsEnabled
    if not _G.stealingChamsEnabled then removeAllStealingChams() end
end
_G.updateStealingChamsColors = updateStealingChamsColors

local PLAYER_ESP_UPDATE_INTERVAL = 3

local function createPlayerBillboard(character, playerName)
    for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") and child.Name == "PlayerESP" then child:Destroy() end
    end
    local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or character:FindFirstChild("Head")
    if not rootPart then return nil end

    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "PlayerESP"
    billboard.Adornee = rootPart
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true

    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    frame.Parent = billboard

    local nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    nameLabel.TextColor3 = _G.PlayerESPColor
    nameLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
    nameLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    nameLabel.TextSize = 15
    nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    nameLabel.Text = string.upper(playerName)
    nameLabel.Parent = frame

    billboard.Parent = character
    return billboard
end

local function createPlayerHighlight(character)
    pcall(function()
        for _, child in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if (child:IsA("Highlight") or child:IsA("SelectionBox")) and
               (child.Name == "PlayerESPHighlight" or child.Name == "PlayerESPBox") then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)

    local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
    highlight.Name = "PlayerESPHighlight"
    highlight.FillTransparency = 1
    highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
    highlight.OutlineColor = _G.PlayerESPColor
    highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
    highlight.Enabled = true

    local success = pcall(function() highlight.Parent = character end)
    if success and highlight.Parent then return highlight end

    highlight:Destroy()
    local box = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
    box.Name = "PlayerESPBox"
    box.LineThickness = 0.05
    box.Color3 = _G.PlayerESPColor
    box.SurfaceTransparency = 1
    box.Adornee = character
    box.Parent = character
    return box
end

local function addPlayerESP(playerObj)
    if playerObj == LocalPlayer then return end
    local character = playerObj.Character
    if not character then return end
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local billboard = createPlayerBillboard(character, playerObj.Name)
    local highlight = createPlayerHighlight(character)

    if billboard and highlight then
        trackedPlayers[playerObj.UserId] = { player = playerObj, character = character, billboard = billboard, highlight = highlight }
    end
end

local function removePlayerESP(userId)
    local espData = trackedPlayers[userId]
    if espData then
        if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
        if espData.highlight then pcall(function() espData.highlight:Destroy() end) end
        trackedPlayers[userId] = nil
    end
end

local function updatePlayerESPColors()
    for userId, espData in pairs(trackedPlayers) do
        if espData.billboard and espData.billboard.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                local frame = espData.billboard:FindFirstChildOfClass("Frame")
                if frame then
                    for _, child in ipairs(frame:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("TextLabel") then child.TextColor3 = _G.PlayerESPColor end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        if espData.highlight and espData.highlight.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                if espData.highlight:IsA("Highlight") then espData.highlight.OutlineColor = _G.PlayerESPColor
                elseif espData.highlight:IsA("SelectionBox") then espData.highlight.Color3 = _G.PlayerESPColor end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function updatePlayerESP()
    if not _G.playerESPEnabled then return end
    local currentTime = tick()
    for userId, espData in pairs(_espCache.players) do
        local playerObj = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(userId)
        local character = espData.character
        if not playerObj or not playerObj.Parent or not character or not character.Parent then
            removePlayerESP(userId)
            _cacheTimestamps[userId] = nil
        elseif playerObj.Character ~= character or 
               currentTime - (_cacheTimestamps[userId] or 0) > _cacheValidity then
            removePlayerESP(userId)
            addPlayerESP(playerObj)
            _cacheTimestamps[userId] = currentTime
        elseif not espData.billboard or not espData.billboard.Parent or not espData.highlight or not espData.highlight.Parent then
            removePlayerESP(userId)
            addPlayerESP(playerObj)
            _cacheTimestamps[userId] = currentTime
        end
    end
    for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if playerObj ~= LocalPlayer and not _espCache.players[playerObj.UserId] and playerObj.Character then
            pcall(function() addPlayerESP(playerObj) end)
            _cacheTimestamps[playerObj.UserId] = currentTime
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllPlayerESP()
    for userId, _ in pairs(trackedPlayers) do removePlayerESP(userId) end
    trackedPlayers = {}
    _G.trackedPlayers = {}
end

_G.updatePlayerESP = updatePlayerESP
_G.removeAllPlayerESP = removeAllPlayerESP
_G.togglePlayerESP = function()
    _G.playerESPEnabled = not _G.playerESPEnabled
    if not _G.playerESPEnabled then removeAllPlayerESP() end
end
_G.updatePlayerESPColors = updatePlayerESPColors

-- ============================================================
-- CLICK-TO-ADMIN: Click on ESP-highlighted players to admin them
-- ============================================================
if _G.clickToAdminEnabled == nil then _G.clickToAdminEnabled = false end

local clickToAdminConnection = nil
local clickToAdminCooldown = 0

local function getPlayerFromMouse()
    local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
    if not camera then return nil end

    local mouse = LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
    if not mouse then return nil end

    local unitRay = camera:ScreenPointToRay(mouse.X, mouse.Y)
    local rayParams = RaycastParams.new()
    rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Blacklist
    local localChar = LocalPlayer.Character
    rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = localChar and {localChar} or {}

    local result = workspace:Raycast(unitRay.Origin, unitRay.Direction * 5000, rayParams)
    if result and result.Instance then
        local hitPart = result.Instance
        local model = hitPart:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
        while model do
            local player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(model)
            if player and player ~= LocalPlayer then
                return player
            end
            model = model:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
        end
    end

    -- Fallback: find nearest player to click position in screen space
    local mousePos = Vector2.new(mouse.X, mouse.Y)
    local bestPlayer = nil
    local bestDist = 80 -- max pixel distance to count as a "click on player"

    for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if playerObj ~= LocalPlayer and playerObj.Character then
            local hrp = playerObj.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or playerObj.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if hrp then
                local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(hrp.Position)
                if onScreen then
                    local dist = (Vector2.new(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y) - mousePos).Magnitude
                    if dist < bestDist then
                        bestDist = dist
                        bestPlayer = playerObj
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    return bestPlayer
end

local function showClickAdminMenu(targetPlayer)
    if not targetPlayer then return end

    -- Remove old menu if exists
    pcall(function()
        local cg = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")) or game:GetService("CoreGui")
        local old = cg:FindFirstChild("ClickAdminMenu")
        if old then old:Destroy() end
    end)

    local mouse = LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
    local menuX = mouse.X
    local menuY = mouse.Y

    local menuGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    menuGui.Name = "ClickAdminMenu"
    menuGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
    menuGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    pcall(function()
        menuGui.Parent = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")) or game:GetService("CoreGui")
    end)

    -- Background dismiss button
    local dismissBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", menuGui)
    dismissBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    dismissBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    dismissBtn.Text = ""
    dismissBtn.ZIndex = 1
    dismissBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        menuGui:Destroy()
    end)

    local menuWidth = isMobile and 160 or 200
    local buttonHeight = isMobile and 26 or 30
    local commands = {
        {label = "Admin All", cmd = "all"},
        {label = "Ragdoll", cmd = "ragdoll"},
        {label = "Rocket", cmd = "rocket"},
        {label = "Jail", cmd = "jail"},
        {label = "Balloon", cmd = "balloon"},
        {label = "Inverse", cmd = "inverse"},
        {label = "Tiny", cmd = "tiny"},
        {label = "Morph", cmd = "morph"},
    }
    local menuHeight = (#commands * (buttonHeight + 3)) + 40

    -- Clamp position to screen
    local screenSize = menuGui.AbsoluteSize
    if menuX + menuWidth > screenSize.X then menuX = screenSize.X - menuWidth - 10 end
    if menuY + menuHeight > screenSize.Y then menuY = screenSize.Y - menuHeight - 10 end

    local menuFrame = Instance.new("Frame", menuGui)
    menuFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, menuWidth, 0, menuHeight)
    menuFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, menuX, 0, menuY)
    menuFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 14, 16)
    menuFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.05
    menuFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    menuFrame.ZIndex = 10
    Instance.new("UICorner", menuFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

    local uiStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", menuFrame)
    uiStroke.Color = _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    uiStroke.Thickness = 1
    uiStroke.Transparency = 0.5

    -- Header with player name
    local header = Instance.new("TextLabel", menuFrame)
    header.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 30)
    header.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 5)
    header.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    header.Text = targetPlayer.Name
    header.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    header.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
    header.TextColor3 = _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    header.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    header.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
    header.ZIndex = 11

    for i, cmd in ipairs(commands) do
        local btn = Instance.new("TextButton", menuFrame)
        btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, buttonHeight)
        btn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 33 + ((i - 1) * (buttonHeight + 3)))
        btn.BackgroundColor3 = cmd.cmd == "all" and Color3.fromRGB(40, 25, 30) or Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
        btn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
        btn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        btn.Text = cmd.label
        btn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        btn.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
        btn.TextColor3 = cmd.cmd == "all" and Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 110) or Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 215)
        btn.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        btn.ZIndex = 11
        Instance.new("UICorner", btn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local btnPadding = Instance.new("UIPadding", btn)
        btnPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 8)

        btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.05}):Play()
        end)
        btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.3}):Play()
        end)

        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            task.spawn(function()
                if cmd.cmd == "all" then
                    local adminCommands = {"ragdoll", "rocket", "jail", "balloon", "inverse", "tiny", "morph"}
                    for _, c in ipairs(adminCommands) do
                        task.spawn(function()
                            if _G.setCommandCooldown then _G.setCommandCooldown(c) end
                            executeAdmin(targetPlayer, c)
                            print(c, targetPlayer.Name)
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.15)
                    end
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                            Title = "Click Admin",
                            Text = "Admin All on \"" .. targetPlayer.Name .. "\"",
                            Duration = 3
                        })
                    end)
                elseif cmd.cmd == "kick" then
                    pcall(function()
                        local adminR = _REMOTES.adminRemote
                        local adminK = _REMOTES.adminKey
                        if adminR and adminK then
                            adminR:FireServer(adminK, targetPlayer, "kick")
                        end
                    end)
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                            Title = "Click Admin",
                            Text = "Kicked \"" .. targetPlayer.Name .. "\"",
                            Duration = 3
                        })
                    end)
                else
                    if _G.setCommandCooldown then _G.setCommandCooldown(cmd.cmd) end
                    executeAdmin(targetPlayer, cmd.cmd)
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                            Title = "Click Admin",
                            Text = cmd.cmd .. " on \"" .. targetPlayer.Name .. "\"",
                            Duration = 2
                        })
                    end)
                end
            end)
            menuGui:Destroy()
        end)
    end

    -- Auto-close after 8 seconds
    task.delay(8, function()
        if menuGui and menuGui.Parent then
            menuGui:Destroy()
        end
    end)
end

local function startClickToAdmin()
    if clickToAdminConnection then return end

    clickToAdminConnection = _track(UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        if not _G.clickToAdminEnabled then return end
        if not _G.playerESPEnabled then return end -- only works when ESP is on

        local isClick = input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
        local isTap = input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch

        if not isClick and not isTap then return end

        -- Cooldown to prevent spam
        if tick() - clickToAdminCooldown < 0.5 then return end
        clickToAdminCooldown = tick()

        -- Check if clicking on a UI element (ignore if so)
        pcall(function()
            local cg = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")) or game:GetService("CoreGui")
            local guis = LocalPlayer:GetGuiObjectsAtPosition(input.Position.X, input.Position.Y)
            for _, gui in ipairs(guis) do
                -- If clicking on any GUI that isn't the click admin menu itself, skip
                if gui:IsDescendantOf(cg) or gui:IsDescendantOf(LocalPlayer.PlayerGui) then
                    local screenGui = gui:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("ScreenGui")
                    if screenGui and screenGui.Name ~= "ClickAdminMenu" then
                        return
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        local targetPlayer = getPlayerFromMouse()
        if targetPlayer then
            showClickAdminMenu(targetPlayer)
        end
    end))
end

local function stopClickToAdmin()
    if clickToAdminConnection then
        pcall(function() clickToAdminConnection:Disconnect() end)
        clickToAdminConnection = nil
    end
    pcall(function()
        local cg = cloneref and cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")) or game:GetService("CoreGui")
        local old = cg:FindFirstChild("ClickAdminMenu")
        if old then old:Destroy() end
    end)
end

_G.toggleClickToAdmin = function()
    _G.clickToAdminEnabled = not _G.clickToAdminEnabled
    if _G.clickToAdminEnabled then
        startClickToAdmin()
    else
        stopClickToAdmin()
    end
    return _G.clickToAdminEnabled
end

if _G.clickToAdminEnabled then
    task.spawn(startClickToAdmin)
end

local BRAINROT_UPDATE_INTERVAL = 0.5

local function formatValueShort(value)
    if value >= 1e12 then return string.format("%.1ft/s", value / 1e12)
    elseif value >= 1e9 then return string.format("%.1fb/s", value / 1e9)
    elseif value >= 1e6 then return string.format("%.0fm/s", value / 1e6)
    elseif value >= 1e3 then return string.format("%.0fk/s", value / 1e3)
    else return string.format("%.0f/s", value) end
end

local function findAllBrainrots()
    local allDetectedItems = {}
    local myPlot = nil
    local plotsFolderLocal = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")

    if plotsFolderLocal then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolderLocal:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local text = textLabel.Text:lower()
                        if (LocalPlayer.Name and text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower(), 1, true)) or
                           (LocalPlayer.DisplayName and text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true)) then
                            myPlot = plot
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local plotOwners = {}
    if plotsFolderLocal then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolderLocal:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local plotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local ownerText = textLabel.Text
                        local ownerInGame = false
                        for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.Name:lower(), 1, true) or
                               ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                ownerInGame = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        plotOwners[plot] = { position = plotPos, ownerInGame = ownerInGame, isMyPlot = (plot == myPlot) }
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local debrisFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
    if debrisFolder then
        for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                local closestPlot, closestPlotDist = nil, math.huge
                if plotsFolderLocal then
                    for plot, plotData in pairs(plotOwners) do
                        local dx = obj.Position.X - plotData.position.X
                        local dz = obj.Position.Z - plotData.position.Z
                        local dist = math.sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                        if dist < closestPlotDist then closestPlotDist = dist closestPlot = plot end
                    end
                end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and plotOwners[closestPlot].isMyPlot then continue end
                if closestPlotDist > 300 then continue end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and not plotOwners[closestPlot].ownerInGame then continue end

                local displayNameLabel, generationLabel = nil, nil
                for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                        for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                            if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                if label.Name == "DisplayName" then displayNameLabel = label
                                elseif label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then generationLabel = label end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                if displayNameLabel and generationLabel then
                    local displayName = displayNameLabel.Text or "Unknown"
                    local genText = string.lower(generationLabel.Text or "0")
                    local petValue = parsePetValue(genText)

                    if petValue >= 5000000 then
                        table.insert(allDetectedItems, { brainrot = obj, value = petValue, name = displayName })
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    table.sort(allDetectedItems, function(a, b) return a.value > b.value end)

    local maxItems = _G.MaxBrainrotESPItems or 15
    if #allDetectedItems > maxItems then
        local limitedItems = {}
        for i = 1, maxItems do
            limitedItems[i] = allDetectedItems[i]
        end
        return limitedItems
    end

    return allDetectedItems
end

local function createBrainrotBillboard(brainrot, value, itemName)
    local primaryPart = brainrot
    if not brainrot:IsA("BasePart") then
        primaryPart = brainrot.PrimaryPart or brainrot:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
    end
    if not primaryPart then return nil end

    for _, child in ipairs(primaryPart:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") and child.Name == "BrainrotESP" then child:Destroy() end
    end

    local lowerItemName = (itemName or ""):lower()
    local isRedItem = lowerItemName:find("hydra dragon cannelloni", 1, true) or
        lowerItemName:find("dragon cannelloni", 1, true) or lowerItemName:find("meowl", 1, true) or
        lowerItemName:find("skibidi toilet", 1, true) or lowerItemName:find("strawberry elephant", 1, true) or
        lowerItemName:find("capitano moby", 1, true) or lowerItemName:find("la supreme combinasion", 1, true) or
        lowerItemName:find("dragon gingerini", 1, true) or lowerItemName:find("cerberus", 1, true) or
        lowerItemName:find("headless horseman", 1, true)

    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "BrainrotESP"
    billboard.Adornee = primaryPart
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 72)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, -8, 0)
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true

    local nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 44)
    nameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    nameLabel.TextColor3 = isRedItem and Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0) or (_G.BrainrotESPColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0))
    nameLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.3
    nameLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    nameLabel.TextSize = 18
    nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    nameLabel.TextWrapped = true
    nameLabel.RichText = true
    nameLabel.Text = stripTags(itemName) or "Unknown"
    nameLabel.Parent = billboard

    local valueLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    valueLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28)
    valueLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 40)
    valueLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    valueLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
    valueLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.3
    valueLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    valueLabel.TextSize = 16
    valueLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    valueLabel.Text = "$" .. formatValueShort(value)
    valueLabel.Parent = billboard

    billboard.Parent = primaryPart
    return billboard
end

local function updateBrainrotESPColors()
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedBrainrotESP) do
        if espData.billboard and espData.billboard.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                for _, child in ipairs(espData.billboard:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("TextLabel") and child.Position == UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0) then
                        -- Only update name label color if not a red (priority) item
                        if child.TextColor3 ~= Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0) then
                            child.TextColor3 = _G.BrainrotESPColor
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function updateBrainrotESP()
    if not _G.brainrotESPEnabled then return end
    local currentTime = tick()
    local allDetectedItems = findAllBrainrots()
    local validItems = {}
    for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do
        validItems[item.brainrot] = item
        if not _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot] or 
           currentTime - (_cacheTimestamps[item.brainrot] or 0) > _cacheValidity then
            if _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot] and 
               _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot].billboard and 
               _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot].billboard.Parent then
                _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot].billboard:Destroy()
            end
            local billboard = createBrainrotBillboard(item.brainrot, item.value, item.name)
            if billboard then 
                _espCache.brainrot[item.brainrot] = { 
                    billboard = billboard, 
                    value = item.value, 
                    name = item.name 
                }
                _cacheTimestamps[item.brainrot] = currentTime
            end
        end
    end
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(_espCache.brainrot) do
        if not validItems[brainrot] then
            if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
            _espCache.brainrot[brainrot] = nil
            _cacheTimestamps[brainrot] = nil
        elseif espData.billboard and not espData.billboard.Parent then
            local item = validItems[brainrot]
            espData.billboard = createBrainrotBillboard(brainrot, item.value, item.name)
            _cacheTimestamps[brainrot] = currentTime
        end
    end
end


local function removeAllBrainrotESP()
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedBrainrotESP) do
        if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
    end
    trackedBrainrotESP = {}
    _G.trackedBrainrotESP = {}
end

_G.updateBrainrotESP = updateBrainrotESP
_G.removeAllBrainrotESP = removeAllBrainrotESP
_G.toggleBrainrotESP = function()
    _G.brainrotESPEnabled = not _G.brainrotESPEnabled
    if not _G.brainrotESPEnabled then removeAllBrainrotESP() end
end
_G.updateBrainrotESPColors = updateBrainrotESPColors

    return "normal"

local rainbowHue = 0
local yinyangToggle = false

TeleportBack = function()
    if CurrentRoot == nil then
        return
    end

    local character = player.Character
    if not character then
        return
    end

    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    local backpack = player:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")
    if not humanoid or not backpack then
        return
    end

    local toolName = _G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet"

    local carpet = character:FindFirstChild(toolName)
    if not carpet then
        carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName)
    end

    if carpet and carpet:IsA("Tool") and carpet.Parent == backpack then
        humanoid:EquipTool(carpet)
    end

    local itemHeight = CurrentRoot.Position.Y
    local PlayerHeight = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").Position.Y

    local isFirstFloor = (itemHeight <= 6.11)
    local isSecondFloor = (itemHeight >= 11 and itemHeight <= 23.15)
    local isThirdFloor = (itemHeight > 23.15)

    local isPlayerFirstFloor = (PlayerHeight <= 6.11)
    local isPlayerSecondFloor = (PlayerHeight >= 11 and PlayerHeight <= 25)
    local isPlayerThirdFloor = (PlayerHeight > 25)


    --character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame = CFrame.new(CurrentRoot.CFrame.X, character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame.Y, CurrentRoot.CFrame.Z)

    if isFirstFloor and isPlayerFirstFloor or isSecondFloor and isPlayerSecondFloor or isThirdFloor and isPlayerThirdFloor then
        character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame = CFrame.new(CurrentRoot.CFrame.X, character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame.Y, CurrentRoot.CFrame.Z)
    elseif isSecondFloor and isPlayerFirstFloor or isThirdFloor and isPlayerSecondFloor then
        character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame = CFrame.new(CurrentRoot.CFrame.X, character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame.Y, CurrentRoot.CFrame.Z)
        pcall(_G.enableFloat)
    end
end


local function getMutationColor(mutation)
    local mutLower = mutation:lower()

    if mutLower == "rainbow" then
        rainbowHue = (rainbowHue + 0.02) % 1
        return Color3.fromHSV(rainbowHue, 1, 1)
    end

    if mutLower == "yin-yang" or mutLower == "yinyang" then
        yinyangToggle = not yinyangToggle
        if yinyangToggle then
            return Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) -- White
        else
            return Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30) -- Near black
        end
    end

    return mutationColorsForChams[mutLower] or mutationColorsForChams["normal"]
end

local chams_priorityItems = {
    "strawberry elephant", "headless horseman", "meowl", "skibidi toilet",
    "hydra dragon cannelloni", "dragon gingerini", "la supreme combinasion",
    "dragon cannelloni", "cerberus", "capitano moby", "la casa boo",
    "cooki and milki", "burguro and fryuro", "ketupat bros", "reinito sleighito",
    "ginger gerat", "spooky and pumpky", "fragrama and chocrama",
    "festive 67", "garama and madundung"
}

local function getChamsColor(value, isPriority)
    if isPriority or value >= 1000000000 then -- 1B+ or priority
        return Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0) -- Red
    else
        return _G.BrainrotChamsColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) -- Custom color or white
    end
end

local function createBrainrotHighlight(brainrot, isPriority, value)
    pcall(function()
        for _, child in ipairs(brainrot:GetChildren()) do
            if (child:IsA("Highlight") or child:IsA("SelectionBox")) and
               (child.Name == "BrainrotChamsHighlight" or child.Name == "BrainrotChamsBox") then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)

    local outlineColor = getChamsColor(value, isPriority)

    local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
    highlight.Name = "BrainrotChamsHighlight"
    highlight.FillTransparency = 1  -- No fill, outline only
    highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0  -- Solid outline
    highlight.OutlineColor = outlineColor
    highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
    highlight.Enabled = true

    local highlightSuccess = pcall(function()
        if brainrot:IsA("BasePart") then
            highlight.Parent = brainrot
        elseif brainrot:IsA("Model") then
            highlight.Parent = brainrot
        end
    end)

    if not highlightSuccess or not highlight.Parent then
        pcall(function() highlight:Destroy() end)

        local box = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
        box.Name = "BrainrotChamsBox"
        box.LineThickness = 0.05
        box.Color3 = outlineColor
        box.SurfaceTransparency = 1  -- No fill, outline only

        if brainrot:IsA("BasePart") then
            box.Adornee = brainrot
            box.Parent = brainrot
        elseif brainrot:IsA("Model") then
            box.Adornee = brainrot
            box.Parent = brainrot
        end

        return box
    end

    return highlight
end

local function scanBrainrotsForChams()
    local allDetectedItems = {}

    local myPlot = nil
    local plotsFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")

    if plotsFolder then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local text = textLabel.Text:lower()
                        if (LocalPlayer.Name and text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower(), 1, true)) or
                           (LocalPlayer.DisplayName and text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true)) then
                            myPlot = plot
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local plotOwners = {}
    if plotsFolder then
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
            local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
            if plotSign then
                local plotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                    if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                        local ownerText = textLabel.Text
                        local ownerInGame = false
                        for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.Name:lower(), 1, true) or
                               ownerText:lower():find(playerObj.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                ownerInGame = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        plotOwners[plot] = {
                            position = plotPos,
                            ownerInGame = ownerInGame,
                            isMyPlot = (plot == myPlot)
                        }
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local debrisFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
    if debrisFolder then
        for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                local closestPlot = nil
                local closestPlotDist = math.huge
                if plotsFolder then
                    for plot, plotData in pairs(plotOwners) do
                        local dx = obj.Position.X - plotData.position.X
                        local dz = obj.Position.Z - plotData.position.Z
                        local dist = math.sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                        if dist < closestPlotDist then
                            closestPlotDist = dist
                            closestPlot = plot
                        end
                    end
                end

                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and plotOwners[closestPlot].isMyPlot then
                    continue
                end

                if closestPlotDist > 300 then
                    continue
                end

                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and not plotOwners[closestPlot].ownerInGame then
                    continue
                end

                local displayNameLabel = nil
                local generationLabel = nil

                for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                        for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                            if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                if label.Name == "DisplayName" then
                                    displayNameLabel = label
                                elseif label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then
                                    generationLabel = label
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                if displayNameLabel and generationLabel then
                    local displayName = displayNameLabel.Text or "Unknown"
                    local genText = string.lower(generationLabel.Text or "0")

                    local petValue = parsePetValue(genText)

                    local isPriority = false
                    local lowerName = displayName:lower()

                    for _, priorityItemName in ipairs(chams_priorityItems) do
                        if lowerName:find(priorityItemName, 1, true) then
                            isPriority = true
                            break
                        end
                    end

                    table.insert(allDetectedItems, {
                        brainrot = obj,
                        value = petValue,
                        name = displayName,
                        isPriority = isPriority
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end

    return allDetectedItems
end

local function updateBrainrotChams()
    if not _G.brainrotChamsEnabled then return end

    local allDetectedItems = scanBrainrotsForChams()

    for brainrot, chamsData in pairs(trackedBrainrotChams) do
        local stillValid = false

        for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do
            if item.brainrot == brainrot then
                stillValid = true
                break
            end
        end

        if not stillValid then
            if chamsData.highlight then
                pcall(function() chamsData.highlight:Destroy() end)
            end
            trackedBrainrotChams[brainrot] = nil
        end
    end

    for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do
        if not trackedBrainrotChams[item.brainrot] then
            local highlight = createBrainrotHighlight(item.brainrot, item.isPriority or false, item.value)

            if highlight then
                trackedBrainrotChams[item.brainrot] = {
                    highlight = highlight,
                    value = item.value,
                    name = item.name,
                    isPriority = item.isPriority or false
                }
            end
        end
    end
end

local function updateBrainrotChamsColors()
    for brainrot, chamsData in pairs(trackedBrainrotChams) do
        if chamsData.highlight and chamsData.highlight.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                local color = getChamsColor(chamsData.value or 0, chamsData.isPriority or false)
                if chamsData.highlight:IsA("Highlight") then
                    chamsData.highlight.OutlineColor = color
                elseif chamsData.highlight:IsA("SelectionBox") then
                    chamsData.highlight.Color3 = color
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllBrainrotChams()
    for brainrot, chamsData in pairs(trackedBrainrotChams) do
        if chamsData.highlight then
            pcall(function() chamsData.highlight:Destroy() end)
        end
        trackedBrainrotChams[brainrot] = nil
    end
end

_G.updateBrainrotChams = updateBrainrotChams
_G.removeAllBrainrotChams = removeAllBrainrotChams
_G.scanBrainrotsForChams = scanBrainrotsForChams
_G.createBrainrotHighlight = createBrainrotHighlight
_G.toggleBrainrotChams = function()
    _G.brainrotChamsEnabled = not _G.brainrotChamsEnabled
    if _G.brainrotChamsEnabled then
        updateBrainrotChams()
    else
        removeAllBrainrotChams()
    end
end
_G.updateBrainrotChamsColors = updateBrainrotChamsColors

        ["FFlagDisableGPUThrottle"] = "True",
        ["FFlagEnableMicroProfiler"] = "False",
        ["FFlagEnableDebugStats"] = "False"

    local setFFlag = setfflag or SetFastFlag or setfastflag or SetFFlag
    if setFFlag then
        for flag, value in pairs(fflags) do
            pcall(function()
                setFFlag(flag, value)
            end)
        end
    end

    pcall(function() rconsoleclose() end)
    pcall(function() clearconsole() end)
    pcall(function() game:GetService("LogService"):ClearOutput() end)

    local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
    local players = game:GetService("Players")
    local terrain = workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain")

    local processedModels = {}

    local function applyLighting()
        pcall(function()
            lighting.GlobalShadows = false
            lighting.FogEnd = 9e9
            lighting.Brightness = 3
            lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.ShadowSoftness = 0
            lighting.ClockTime = 0
            lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0
            lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 0
            lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        end)
    end

    local function stopAnimations(model)
        if not model or processedModels[model] then return end
        processedModels[model] = true
        for _, v in pairs(model:GetDescendants()) do
            pcall(function()
                if v:IsA("Animator") then
                    for _, track in pairs(v:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                        track:Stop()
                        track:Destroy()
                    end
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("Animation") or v:IsA("AnimationController") then
                    v:Destroy()
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local function stripCharacter(character)
        if not character then return end
        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            pcall(function()
                if v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("ShirtGraphic") or v:IsA("Accessory") then
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("Decal") and v.Name == "face" then
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                    v.TextureID = ""
                elseif v:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                    v.TextureId = ""
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local function cleanObject(v)
        if protectedBeamNames[v.Name] then return end
        if v:IsA("Beam") and v.Parent and v.Parent.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then return end
        if v:IsA("Attachment") and v.Parent and v.Parent.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then return end

        pcall(function()
            if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or v:IsA("Trail") or v:IsA("Smoke") or v:IsA("Fire") or v:IsA("Sparkles") then
                v.Enabled = false
            elseif v:IsA("Beam") then
                v.Enabled = false
            elseif v:IsA("Decal") or v:IsA("Texture") then
                v:Destroy()
            elseif v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                v.Reflectance = 0
                v.TextureID = ""
            elseif v:IsA("Part") or v:IsA("BasePart") then
                v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                v.Reflectance = 0
            elseif v:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                v.TextureId = ""
            elseif v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("ShirtGraphic") then
                v:Destroy()
            end
        end)
    end

    for _, child in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Atmosphere") or child:IsA("Clouds") or child:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or child:IsA("BlurEffect") or child:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or child:IsA("BloomEffect") or child:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
            pcall(function() child:Destroy() end)
        end
    end

    applyLighting()

    lighting.Changed:Connect(applyLighting)

    task.spawn(function()
        while _G.FPSBoostEnabled and task.wait(1) do
            applyLighting()
        end
    end)

    if terrain then
        pcall(function()
            terrain.WaterWaveSize = 0
            terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
            terrain.WaterReflectance = 0
            terrain.WaterTransparency = 0
            terrain.Decoration = false
        end)
    end

    pcall(function() settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 1 end)
    pcall(function() sethiddenproperty(lighting, "Technology", 2) end)

    -- Batched processing: yield every 200 objects to prevent massive frame drop on load-in
    task.spawn(function()
        local descendants = workspace:GetDescendants()
        local BATCH_SIZE = 200
        for i = 1, #descendants, BATCH_SIZE do
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then break end
            local batchEnd = math.min(i + BATCH_SIZE - 1, #descendants)
            for j = i, batchEnd do
                local v = descendants[j]
                if v and v.Parent then
                    cleanObject(v)
                    if v:IsA("Model") then
                        stopAnimations(v)
                    end
                end
            end
            if i + BATCH_SIZE <= #descendants then
                task.wait() -- Yield to let frames render between batches
            end
        end
    end)

    workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(v)
        if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
        task.wait()
        cleanObject(v)
        if v:IsA("Model") then
            stopAnimations(v)
        end
    end)

    for _, player in pairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character then
            stripCharacter(player.Character)
        end
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
            task.wait(1)
            stripCharacter(character)
        end)
    end

    players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
            task.wait(1)
            stripCharacter(character)
        end)
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        while _G.FPSBoostEnabled and task.wait(3) do
            for _, player in pairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    stripCharacter(player.Character)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function getTraits(brainrot)
    local foundTraits = {}
    local foundIds = {}
    pcall(function()
        for _, child in pairs(brainrot:GetDescendants()) do
            -- Check named trait containers
            if child.Name == "Traits" or child.Name == "TraitsFrame" then
                for _, traitChild in pairs(child:GetChildren()) do
                    if traitChild:IsA("ImageLabel") then
                        local imageId = traitChild.Image
                        if traitsData[imageId] and not foundIds[imageId] then
                            foundIds[imageId] = true
                            table.insert(foundTraits, { image = imageId, data = traitsData[imageId] })
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            -- Also check any ImageLabel descendant directly (some game versions skip the Traits frame)
            if child:IsA("ImageLabel") and not foundIds[child.Image] then
                local imageId = child.Image
                if traitsData[imageId] then
                    foundIds[imageId] = true
                    table.insert(foundTraits, { image = imageId, data = traitsData[imageId] })
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    return foundTraits
end

local function createTraitBillboard(brainrot)
    for _, child in ipairs(brainrot:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") and child.Name == "TraitESP" then child:Destroy() end
    end

    local traits = getTraits(brainrot)
    if #traits == 0 then return nil end

    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "TraitESP"
    billboard.Adornee = brainrot
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 30)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, -7, 0)
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true

    local traitFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    traitFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    traitFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    traitFrame.Parent = billboard

    local traitList = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    traitList.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
    traitList.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
    traitList.Padding = UDim.new(0, 6)
    traitList.Parent = traitFrame

    for _, trait in ipairs(traits) do
        local traitIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
        traitIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
        traitIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        traitIcon.Image = trait.image
        traitIcon.Parent = traitFrame

    end

    billboard.Parent = brainrot
    return billboard
end

local function updateTraitESPColors()
end

local function updateTraitESP()
    if not _G.traitESPEnabled then return end
    local allDetectedItems = findAllBrainrots()

    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedTraitESP) do
        local stillValid = false
        for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do if item.brainrot == brainrot then stillValid = true break end end
        if not stillValid then
            if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
            trackedTraitESP[brainrot] = nil
        end
    end

    for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do
        if not trackedTraitESP[item.brainrot] then
            local billboard = createTraitBillboard(item.brainrot)
            if billboard then trackedTraitESP[item.brainrot] = { billboard = billboard } end
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllTraitESP()
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedTraitESP) do
        if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
    end
    trackedTraitESP = {}
    _G.trackedTraitESP = {}
end

_G.updateTraitESP = updateTraitESP
_G.removeAllTraitESP = removeAllTraitESP
_G.toggleTraitESP = function()
    _G.traitESPEnabled = not _G.traitESPEnabled
    if not _G.traitESPEnabled then removeAllTraitESP() end
end
_G.updateTraitESPColors = updateTraitESPColors

local function getMutations(brainrot)
    local foundMutation
    local final = "Normal"

    pcall(function()
        for _, child in pairs(brainrot:GetDescendants()) do
            if child.Name == "Mutation" then
                foundMutation = child
            end
        end
    end)

    if not foundMutation then return {"Normal"} end

    final = foundMutation.Text
    if foundMutation.Visible == false then final = "Normal" end

    return {final}
end

local function createMutationBillboard(brainrot)
    for _, child in ipairs(brainrot:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") and child.Name == "MutationESP" then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end

    if not _G.mutationESPEnabled then
        return nil
    end

    local mutations = getMutations(brainrot)

    if #mutations == 0 then
        return nil
    end

    local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    billboard.Name = "MutationESP"
    billboard.Adornee = brainrot
    billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 40)
    billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, -3, 0)
    billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true

    local mutationFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    mutationFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    mutationFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    mutationFrame.Parent = billboard

    local mutationList = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    mutationList.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
    mutationList.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
    mutationList.Padding = UDim.new(0, 5)
    mutationList.Parent = mutationFrame

    local mutationTextSize = 12
    if #mutations >= 4 then
        mutationTextSize = 8
    elseif #mutations >= 2 then
        mutationTextSize = 10
    end

    for _, mutation in ipairs(mutations) do
        local mutLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        mutLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 1, 0)
        mutLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1  -- No background box (from document)
        mutLabel.Text = string.upper(mutation)
        local mutColor = getMutationColor(mutation)
        mutLabel.TextColor3 = mutColor
        mutLabel.TextSize = mutationTextSize
        mutLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        mutLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        mutLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        mutLabel.Parent = mutationFrame
    end

    billboard.Parent = brainrot
    return billboard
end

local function updateMutationESPColors()
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedMutationESP) do
        if espData.billboard and espData.billboard.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                local mutationFrame = espData.billboard:FindFirstChildOfClass("Frame")
                if mutationFrame then
                    for _, label in ipairs(mutationFrame:GetChildren()) do
                        if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                            local mutationName = label.Text:lower()
                            local mutColor = getMutationColor(mutationName)
                            label.TextColor3 = mutColor
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function updateMutationESP()
    if not _G.mutationESPEnabled then
        return
    end
    local allDetectedItems = findAllBrainrots()

    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedMutationESP) do
        local stillValid = false
        for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do if item.brainrot == brainrot then stillValid = true break end end
        if not stillValid then
            if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
            trackedMutationESP[brainrot] = nil
        end
    end

    for _, item in ipairs(allDetectedItems) do
        if not trackedMutationESP[item.brainrot] then
            local billboard = createMutationBillboard(item.brainrot)
            if billboard then trackedMutationESP[item.brainrot] = { billboard = billboard } end
        end
    end
end

local function removeAllMutationESP()
    for brainrot, espData in pairs(trackedMutationESP) do
        if espData.billboard then pcall(function() espData.billboard:Destroy() end) end
    end
    trackedMutationESP = {}
    _G.trackedMutationESP = {}
end

_G.updateMutationESP = updateMutationESP
_G.removeAllMutationESP = removeAllMutationESP
_G.toggleMutationESP = function()
    _G.mutationESPEnabled = not _G.mutationESPEnabled
    if not _G.mutationESPEnabled then removeAllMutationESP() end
end
_G.updateMutationESPColors = updateMutationESPColors

            checkCounter = 0
            if not plotBeam or not plotBeam.Parent or not plotBeamAttachment0 or not plotBeamAttachment0.Parent then
                pcall(function() createPlotBeam() end)
            end
        end
    end))

LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    task.wait(1)
    if _G.plotTransparencyEnabled and plotsFolder then for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do applyTransparencyToPlot(plot) end end
    if _G.rainbowBeamEnabled then pcall(createPlotBeam) end
    resetBrainrotBeam()
    task.wait(0.1)
    if _G.brainrotBeamEnabled then pcall(updateBrainrotBeam) end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local plotsFolder = Workspace:WaitForChild("Plots", 10)
    if not plotsFolder then return end

    local connectedPlots = {}

    local function handlePlot(plot)
        if connectedPlots[plot] then return end
        connectedPlots[plot] = true

        if _G.plotTransparencyEnabled then
            for _, descendant in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
                if descendant:IsA("BasePart") then
                    applyTransparencyToPlot(plot)
                    break
                end
            end
        end

plot.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(descendant)
        end)

        if _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled then
            pcall(updatePlotTimerESP)
        end
    end

    for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
        handlePlot(plot)
    end

    plotsFolder.ChildAdded:Connect(handlePlot)
end)

Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
    if not _G.MineESPEnabled then return end
    task.wait(0.1)
    local name = obj.Name:lower()
    if name:find("subspace") or name:find("tripmine") then
        local topMine = getTopLevelMine(obj)
        if topMine and not trackedMines[topMine] then pcall(function() addMineESP(topMine) end) end
    end
end)

Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(playerObj)
    removeStealingESP(playerObj.UserId)
    removeStealingChams(playerObj.UserId)
    removePlayerESP(playerObj.UserId)
end)

for _, playerObj in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
    if playerObj ~= LocalPlayer then
        playerObj.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
            task.spawn(function()
                task.wait(0.1)
                removeStealingESP(playerObj.UserId)
                removeStealingChams(playerObj.UserId)
                if _G.playerESPEnabled then pcall(function() removePlayerESP(playerObj.UserId) addPlayerESP(playerObj) end) end
            end)
        end)
    end
end

Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(playerObj)
    playerObj.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
        task.spawn(function()
            task.wait(1.5)
            if _G.playerESPEnabled then pcall(function() removePlayerESP(playerObj.UserId) addPlayerESP(playerObj) end) end
        end)
    end)
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local dxhubGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    dxhubGui.Name = "22SHubGui"
    dxhubGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    dxhubGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
    dxhubGui.Parent = cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui"))


    local GUI_WIDTH = isMobile and 480 or 620
    local GUI_HEIGHT = isMobile and 400 or 480
    local SIDEBAR_WIDTH = isMobile and 85 or 110

    local MainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    MainFrame.Name = "22SMainFrame"
    MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, GUI_WIDTH, 0, GUI_HEIGHT)
    MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -GUI_WIDTH/2, 0.5, -GUI_HEIGHT/2)
    MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 14, 16)
    MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0
    MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    MainFrame.Visible = false
    MainFrame.Parent = dxhubGui


    -- ── Partículas blancas flotantes ──────────────────────────────────────
    local function addParticles(parentFrame)
        if not parentFrame then return end
        local RunSvc = game:GetService("RunService")
        local particleCount = 18
        local particles = {}

        for i = 1, particleCount do
            local p = Instance.new("Frame")
            p.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            p.BorderSizePixel = 0
            local sz = math.random(2, 5)
            p.Size = UDim2.new(0, sz, 0, sz)
            p.BackgroundTransparency = math.random(40, 75) / 100
            p.ZIndex = 9999
            p.Position = UDim2.new(math.random(0, 95) / 100, 0, math.random(0, 95) / 100, 0)
            Instance.new("UICorner", p).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
            p.Parent = parentFrame

            particles[i] = {
                frame   = p,
                x       = math.random(0, 95) / 100,
                y       = math.random(0, 100) / 100,
                speed   = math.random(3, 9) / 1000,
                drift   = (math.random(-10, 10)) / 10000,
                opacity = math.random(25, 65) / 100,
                phase   = math.random(0, 628) / 100,
            }
        end

        local conn
        conn = RunSvc.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
            if not parentFrame or not parentFrame.Parent then
                conn:Disconnect()
                return
            end
            local t = tick()
            for _, pt in ipairs(particles) do
                if not pt.frame or not pt.frame.Parent then continue end
                pt.y = pt.y - pt.speed
                pt.x = pt.x + pt.drift
                if pt.y < -0.05 then
                    pt.y = 1.05
                    pt.x = math.random(0, 95) / 100
                end
                if pt.x < 0 then pt.x = 1 end
                if pt.x > 1 then pt.x = 0 end
                local pulse = 0.15 * math.sin(t * 1.5 + pt.phase)
                local alpha = math.clamp(pt.opacity + pulse, 0, 0.8)
                pt.frame.Position = UDim2.new(pt.x, 0, pt.y, 0)
                pt.frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1 - alpha
            end
        end)
    end
    -- ── Fin partículas ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    Instance.new("UICorner", MainFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, isMobile and 8 or 10)
    task.spawn(function() addParticles(MainFrame) end)

    local HeaderBar = Instance.new("Frame", MainFrame)
    HeaderBar.Name = "HeaderBar"
    HeaderBar.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 38 or 46)
    HeaderBar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    HeaderBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 19, 22)
    HeaderBar.BackgroundTransparency = 0
    HeaderBar.BorderSizePixel = 0
    HeaderBar.ZIndex = 2

    Instance.new("UICorner", HeaderBar).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, isMobile and 8 or 10)

    local TitleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", HeaderBar)
    TitleLabel.Name = "Title"
    TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 1, 0)
    TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 0)
    TitleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    TitleLabel.Text = "Bomboclat Wallah Hub"
    TitleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
    TitleLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 14 or 16
    TitleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    TitleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    TitleLabel.ZIndex = 3

    local CloseButton = Instance.new("TextButton", HeaderBar)
    CloseButton.Name = "CloseButton"
    CloseButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 18 or 20, 0, isMobile and 18 or 20)
    CloseButton.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 32 or 38), 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
    CloseButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 35)
    CloseButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
    CloseButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
    CloseButton.Text = "X"
    CloseButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    CloseButton.TextSize = isMobile and 12 or 14
    CloseButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 210)
    CloseButton.ZIndex = 4

    Instance.new("UICorner", CloseButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    CloseButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(CloseButton, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 42, 48)}):Play()
    end)
    CloseButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(CloseButton, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 35)}):Play()
    end)
    CloseButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        MainFrame.Visible = false
    end)

    -- Inconspicuous snake game button (small dot left of close)
    local SnakeBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", HeaderBar)
    SnakeBtn.Name = "SnakeBtn"
    SnakeBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 14 or 16, 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)
    SnakeBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 52 or 62), 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 8))
    SnakeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(34, 36, 40)
    SnakeBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.4
    SnakeBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
    SnakeBtn.Text = ""
    SnakeBtn.ZIndex = 4
    Instance.new("UICorner", SnakeBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    SnakeBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(SnakeBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 180, 60), BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end)
    SnakeBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(SnakeBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(34, 36, 40), BackgroundTransparency = 0.4}):Play()
    end)

    -- Snake game overlay
    local snakeGameActive = false
    local snakeFrame = nil

    local function createSnakeGame()
        if snakeFrame then snakeFrame:Destroy() end

        local GRID = 15
        local CELL = isMobile and 14 or 18
        local BOARD = GRID * CELL
        local TICK_RATE = 0.12

        snakeFrame = Instance.new("Frame", MainFrame)
        snakeFrame.Name = "SnakeGame"
        snakeFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, BOARD + 20, 0, BOARD + 60)
        snakeFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -(BOARD + 20)/2, 0.5, -(BOARD + 60)/2)
        snakeFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 10, 10)
        snakeFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.05
        snakeFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        snakeFrame.ZIndex = 20
        Instance.new("UICorner", snakeFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)

        local scoreLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", snakeFrame)
        scoreLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 30)
        scoreLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 5)
        scoreLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        scoreLabel.Text = "Snake  |  Score: 0"
        scoreLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        scoreLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        scoreLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
        scoreLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        scoreLabel.ZIndex = 21

        local closeSnake = Instance.new("TextButton", snakeFrame)
        closeSnake.Size = UDim2.new(0, 24, 0, 24)
        closeSnake.Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0, 6)
        closeSnake.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 50, 50)
        closeSnake.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
        closeSnake.BorderSizePixel = 0
        closeSnake.Text = "X"
        closeSnake.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        closeSnake.TextSize = 12
        closeSnake.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 150, 150)
        closeSnake.ZIndex = 22
        Instance.new("UICorner", closeSnake).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local board = Instance.new("Frame", snakeFrame)
        board.Size = UDim2.new(0, BOARD, 0, BOARD)
        board.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -BOARD/2, 0, 38)
        board.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 20)
        board.BorderSizePixel = 0
        board.ZIndex = 21
        Instance.new("UICorner", board).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

        -- Cell pool
        local cellPool = {}
        local function getCell(x, y, color)
            local cell = Instance.new("Frame", board)
            cell.Size = UDim2.new(0, CELL - 1, 0, CELL - 1)
            cell.Position = UDim2.new(0, (x - 1) * CELL, 0, (y - 1) * CELL)
            cell.BackgroundColor3 = color
            cell.BorderSizePixel = 0
            cell.ZIndex = 22
            Instance.new("UICorner", cell).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
            return cell
        end

        -- Game state
        local snake = {{x = 8, y = 8}, {x = 7, y = 8}, {x = 6, y = 8}}
        local dir = {x = 1, y = 0}
        local nextDir = {x = 1, y = 0}
        local food = {x = 12, y = 8}
        local score = 0
        local alive = true
        local running = true
        local cells = {}

        local function spawnFood()
            local occupied = {}
            for _, s in ipairs(snake) do
                occupied[s.x .. "," .. s.y] = true
            end
            local attempts = 0
            repeat
                food.x = math.random(1, GRID)
                food.y = math.random(1, GRID)
                attempts = attempts + 1
            until not occupied[food.x .. "," .. food.y] or attempts > 200
        end

        local function render()
            for _, c in ipairs(cells) do c:Destroy() end
            cells = {}

            -- Food
            table.insert(cells, getCell(food.x, food.y, Color3.fromRGB(255, 60, 60)))

            -- Snake
            for i, s in ipairs(snake) do
                local brightness = math.max(80, 200 - (i - 1) * 12)
                table.insert(cells, getCell(s.x, s.y, Color3.fromRGB(40, brightness, 40)))
            end
        end

        local function step()
            if not alive then return end
            dir = nextDir

            local head = snake[1]
            local newHead = {x = head.x + dir.x, y = head.y + dir.y}

            -- Wrap around walls
            if newHead.x < 1 then newHead.x = GRID
            elseif newHead.x > GRID then newHead.x = 1 end
            if newHead.y < 1 then newHead.y = GRID
            elseif newHead.y > GRID then newHead.y = 1 end

            -- Self collision
            for _, s in ipairs(snake) do
                if s.x == newHead.x and s.y == newHead.y then
                    alive = false
                    scoreLabel.Text = "Game Over!  Score: " .. score .. "  (press any key)"
                    return
                end
            end

            table.insert(snake, 1, newHead)

            if newHead.x == food.x and newHead.y == food.y then
                score = score + 1
                scoreLabel.Text = "Snake  |  Score: " .. score
                spawnFood()
            else
                table.remove(snake)
            end

            render()
        end

        -- Input
        local snakeInputConn
        snakeInputConn = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gp)
            if not running then return end
            if not alive then
                -- Restart
                snake = {{x = 8, y = 8}, {x = 7, y = 8}, {x = 6, y = 8}}
                dir = {x = 1, y = 0}
                nextDir = {x = 1, y = 0}
                score = 0
                alive = true
                spawnFood()
                scoreLabel.Text = "Snake  |  Score: 0"
                render()
                return
            end

            local kc = input.KeyCode
            if (kc == Enum.KeyCode.W or kc == Enum.KeyCode.Up) and dir.y ~= 1 then
                nextDir = {x = 0, y = -1}
            elseif (kc == Enum.KeyCode.S or kc == Enum.KeyCode.Down) and dir.y ~= -1 then
                nextDir = {x = 0, y = 1}
            elseif (kc == Enum.KeyCode.A or kc == Enum.KeyCode.Left) and dir.x ~= 1 then
                nextDir = {x = -1, y = 0}
            elseif (kc == Enum.KeyCode.D or kc == Enum.KeyCode.Right) and dir.x ~= -1 then
                nextDir = {x = 1, y = 0}
            end
        end)

        -- Touch/swipe controls for mobile
        local touchStart = nil
        local touchConn1, touchConn2
        touchConn1 = UserInputService.TouchStarted:Connect(function(touch)
            if not running then return end
            touchStart = touch.Position
        end)
        touchConn2 = UserInputService.TouchEnded:Connect(function(touch)
            if not running or not touchStart or not alive then return end
            local delta = touch.Position - touchStart
            if delta.Magnitude < 20 then return end
            if math.abs(delta.X) > math.abs(delta.Y) then
                if delta.X > 0 and dir.x ~= -1 then nextDir = {x = 1, y = 0}
                elseif delta.X < 0 and dir.x ~= 1 then nextDir = {x = -1, y = 0} end
            else
                if delta.Y > 0 and dir.y ~= -1 then nextDir = {x = 0, y = 1}
                elseif delta.Y < 0 and dir.y ~= 1 then nextDir = {x = 0, y = -1} end
            end
            touchStart = nil
        end)

        closeSnake.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            running = false
            snakeGameActive = false
            if snakeInputConn then snakeInputConn:Disconnect() end
            if touchConn1 then touchConn1:Disconnect() end
            if touchConn2 then touchConn2:Disconnect() end
            snakeFrame:Destroy()
            snakeFrame = nil
        end)

        render()

        -- Game loop
        task.spawn(function()
            while running do
                step()
                task.wait(TICK_RATE)
            end
        end)
    end

    SnakeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if snakeGameActive then
            if snakeFrame then
                snakeFrame.Visible = not snakeFrame.Visible
            end
        else
            snakeGameActive = true
            createSnakeGame()
        end
    end)

    local function createTabButton(name, index)
        local TabButton = Instance.new("TextButton", TabList)
        TabButton.Name = name .. "Tab"
        TabButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 28 or 32)
        TabButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 23, 28)
        TabButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        TabButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
        TabButton.Text = name
        TabButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        TabButton.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        TabButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 150, 165)
        TabButton.LayoutOrder = index
        TabButton.ZIndex = 4

        Instance.new("UICorner", TabButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)


        TabButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if TabButton.TextColor3 ~= Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) then
                TweenService:Create(TabButton, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.05}):Play()
            end
        end)
        TabButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if TabButton.TextColor3 ~= Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) then
                TweenService:Create(TabButton, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.05}):Play()
            end
        end)

        tabButtons[name] = {button = TabButton}
        return TabButton
    end

    local function createContentPanel(name)
        local Panel = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", ContentArea)
        Panel.Name = name .. "Panel"
        Panel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        Panel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)

        Panel.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        Panel.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        Panel.Visible = false
        Panel.ZIndex = 3

        local PanelLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", Panel)
        PanelLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 6)
        PanelLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        PanelPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 8)
        PanelPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 8)
        PanelPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 4)
        PanelPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 8)

        return Panel
    end

    local currentTab = nil
    local function switchTab(tabName)
        for name, data in pairs(tabButtons) do
            TweenService:Create(data.button, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 23, 28),
                BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
                TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 150, 165)
            }):Play()
        end

        for name, panel in pairs(contentPanels) do
            panel.Visible = false
        end

        if tabButtons[tabName] then
            TweenService:Create(tabButtons[tabName].button, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32),
                BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
                TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            }):Play()
        end

        if contentPanels[tabName] then
            contentPanels[tabName].Visible = true
        end

        currentTab = tabName
    end

    for i, tabName in ipairs(tabs) do
        local button = createTabButton(tabName, i)
        createContentPanel(tabName)

        button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            switchTab(tabName)
        end)
    end
