    _G.createdxhubToggle = function(parent, labelText, defaultState, callback)
        local ToggleContainer = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        ToggleContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 32 or 36)
        ToggleContainer.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
        ToggleContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        ToggleContainer.BorderSizePixel = 0
        ToggleContainer.ZIndex = 4

        Instance.new("UICorner", ToggleContainer).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel", ToggleContainer)
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -55, 1, 0)
        Label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.Text = labelText
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        Label.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.ZIndex = 5

        local SwitchTrack = Instance.new("Frame", ToggleContainer)
        SwitchTrack.Name = "SwitchTrack"
        SwitchTrack.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 36 or 40, 0, isMobile and 16 or 18)
        SwitchTrack.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 44 or 48), 0.5, -(isMobile and 8 or 9))
        SwitchTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)
        SwitchTrack.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SwitchTrack.ZIndex = 5

        Instance.new("UICorner", SwitchTrack).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local SwitchKnob = Instance.new("Frame", SwitchTrack)
        SwitchKnob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 12 or 14, 0, isMobile and 12 or 14)
        SwitchKnob.Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 6 or 7))
        SwitchKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 210)
        SwitchKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SwitchKnob.ZIndex = 6

        Instance.new("UICorner", SwitchKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local isEnabled = defaultState or false

        _G.SWITCH_TRACKS = _G.SWITCH_TRACKS or {}
        _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR = _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        table.insert(_G.SWITCH_TRACKS, {track = SwitchTrack, getState = function() return isEnabled end})

        local function updateToggle()
            if isEnabled then
                TweenService:Create(SwitchKnob, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
                    Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 14 or 16), 0.5, -(isMobile and 6 or 7)),
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
                }):Play()
                TweenService:Create(SwitchTrack, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                }):Play()
            else
                TweenService:Create(SwitchKnob, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
                    Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 6 or 7)),
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 210)
                }):Play()
                TweenService:Create(SwitchTrack, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)
                }):Play()
            end
        end

        local ToggleButton = Instance.new("TextButton", ToggleContainer)
        ToggleButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        ToggleButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        ToggleButton.Text = ""
        ToggleButton.ZIndex = 7

        ToggleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            isEnabled = not isEnabled
            updateToggle()
            if callback then
                callback(isEnabled)
            end
            if _G.saveKeybinds then
                task.defer(function()
                    pcall(_G.saveKeybinds)
                end)
            end
        end)

        ToggleButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(ToggleContainer, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.05}):Play()
        end)
        ToggleButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(ToggleContainer, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.05}):Play()
        end)

        updateToggle()

        if isEnabled and callback then
            task.defer(function()
                pcall(callback, isEnabled)
            end)
        end

        return ToggleContainer
    end

    _G.createdxhubKeybind = function(parent, labelText, defaultKey, callback)
        local varName = labelText:gsub(" ", "") .. "Key"  -- e.g., "Instant Clone" -> "InstantCloneKey"
        local varOverrides = {
            ManualTeleportKey = "ManualTPKey",
            AutoTeleportKey = "AutoTPKey",
        }
        local actualVarName = varOverrides[varName] or varName

        if not _G[actualVarName] and defaultKey then
            local success, keyCode = pcall(function()
                return Enum.KeyCode[defaultKey]
            end)
            if success then
                _G[actualVarName] = keyCode
            end
        end

        local displayKey = defaultKey or "None"
        if _G[actualVarName] and typeof(_G[actualVarName]) == "EnumItem" then
            displayKey = _G[actualVarName].Name
        end

        local KeybindContainer = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        KeybindContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 32 or 36)
        KeybindContainer.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
        KeybindContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        KeybindContainer.BorderSizePixel = 0
        KeybindContainer.ZIndex = 4

        Instance.new("UICorner", KeybindContainer).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        local KeybindLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", KeybindContainer)
        KeybindLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0)
        KeybindLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        KeybindLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        KeybindLabel.Text = labelText
        KeybindLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        KeybindLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        KeybindLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
        KeybindLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        KeybindLabel.ZIndex = 5

        local KeybindButton = Instance.new("TextButton", KeybindContainer)
        KeybindButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.4, -16, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
        KeybindButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.6, 4, 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
        KeybindButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)
        KeybindButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
        KeybindButton.Text = "[" .. displayKey .. "]"
        KeybindButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        KeybindButton.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
        KeybindButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 190, 200)
        KeybindButton.ZIndex = 5

        Instance.new("UICorner", KeybindButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        KeybindButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            KeybindButton.Text = "Press any key..."
            KeybindButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

            local connection
            connection = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
                if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
                    local keyName = input.KeyCode.Name
                    KeybindButton.Text = "[" .. keyName .. "]"
                    KeybindButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 190, 200)

                    connection:Disconnect()

                    if callback then
                        callback(input.KeyCode)
                    end

                end
            end)
        end)

        return KeybindContainer
    end

        OptionsScroll.BorderSizePixel = 0

        OptionsScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        OptionsScroll.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        OptionsScroll.ZIndex = 101

        local OptionsLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", OptionsScroll)
        OptionsLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)

        for _, option in ipairs(options) do

            OptionButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, isMobile and 28 or 32)
            OptionButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
            OptionButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
            OptionButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
            OptionButton.Text = option
            OptionButton.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            OptionButton.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
            OptionButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
            OptionButton.ZIndex = 102

            Instance.new("UICorner", OptionButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            OptionButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(OptionButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
                    BackgroundTransparency = 0.85
                }):Play()
            end)
            OptionButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(OptionButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32),
                    BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
                }):Play()
            end)

            OptionButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                SelectedOption.Text = option
                OptionsList.Visible = false
                if callback then
                    callback(option)
                end
                if _G.saveKeybinds then
                    task.defer(function()
                        pcall(_G.saveKeybinds)
                    end)
                end

        end

        local DropdownButton = Instance.new("TextButton", DropdownContainer)
        DropdownButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -20, 1, 0)
        DropdownButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 4, 0, 0)
        DropdownButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        DropdownButton.Text = ""
        DropdownButton.ZIndex = 7

        DropdownButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            OptionsList.Visible = not OptionsList.Visible
        end)

        return DropdownContainer
    end

    _G.createdxhubColorPicker = function(parent, labelText, defaultColor, callback)
        local ColorContainer = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        ColorContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 32 or 36)

        Label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.Text = labelText
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        Label.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12

        ColorBox.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 36 or 40), 0.5, -(isMobile and 10 or 12))
        ColorBox.BackgroundColor3 = defaultColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        ColorBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
        ColorBox.ZIndex = 5

        Instance.new("UICorner", ColorBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)


        local colorPalette = {
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0), Color3.fromRGB(255, 85, 85), Color3.fromRGB(200, 0, 0),
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 170, 0), Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100), Color3.fromRGB(200, 120, 0),
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0), Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 150), Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 0),
            Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0), Color3.fromRGB(85, 255, 85), Color3.fromRGB(0, 200, 0),
            Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 255), Color3.fromRGB(0, 200, 255), Color3.fromRGB(0, 150, 200),
            Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 255), Color3.fromRGB(85, 85, 255), Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 200),
            Color3.fromRGB(170, 0, 255), Color3.fromRGB(200, 85, 255), Color3.fromRGB(130, 0, 200),
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 255), Color3.fromRGB(255, 85, 255), Color3.fromRGB(200, 0, 200),
            Color3.fromRGB(139, 69, 19), Color3.fromRGB(180, 100, 50), Color3.fromRGB(100, 50, 20),
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200), Color3.fromRGB(128, 128, 128),
            Color3.fromRGB(64, 64, 64), Color3.fromRGB(32, 32, 32), Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0),
        }

        local ColorWheel = Instance.new("Frame")
        ColorWheel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 320 or 380, 0, isMobile and 240 or 280)
        ColorWheel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -(isMobile and 160 or 190), 0.5, -(isMobile and 120 or 140))
        ColorWheel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 18, 22)
        ColorWheel.BorderSizePixel = 0
        ColorWheel.Visible = false
        ColorWheel.ZIndex = 3000

        Instance.new("UICorner", ColorWheel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)


        local WheelTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel", ColorWheel)
        WheelTitle.Size = UDim2.new(1, -50, 0, isMobile and 32 or 38)
        WheelTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        WheelTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        WheelTitle.Text = "ðŸŽ¨ " .. labelText
        WheelTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
        WheelTitle.TextSize = isMobile and 13 or 15
        WheelTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        WheelTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        WheelTitle.ZIndex = 101

        local CloseBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", ColorWheel)
        CloseBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 18 or 20, 0, isMobile and 18 or 20)
        CloseBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 22 or 24), 0, isMobile and 4 or 4)
        CloseBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)
        CloseBtn.Text = "—"
        CloseBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold

        Instance.new("UICorner", CloseBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            ColorWheel.Visible = false
        end)

        local ColorGrid = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", ColorWheel)
        ColorGrid.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, -(isMobile and 44 or 50))
        ColorGrid.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, isMobile and 36 or 42)

        GridLayout.CellSize = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 38 or 44, 0, isMobile and 38 or 44)
        GridLayout.CellPadding = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 8)
        GridLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        for i, color in ipairs(colorPalette) do

            ColorOption.Text = ""
            ColorOption.ZIndex = 102

            Instance.new("UICorner", ColorOption).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            ColorOption.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            end)

                end

        local PickerButton = Instance.new("TextButton", ColorContainer)

    end

    for tabName, panel in pairs(contentPanels) do

    if contentPanels["Main"] then
        local mainPanel = contentPanels["Main"]

        _G.createdxhubSection(mainPanel, "TELEPORT")

        _G.createdxhubToggle(mainPanel, "Auto Teleport", _G.AutoTeleportEnabled or false, function(enabled)
            warn("[dxhub] Auto TP toggled: " .. tostring(enabled))
            _G.AutoTeleportEnabled = enabled
            _G.autoTPButtonEnabled = enabled
            if _G.savedBinds then _G.savedBinds.AutoTPEnabled = enabled end
            if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
            if _G.setAutoTPState then
                pcall(function() _G.setAutoTPState(enabled) end)
            end
            if enabled then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local waitTime = 0
                    while not _G.TeleportToHighest and waitTime < 10 do
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        waitTime = waitTime + 0.1
                    end

                    for i = 1, 30 do
                        local debris = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
                        if debris and #debris:GetChildren() > 0 then
                            task.wait(0.3)
                            break
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end

                    if _G.TeleportToHighest and _G.AutoTeleportEnabled then
                        repeat task.wait(1) until game:IsLoaded()
                        local ok, err = pcall(_G.TeleportToHighest)
                        if not ok then
                            warn("[dxhub] Auto TP error: " .. tostring(err))
                        end
                        task.delay(3, function()
                            _G.isTeleporting = false
                        end)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(mainPanel, "Auto Clone After Teleport", _G.AutoCloneAfterTP or false, function(enabled)
            _G.AutoCloneAfterTP = enabled
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(mainPanel, "Auto Float To Brainrot", _G.AutoFloatToBrainrot or false, function(enabled)
            _G.AutoFloatToBrainrot = enabled
            _G.AutoFloatThirdFloor = enabled

            _G.AutoTpBackAfterHit = enabled

        -- Teleport Type removed from main tab - now controlled via Auto Steal Panel

        stealRadiusMainInput.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)
        stealRadiusMainInput.BorderSizePixel = 0
        stealRadiusMainInput.Text = tostring(_G.AutoStealRadius or 60)
        stealRadiusMainInput.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        stealRadiusMainInput.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
        stealRadiusMainInput.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
        stealRadiusMainInput.ClearTextOnFocus = false
        Instance.new("UICorner", stealRadiusMainInput).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
        stealRadiusMainInput.FocusLost:Connect(function()
            local v = tonumber(stealRadiusMainInput.Text)
            if v and v > 0 then
                _G.AutoStealRadius = v
            else
                stealRadiusMainInput.Text = tostring(_G.AutoStealRadius or 60)
            end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubDropdown(mainPanel, "Steal Type",
            {"Highest Value", "Priority Config"},

                    _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = false
                else
                    _G.AutoStealHighestEnabled = false
                    _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = true
                end
            end
        )

        if (_G.StealType or "Highest Value") == "Highest Value" then
            _G.AutoStealHighestEnabled = true
            _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = false

        _G.createdxhubSection(mainPanel, "AFTER STEAL")

        if _G.autoKickEnabled == nil then _G.autoKickEnabled = false end

        local afterStealSpeedFill = Instance.new("Frame", afterStealSpeedTrack)
        afterStealSpeedFill.Size = UDim2.new(initPctAS, 0, 1, 0)
        afterStealSpeedFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

        Instance.new("UICorner", afterStealSpeedFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        afterStealSpeedKnob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
        afterStealSpeedKnob.Position = UDim2.new(initPctAS, -5, 0.5, -5)
        afterStealSpeedKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        afterStealSpeedKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        afterStealSpeedKnob.ZIndex = 7

        local afterStealSpeedDragging = false
        afterStealSpeedKnob.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                afterStealSpeedDragging = true
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                afterStealSpeedDragging = false
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if afterStealSpeedDragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                local trackAbsPos = afterStealSpeedTrack.AbsolutePosition.X
                local trackAbsSize = afterStealSpeedTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
                local relX = math.clamp((input.Position.X - trackAbsPos) / trackAbsSize, 0, 1)
                local newVal = math.floor(16 + relX * (29 - 16) + 0.5)
                _G.AfterStealWalkspeedValue = newVal
                afterStealSpeedLabel.Text = "After Steal Speed: " .. tostring(newVal)
                afterStealSpeedFill.Size = UDim2.new(relX, 0, 1, 0)
                afterStealSpeedKnob.Position = UDim2.new(relX, -5, 0.5, -5)
            end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(mainPanel, "Auto Kick After Steal", _G.autoKickEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.autoKickEnabled = enabled

            _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal = enabled

            _G.AutoTurretOnSteal = enabled
            if enabled and _G.scanExistingSentries then
                pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)

            _G.CarpetSpeedEnabled = enabled

        carpetSliderFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

        carpetSliderKnob.Position = UDim2.new(initialPct, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
        carpetSliderKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        carpetSliderKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        carpetSliderKnob.ZIndex = 7
        Instance.new("UICorner", carpetSliderKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local carpetSliderDragging = false

        local function updateCarpetSlider(input)
            local trackPos = carpetSliderTrack.AbsolutePosition.X
            local trackWidth = carpetSliderTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
            local relativeX = math.clamp((input.Position.X - trackPos) / trackWidth, 0, 1)
            local speed = math.floor(100 + relativeX * 400)
            _G.CarpetSpeedValue = speed
            carpetSpeedLabel.Text = "Speed: " .. tostring(speed)
            carpetSliderFill.Size = UDim2.new(relativeX, 0, 1, 0)
            carpetSliderKnob.Position = UDim2.new(relativeX, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
        end

        carpetSliderTrack.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                carpetSliderDragging = true
                updateCarpetSlider(input)
            end
        end)

        carpetSliderKnob.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                carpetSliderDragging = true
            end
        end)

        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if carpetSliderDragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                updateCarpetSlider(input)
            end
        end)

        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                carpetSliderDragging = false
            end
        end)

    end

        _G.StealLoggerEnabled = _G.StealLoggerEnabled or false
        _G.StolenItemsList = _G.StolenItemsList or {}

        _G.createdxhubToggle(stealsPanel, "Enable Steal Tracker", _G.StealLoggerEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.StealLoggerEnabled = enabled
            if _G.saveKeybinds then task.defer(pcall, _G.saveKeybinds) end
        end)

        -- Scrollable list container for stolen items
        local stealLogScroll = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", stealsPanel)
        stealLogScroll.Name = "StealLogScroll"
        stealLogScroll.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 240 or 320)
        stealLogScroll.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 19, 23)
        stealLogScroll.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
        stealLogScroll.BorderSizePixel = 0
        stealLogScroll.ScrollBarThickness = 4
        stealLogScroll.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 75)
        stealLogScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        stealLogScroll.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        stealLogScroll.ZIndex = 4
        Instance.new("UICorner", stealLogScroll).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        local stealLogLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", stealLogScroll)
        stealLogLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
        stealLogLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        local stealLogPadding = Instance.new("UIPadding", stealLogScroll)
        stealLogPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 6)
        stealLogPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 6)
        stealLogPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 4)
        stealLogPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 4)

        local noItemsLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", stealLogScroll)
        noItemsLabel.Name = "NoItemsLabel"
        noItemsLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)
        noItemsLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        noItemsLabel.Text = "No steals logged yet..."
        noItemsLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        noItemsLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
        noItemsLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 95, 110)
        noItemsLabel.ZIndex = 5

        local stealEntryOrder = 0

        _G.addStolenItemEntry = function(itemName, timestamp)
            if not itemName or itemName == "" then return end
            pcall(function()
                if noItemsLabel then noItemsLabel.Visible = false end
                stealEntryOrder = stealEntryOrder + 1
                local entryIndex = stealEntryOrder
                local stealTime = timestamp or os.time()
                table.insert(_G.StolenItemsList, {name = itemName, time = stealTime})

                local EntryFrame = Instance.new("Frame", stealLogScroll)
                EntryFrame.Name = "StealEntry_" .. entryIndex
                EntryFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 28 or 32)
                EntryFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
                EntryFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
                EntryFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                EntryFrame.LayoutOrder = entryIndex
                EntryFrame.ZIndex = 5
                Instance.new("UICorner", EntryFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

                -- Item name only
                local NameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", EntryFrame)
                NameLabel.Name = "ItemName"
                NameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -45, 1, 0)
                NameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
                NameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                NameLabel.Text = itemName
                NameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                NameLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
                NameLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 230, 245)
                NameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                NameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
                NameLabel.ZIndex = 6

                -- Remove button (X)
                local RemoveBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", EntryFrame)
                RemoveBtn.Name = "RemoveBtn"
                RemoveBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 22 or 26, 0, isMobile and 22 or 26)
                RemoveBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 28 or 32), 0.5, -(isMobile and 11 or 13))
                RemoveBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 50, 50)
                RemoveBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.6
                RemoveBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
                RemoveBtn.Text = "X"
                RemoveBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                RemoveBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
                RemoveBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 120, 120)
                RemoveBtn.ZIndex = 7
                Instance.new("UICorner", RemoveBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

                RemoveBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    TweenService:Create(RemoveBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.2}):Play()
                end)
                RemoveBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    TweenService:Create(RemoveBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.6}):Play()
                end)

                RemoveBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    for i, entry in ipairs(_G.StolenItemsList) do
                        if entry.name == itemName and entry.time == stealTime then
                            table.remove(_G.StolenItemsList, i)
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    EntryFrame:Destroy()
                    if #_G.StolenItemsList == 0 and noItemsLabel then
                        noItemsLabel.Visible = true
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end

        -- Clear all button
        local clearAllBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", stealsPanel)
        clearAllBtn.Name = "ClearAllSteals"
        clearAllBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 28 or 32)
        clearAllBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 40, 40)
        clearAllBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
        clearAllBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        clearAllBtn.Text = "Clear All Steals"
        clearAllBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        clearAllBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        clearAllBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 180, 180)
        clearAllBtn.ZIndex = 4
        Instance.new("UICorner", clearAllBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        clearAllBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(clearAllBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.1}):Play()
        end)
        clearAllBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(clearAllBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.3}):Play()
        end)

        clearAllBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            _G.StolenItemsList = {}
            for _, child in ipairs(stealLogScroll:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Frame") and child.Name:find("StealEntry_") then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
            if noItemsLabel then noItemsLabel.Visible = true end
        end)

    end

-- ============================================================
-- PRIORITY PANEL v9
-- Modern clean UI, closer viewports, fixed priority TP
-- Replace entire "if contentPanels["Priority"] then" block
-- ============================================================

-- ============================================================
-- PRIORITY TP FIX
-- Runs every 0.05s, sets CurrentAutoStealTarget to whichever
-- priority animal is #1 in the list (top-down order) that is
-- currently present in debris and above its minimum value.
-- Falls back to highest value if none found.
-- ============================================================
local _priorityTPActive = false
local function startPriorityTPLoop()
    if _priorityTPActive then return end
    _priorityTPActive = true
    task.spawn(function()
        while _priorityTPActive do
            task.wait(0.05)
            if not (_G.STEAL_MODE == "Priority" or _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled or _G.BRAINROT_PRIORITY_ENABLED) then
                task.wait(0.5)
                continue
            end
            if _G.isTeleporting then continue end

            local pList = _G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS or {}
            local minThresh = (_G.TeleportMinimum or 0) * 1e6

            local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
            if not debrisFolder then continue end

            -- Find my own plot to skip
            local myPlotPos = nil
            local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if plotsFolder then
                local lp = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
                for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                    local ps = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                    if ps then
                        local sg = ps:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                        if sg then
                            local lbl = sg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                            if lbl and lbl.Text then
                                local t = lbl.Text:lower()
                                if t:find(lp.Name:lower(),1,true) or t:find(lp.DisplayName:lower(),1,true) then
                                    myPlotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            -- Scan debris, build a map: lowerName -> {part, genValue, position}
            local debrisMap = {}
            for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
                if not obj:IsA("BasePart") then continue end
                if myPlotPos then
                    local dx = obj.Position.X - myPlotPos.X
                    local dz = obj.Position.Z - myPlotPos.Z
                    if math.sqrt(dx*dx+dz*dz) < 50 then continue end
                end
                local displayName, genValue = nil, nil
                for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                        for _, lbl in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                            if lbl:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                if lbl.Name == "DisplayName" then
                                    displayName = lbl.Text
                                elseif lbl.Name == "Generation" and (lbl.Text or ""):find("/s") then
                                    local gt = lbl.Text:lower()
                                    local n = tonumber(gt:match("[%d%.]+")) or 0
                                    if gt:find("t") then n=n*1e12
                                    elseif gt:find("b") then n=n*1e9
                                    elseif gt:find("m") then n=n*1e6
                                    elseif gt:find("k") then n=n*1e3 end
                                    genValue = n
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if displayName and genValue and genValue >= minThresh then
                    local key = displayName:lower()
                    if not debrisMap[key] or genValue > debrisMap[key].genValue then
                        debrisMap[key] = {
                            part = obj,
                            name = displayName,
                            genValue = genValue,
                            value = genValue,
                            position = obj.Position - Vector3.new(0,11,0),
                        }
                    end
                end
            end

            -- Walk priority list TOP TO BOTTOM, pick first one that exists
            local target = nil
            if #pList > 0 then
                for _, animalName in ipairs(pList) do
                    local key = animalName:lower()
                    local entry = debrisMap[key]
                    if entry then
                        -- check per-animal minimum
                        local animalMin = (_G.PRIORITY_ANIMAL_MINIMUMS and
                            (_G.PRIORITY_ANIMAL_MINIMUMS[key] or 0) or 0) * 1e6
                        if entry.genValue >= animalMin then
                            target = entry
                            break -- #1 found, stop
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            -- Fallback: highest value in debris
            if not target then
                local bestVal = 0
                for _, entry in pairs(debrisMap) do
                    if entry.genValue > bestVal then
                        bestVal = entry.genValue
                        target = entry
                    end
                end
            end

            if target then
                -- Set every global the auto-steal system might read
                _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget = target
                _G.AutoStealTarget = target
                _G.SelectedStealTarget = nil
                _G.BestStealTarget = target
                -- If there's a setter function, call it too
                if type(_G.setStealTarget) == "function" then
                    pcall(_G.setStealTarget, target)
                end
                if type(_G.setBestTarget) == "function" then
                    pcall(_G.setBestTarget, target)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

task.spawn(function()
    task.wait(2)
    startPriorityTPLoop()
end)

-- Also re-start if called again (e.g. on toggle)
_G.__startPriorityTPLoop = startPriorityTPLoop

_G.PRIORITY_ANIMAL_MINIMUMS = _G.PRIORITY_ANIMAL_MINIMUMS or {}

-- ============================================================
-- VIEWPORT HELPERS
-- ============================================================
local modelsFolder, animsFolder
pcall(function()
    local rs = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    modelsFolder = rs:WaitForChild("Models",3):WaitForChild("Animals",3)
    animsFolder  = rs:WaitForChild("Animations",3):WaitForChild("Animals",3)
end)

local _mCache = {}
local function getClone(name)
    if not modelsFolder then return nil end
    if _mCache[name] then return _mCache[name]:Clone() end
    local m = modelsFolder:FindFirstChild(name)
    if not m then
        for _,c in ipairs(modelsFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if c.Name:lower()==name:lower() then m=c; break end
        end
    end
    if m then _mCache[name]=m; return m:Clone() end
    return nil
end

local function playIdle(clone, name)
    if not animsFolder then return end
    pcall(function()
        local af = animsFolder:FindFirstChild(name)
        if not af then
            for _,c in ipairs(animsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                if c.Name:lower()==name:lower() then af=c; break end
            end
        end
        if not af then return end
        local anim = af:FindFirstChild("Idle") or af:GetChildren()[1]
        if not anim then return end
        local ctrl = clone:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            or clone:FindFirstChildOfClass("AnimationController")
            or Instance.new("AnimationController",clone)
        local animator = ctrl:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
            or Instance.new("Animator",ctrl)
        animator:LoadAnimation(anim):Play(0)
    end)
end

-- VP_ZOOM: smaller = closer. 0.55 is a good close fill
local function makeVP(parent, name, zoom)
    zoom = zoom or 0.55
    local vp = Instance.new("ViewportFrame", parent)
    vp.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
    vp.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    vp.BorderSizePixel = 0
    vp.ZIndex = (parent.ZIndex or 5) + 1

    local wm = Instance.new("WorldModel", vp)
    local cam = Instance.new("Camera", vp)
    vp.CurrentCamera = cam

    task.spawn(function()
        local clone = getClone(name)
        if not clone then return end
        clone.Parent = wm

        -- Move model to origin first
        local pp = clone.PrimaryPart or clone:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
        if clone.PrimaryPart then
            clone:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(0, 0, 0))
        elseif pp then
            pp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
        end

        -- Get bounding box AFTER centering
        local cf, sz
        local ok = pcall(function() cf, sz = clone:GetBoundingBox() end)
        if not ok or not cf or not sz then
            if pp then cf = pp.CFrame; sz = pp.Size
            else return end
        end

        -- Re-center so bounding box center is at origin
        if clone.PrimaryPart then
            local offsetY = cf.Position.Y  -- vertical offset of bbox center
            clone:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(0, -offsetY, 0))
            -- Re-read after adjustment
            pcall(function() cf, sz = clone:GetBoundingBox() end)
        end

        local h  = sz and sz.Y or 3
        local w  = sz and math.max(sz.X, sz.Z) or 2
        local modelSize = math.max(h, w)
        local dist = modelSize * zoom
        local eyeY = 0  -- centered after offset correction above

        cam.FieldOfView = 65
        -- IMPORTANT: camera at NEGATIVE Z so it faces the FRONT of the model
        -- Roblox humanoids face -Z, so camera at -Z sees their face
        cam.CFrame = CFrame.new(
            Vector3.new(0, eyeY, -dist),
            Vector3.new(0, eyeY, 0)
        )

        playIdle(clone, name)
    end)
end

local nameInfo = {}
for _,t in ipairs(TIERS) do
    for _,a in ipairs(t.animals) do
        nameInfo[a.name:lower()] = {tier=t,value=a.value}
    end
end

local function fmtVal(v)
    if not v or v==0 then return "?" end
    if v>=1000 then return string.format("%.0fT/s",v/1000)
    elseif v>=1 then return string.format("$%.0fM/s",v)
    elseif v>=0.001 then return string.format("$%.1fK/s",v*1000)
    elseif v>=0.000001 then return string.format("$%.0f/s",v*1e6)
    else return "<$1/s" end
end

    if #_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS == 0 then
        for _,t in ipairs(TIERS) do
            if t.id=="OG" then

                    table.insert(_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS, a.name)
                end

        for _,v in ipairs(_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS) do
            if v:lower()==name:lower() then return true end
        end
        return false
    end
    local function removeFrom(name)
        for i,v in ipairs(_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS) do
            if v:lower()==name:lower() then table.remove(_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS,i); return end
        end

    srch.ZIndex = 4
    Instance.new("UICorner", srch).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,8)
    Instance.new("UIPadding", srch).PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0,10)

    for _, tier in ipairs(TIERS) do
        local ITEM_H = isMobile and 48 or 56
        local ITEM_VP = isMobile and 40 or 48

        -- header
        local hdr = Instance.new("TextButton", panel)
        hdr.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,isMobile and 34 or 38)
        hdr.BackgroundColor3 = tier.dimBg
        hdr.BackgroundTransparency = 0
        hdr.BorderSizePixel = 0
        hdr.Text = ""
        hdr.ZIndex = 4
        Instance.new("UICorner", hdr).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,9)

        -- stripe
        local hs = Instance.new("Frame", hdr)
        hs.Size = UDim2.new(0,4,1,-8)
        hs.Position = UDim2.new(0,5,0,4)
        hs.BackgroundColor3 = tier.color
        hs.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", hs).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,2)

        -- icon
        local hi = Instance.new("TextLabel", hdr)
        hi.Size = UDim2.new(0,isMobile and 18 or 20,1,0)
        hi.Position = UDim2.new(0,13,0,0)
        hi.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        hi.Text = tier.icon
        hi.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        hi.TextSize = isMobile and 12 or 14
        hi.TextColor3 = tier.color
        hi.ZIndex = 5

        -- name
        local hn = Instance.new("TextLabel", hdr)
        hn.Size = UDim2.new(0.52,0,1,0)
        hn.Position = UDim2.new(0,isMobile and 33 or 37,0,0)
        hn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        hn.Text = tier.label
        hn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        hn.TextSize = isMobile and 12 or 13
        hn.TextColor3 = tier.text
        hn.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        hn.ZIndex = 5

        -- count
        local hc = Instance.new("TextLabel", hdr)
        hc.Size = UDim2.new(0.26,0,1,0)
        hc.Position = UDim2.new(0.62,0,0,0)
        hc.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        hc.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        hc.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 10
        hc.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        hc.ZIndex = 5

        -- chevron
        local hch = Instance.new("TextLabel", hdr)
        hch.Size = UDim2.new(0,isMobile and 16 or 18,1,0)
        hch.Position = UDim2.new(1,-(isMobile and 17 or 19),0,0)
        hch.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        hch.Text = "›"
        hch.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        hch.TextSize = isMobile and 16 or 18
        hch.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,44,60)
        hch.ZIndex = 5

        -- content
        local cont = Instance.new("Frame", panel)
        cont.BackgroundColor3 = tier.dimBg
        cont.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
        cont.BorderSizePixel = 0
        cont.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)
        cont.Visible = false
        cont.ClipsDescendants = true
        cont.ZIndex = 4
        Instance.new("UICorner", cont).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,9)

        local cs = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", cont)
        cs.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
        cs.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        cs.BorderSizePixel = 0
        cs.ScrollBarThickness = 3
        cs.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24,28,40)
        cs.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
        cs.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        cs.ZIndex = 5

        local cl = Instance.new("UIListLayout", cs)
        cl.Padding = UDim.new(0,2)
        local cp = Instance.new("UIPadding", cs)
        cp.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0,4)
        cp.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0,4)
        cp.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0,4)
        cp.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0,4)

        tierContentFrames[tier.id] = cont
        local aRefs = {}

        local function upCount()
            local sel=0
            for _,a in ipairs(tier.animals) do if isIn(a.name) then sel=sel+1 end end
            hc.Text = sel.."/"..#tier.animals
            hc.TextColor3 = sel>0 and tier.text or Color3.fromRGB(34,38,52)
        end

        local function buildRows(q)
            for _,c in ipairs(cs:GetChildren()) do if c:IsA("Frame") then c:Destroy() end end
            aRefs = {}
            local vis = 0

            for _,a in ipairs(tier.animals) do
                if q and q~="" and not a.name:lower():find(q,1,true) then continue end
                vis = vis+1
                local inL = isIn(a.name)

                local ar = Instance.new("Frame", cs)
                ar.Size = UDim2.new(1,-2,0,ITEM_H)
                ar.BackgroundColor3 = inL and tier.dimBg or Color3.fromRGB(12,13,17)
                ar.BackgroundTransparency = inL and 0 or 0.55
                ar.BorderSizePixel = 0
                ar.ZIndex = 6
                Instance.new("UICorner", ar).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,7)

                -- selected indicator
                if inL then
                    local sb = Instance.new("Frame", ar)
                    sb.Size = UDim2.new(0,3,1,-8)
                    sb.Position = UDim2.new(0,3,0,4)
                    sb.BackgroundColor3 = tier.color
                    sb.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    Instance.new("UICorner", sb).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,1)
                end

                -- viewport (close 0.78)
                local vbox = Instance.new("Frame", ar)
                vbox.Size = UDim2.new(0,ITEM_VP,0,ITEM_VP)
                vbox.Position = UDim2.new(0,isMobile and 8 or 10,0.5,-(ITEM_VP/2))
                vbox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(8,9,12)
                vbox.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                vbox.BorderSizePixel = 0
                vbox.ZIndex = 7
                Instance.new("UICorner", vbox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,6)
                if inL then
                    local vs = Instance.new("UIStroke", vbox)
                    vs.Color = tier.color; vs.Thickness = 1.5; vs.Transparency = 0.2
                end
                makeVP(vbox, a.name, 0.78)

                -- checkbox
                local cbX = ITEM_VP+(isMobile and 13 or 15)
                local cb = Instance.new("Frame", ar)
                cb.Size = UDim2.new(0,isMobile and 13 or 15,0,isMobile and 13 or 15)
                cb.Position = UDim2.new(0,cbX,0.5,-(isMobile and 7 or 8))
                cb.BackgroundColor3 = inL and tier.color or Color3.fromRGB(22,24,32)
                cb.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                cb.BorderSizePixel = 0
                cb.ZIndex = 7
                Instance.new("UICorner", cb).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,4)

                local cbT = Instance.new("TextLabel", cb)
                cbT.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
                cbT.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                cbT.Text = inL and "✓" or ""
                cbT.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                cbT.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 9
                cbT.TextColor3 = tier.dimBg
                cbT.ZIndex = 8

                local lblX2 = cbX+(isMobile and 17 or 20)
                local al = Instance.new("TextLabel", ar)
                al.Size = UDim2.new(1,-(lblX2+4),1,0)
                al.Position = UDim2.new(0,lblX2,0,0)
                al.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                al.Text = a.name
                al.Font = inL and Enum.Font.GothamBold or Enum.Font.Gotham
                al.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 11
                al.TextColor3 = inL and tier.text or Color3.fromRGB(96,100,122)
                al.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                al.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
                al.ZIndex = 7

                aRefs[a.name] = {row=ar,cb=cb,tick=cbT,lbl=al}

                local clk = Instance.new("TextButton", ar)
                clk.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
                clk.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                clk.Text = ""
                clk.ZIndex = 9

                local capA = a
                clk.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    local r = aRefs[capA.name]
                    if not r then return end
                    if isIn(capA.name) then
                        removeFrom(capA.name)
                        r.row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(12,13,17)
                        r.row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.55
                        r.cb.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22,24,32)
                        r.tick.Text = ""
                        r.lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(96,100,122)
                        r.lbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                    else
                        table.insert(_G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS, capA.name)
                        r.row.BackgroundColor3 = tier.dimBg
                        r.row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                        r.cb.BackgroundColor3 = tier.color
                        r.tick.Text = "✓"
                        r.lbl.TextColor3 = tier.text
                        r.lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    end
                    upCount()
                    refreshOrder()
                end)
            end

            cont.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0, math.min(vis,5)*(ITEM_H+2)+10)
        end

        tierRebuildFns[tier.id] = function()
            buildRows(srch.Text:lower():match("^%s*(.-)%s*$"))
            upCount()
        end

        upCount()

        hdr.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if openTierId==tier.id then
                openTierId = nil
                cont.Visible = false
                cont.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)
                hch.Text = "›"; hch.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,44,60)
            else
                if openTierId and tierContentFrames[openTierId] then
                    tierContentFrames[openTierId].Visible = false
                    tierContentFrames[openTierId].Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)
                end
                openTierId = tier.id
                buildRows(srch.Text:lower():match("^%s*(.-)%s*$"))
                cont.Visible = true
                hch.Text = "˅"; hch.TextColor3 = tier.color
            end
        end)
    end

    srch:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
        if openTierId and tierRebuildFns[openTierId] then
            pcall(tierRebuildFns[openTierId])
        end
    end)

    refreshOrder()
end

    if contentPanels["ESP"] then
        local espPanel = contentPanels["ESP"]

        _G.createdxhubSection(espPanel, "PLAYER ESP")

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Player ESP", _G.playerESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.playerESPEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then
                task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updatePlayerESP) end)
            else
                _G.removeAllPlayerESP()
            end
            if _G.stealingESPEnabled then
                _G.removeAllStealingESP()
                task.spawn(function() task.wait(0.1) pcall(_G.updateStealingESP) end)
            end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Player ESP Color", _G.PlayerESPColor, function(color)
            _G.PlayerESPColor = color
            _G.updatePlayerESPColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Click to Admin (ESP)", _G.clickToAdminEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.clickToAdminEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then
                if not _G.playerESPEnabled then
                    _G.playerESPEnabled = true
                    task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updatePlayerESP) end)
                end
                task.spawn(startClickToAdmin)
            else
                stopClickToAdmin()
            end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Player Stealing ESP", _G.stealingESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.stealingESPEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateStealingESP) end)
            else _G.removeAllStealingESP() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Stealing ESP Color", _G.StealingESPColor, function(color)
            _G.StealingESPColor = color
            _G.updateStealingESPColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Player Stealing Chams", _G.stealingChamsEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.stealingChamsEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateStealingChams) end)
            else _G.removeAllStealingChams() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Stealing Chams Color", _G.StealingChamsColor, function(color)
            _G.StealingChamsColor = color
            _G.updateStealingChamsColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubSection(espPanel, "BRAINROT ESP")

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Brainrot ESP", _G.brainrotESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.brainrotESPEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateBrainrotESP) end)
            else _G.removeAllBrainrotESP() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubDropdown(espPanel, "Max Items Shown",
            {"5", "10", "15", "20", "25", "30", "50", "100"},
            tostring(_G.MaxBrainrotESPItems or 15),
            function(selected)
                _G.MaxBrainrotESPItems = tonumber(selected) or 15
                if _G.brainrotESPEnabled then
                    _G.removeAllBrainrotESP()
                    task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateBrainrotESP) end)
                end
                if _G.brainrotChamsEnabled then
                    _G.removeAllBrainrotChams()
                    task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateBrainrotChams) end)
                end
                if _G.traitESPEnabled then
                    _G.removeAllTraitESP()
                    task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateTraitESP) end)
                end
                if _G.mutationESPEnabled then
                    _G.removeAllMutationESP()
                    task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateMutationESP) end)
                end
            end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Brainrot ESP Color", _G.BrainrotESPColor, function(color)
            _G.BrainrotESPColor = color
            _G.updateBrainrotESPColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Brainrot Chams", _G.brainrotChamsEnabled or false, function(enabled)
            _G.brainrotChamsEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateBrainrotChams) end)
            else pcall(_G.removeAllBrainrotChams) end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Brainrot Chams Color", _G.BrainrotChamsColor, function(color)
            _G.BrainrotChamsColor = color
            pcall(_G.updateBrainrotChamsColors)
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Trait ESP", _G.traitESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.traitESPEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateTraitESP) end)
            else _G.removeAllTraitESP() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Trait ESP Color", _G.TraitESPColor, function(color)
            _G.TraitESPColor = color
            _G.updateTraitESPColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Mutation ESP", _G.mutationESPEnabled or false, function(enabled)
            _G.mutationESPEnabled = enabled
            if enabled then task.spawn(function() pcall(_G.updateMutationESP) end)
            else pcall(_G.removeAllMutationESP) end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Mutation ESP Color", _G.MutationESPColor, function(color)
            _G.MutationESPColor = color
            pcall(_G.updateMutationESPColors)
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Line To Highest", _G.brainrotBeamEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.brainrotBeamEnabled = enabled
            if not enabled then _G.resetBrainrotBeam() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Line To Highest Color", _G.LineToHighestColor, function(color)
            _G.LineToHighestColor = color
            _G.updateLineToHighestColor()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubSection(espPanel, "ENVIRONMENT")

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Base Timer ESP", _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.PlotTimerESPEnabled = enabled
            if not enabled then _G.removePlotTimerESP() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Base Timer Color", _G.BaseTimerESPColor, function(color)
            _G.BaseTimerESPColor = color
            _G.updateBaseTimerColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Mines ESP", _G.MineESPEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.MineESPEnabled = enabled
            if not enabled then _G.removeAllMineESP() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Mines ESP Color", _G.MinesESPColor, function(color)
            _G.MinesESPColor = color
            _G.updateMinesColors()
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(espPanel, "Line To Base", _G.rainbowBeamEnabled, function(enabled)
            _G.rainbowBeamEnabled = enabled
            if not enabled then _G.resetPlotBeam() else _G.createPlotBeam() end
        end)

        _G.createdxhubColorPicker(espPanel, "Line To Base Color", _G.LineToBaseColor, function(color)
            _G.LineToBaseColor = color
            _G.updateLineToBaseColor()
        end)



        local SliderContainer = Instance.new("Frame", espPanel)
        SliderContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 50 or 58)
        SliderContainer.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
        SliderContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        SliderContainer.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SliderContainer.ZIndex = 4
        Instance.new("UICorner", SliderContainer).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        local SliderLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", SliderContainer)
        SliderLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, isMobile and 20 or 24)
        SliderLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 4)
        SliderLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SliderLabel.Text = "Clear Base Transparency"
        SliderLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        SliderLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        SliderLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
        SliderLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        SliderLabel.ZIndex = 5

        local SliderValue = Instance.new("TextLabel", SliderContainer)
        SliderValue.Size = UDim2.new(0, 50, 0, isMobile and 20 or 24)
        SliderValue.Position = UDim2.new(1, -58, 0, 4)
        SliderValue.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SliderValue.Text = tostring(math.floor(_G.ClearBaseTransparency * 100)) .. "%"
        SliderValue.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        SliderValue.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
        SliderValue.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 215)
        SliderValue.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        SliderValue.ZIndex = 5

        local SliderTrack = Instance.new("Frame", SliderContainer)
        SliderTrack.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, isMobile and 4 or 5)
        SliderTrack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 1, -(isMobile and 16 or 18))
        SliderTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 42, 48)
        SliderTrack.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SliderTrack.ZIndex = 5
        Instance.new("UICorner", SliderTrack).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local SliderFill = Instance.new("Frame", SliderTrack)
        SliderFill.Size = UDim2.new(_G.ClearBaseTransparency, 0, 1, 0)
        SliderFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        SliderFill.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SliderFill.ZIndex = 6
        Instance.new("UICorner", SliderFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local SliderKnob = Instance.new("Frame", SliderTrack)
        SliderKnob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 10 or 12, 0, isMobile and 10 or 12)
        SliderKnob.Position = UDim2.new(_G.ClearBaseTransparency, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
        SliderKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        SliderKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        SliderKnob.ZIndex = 7
        Instance.new("UICorner", SliderKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)


        local sliderDragging = false
        local lastSliderUpdate = 0
        local sliderUpdatePending = false

        local function updateSlider(inputPos)
            local trackAbsPos = SliderTrack.AbsolutePosition
            local trackAbsSize = SliderTrack.AbsoluteSize
            local relativeX = math.clamp((inputPos.X - trackAbsPos.X) / trackAbsSize.X, 0, 1)
            _G.ClearBaseTransparency = relativeX
            SliderFill.Size = UDim2.new(relativeX, 0, 1, 0)
            SliderKnob.Position = UDim2.new(relativeX, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
            SliderValue.Text = tostring(math.floor(relativeX * 100)) .. "%"

            if _G.plotTransparencyEnabled then
                local now = tick()
                if now - lastSliderUpdate > 0.2 then
                    lastSliderUpdate = now
                    task.spawn(function() _G.updateClearBaseTransparency() end)
                elseif not sliderUpdatePending then
                    sliderUpdatePending = true
                    task.delay(0.2, function()
                        sliderUpdatePending = false
                        if _G.plotTransparencyEnabled then
                            _G.updateClearBaseTransparency()
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end

        local SliderButton = Instance.new("TextButton", SliderTrack)
        SliderButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 20)
        SliderButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -10)
        SliderButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        SliderButton.Text = ""
        SliderButton.ZIndex = 8

        SliderButton.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                sliderDragging = true
                updateSlider(input.Position)
            end
        end)
        SliderButton.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                sliderDragging = false
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if sliderDragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                updateSlider(input.Position)
            end
        end)
    end

        local miscPanel = contentPanels["Misc"]

        _G.createdxhubSection(miscPanel, "PANELS")

        _G.createdxhubToggle(miscPanel, "Proximity Panel", _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES and _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.Proximity or false, function(enabled)
            if ProximityPanel then
                ProximityPanel.Visible = enabled

            _G.dxhub_PANELS = _G.dxhub_PANELS or {}
            _G.dxhub_PANELS.Proximity = enabled
            _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.Proximity = enabled

        _G.createdxhubToggle(miscPanel, "Player Controls Panel", _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES and _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.PlayerControls or false, function(enabled)
            if PlayerControlsPanel then

            end
            _G.dxhub_PANELS = _G.dxhub_PANELS or {}

            _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.PlayerControls = enabled
        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(miscPanel, "Admin Panel", _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES and _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.Admin or false, function(enabled)
            if AdminPanel then

                                    -- Direct substring match, no quotes needed

        local function autoSaveConfig()
            if not writefile then return end
            pcall(function()
                local config = {}
                for _, key in ipairs(CONFIG_KEYS) do
                    local value = _G[key]
                    if value ~= nil then
                        if typeof(value) == "Color3" then
                            config[key] = {r = value.R, g = value.G, b = value.B, type = "Color3"}
                        elseif typeof(value) == "EnumItem" then
                            config[key] = {name = value.Name, type = "KeyCode"}
                        elseif typeof(value) == "table" then
                            config[key] = {data = value, type = "table"}
                        else
                            config[key] = value
                        end
                    end
                end
                writefile(CONFIG_FILE, game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONEncode(config))
            end)
        end

        local function autoSavePositions()
            if not writefile then return end
            pcall(function()
                local positions = {}
                local gui = nil
                pcall(function()
                    gui = cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")):FindFirstChild("22SHubGui")
                end)
                if not gui then gui = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("22SHubGui") end
                if not gui then gui = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("22SHub") end
                if gui then
                    local panels = {"AdminPanel", "CooldownPanel", "AutoStealPanel", "MovementPanel", "PlayerControlsPanel", "ProximityPanel", "BaseHubPanel", "TargetPanel", "QuickPanel"}
                    for _, name in ipairs(panels) do
                        local panel = gui:FindFirstChild(name, true)
                        if panel and panel:IsA("Frame") then
                            positions[name] = {
                                XScale = panel.Position.X.Scale,
                                XOffset = panel.Position.X.Offset,
                                YScale = panel.Position.Y.Scale,
                                YOffset = panel.Position.Y.Offset
                            }
                        end
                    end
                end
                if next(positions) then
                    writefile(POSITIONS_FILE, HttpService:JSONEncode(positions))
                end
            end)
        end

        local function autoLoadConfig()
            if not readfile or not isfile then return end
            pcall(function()
                if isfile(CONFIG_FILE) then
                    local jsonStr = readfile(CONFIG_FILE)
                    local config = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(jsonStr)
                    for key, value in pairs(config) do
                        if type(value) == "table" then
                            if value.type == "Color3" then
                                _G[key] = Color3.new(value.r, value.g, value.b)
                            elseif value.type == "KeyCode" then
                                _G[key] = Enum.KeyCode[value.name]
                            elseif value.type == "table" then
                                _G[key] = value.data
                            end
                        else
                            _G[key] = value
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end

        local function autoLoadPositions()
            if not readfile or not isfile then return end
            pcall(function()
                if isfile(POSITIONS_FILE) then
                    local jsonStr = readfile(POSITIONS_FILE)
                    _G.SAVED_UI_POSITIONS = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(jsonStr)
                end
            end)
        end

        autoLoadPositions()

        _G.autoSavePositions = autoSavePositions

            while task.wait(30) do
                pcall(autoSavePositions)
            end
        end)

        local function serializeConfig()
            local config = {}
            for _, key in ipairs(CONFIG_KEYS) do
                local value = _G[key]
                if value ~= nil then
                    if typeof(value) == "Color3" then
                        config[key] = {r = value.R, g = value.G, b = value.B, type = "Color3"}
                    elseif typeof(value) == "EnumItem" then
                        config[key] = {name = value.Name, type = "KeyCode"}
                    elseif type(value) == "table" then
                        config[key] = {data = value, type = "table"}
                    else
                        config[key] = value
                    end
                end
            end
            local success, json = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONEncode(config) end)
            return success and json or nil
        end

        local function deserializeConfig(jsonStr)
            local success, config = pcall(function()
                return HttpService:JSONDecode(jsonStr)
            end)
            if not success or type(config) ~= "table" then 
                return false, "Invalid JSON data" 
            end
            for key, value in pairs(config) do
                if type(value) == "table" then
                    if value.type == "Color3" then
                        _G[key] = Color3.new(value.r, value.g, value.b)
                    elseif value.type == "KeyCode" then
                        pcall(function() _G[key] = Enum.KeyCode[value.name] end)
                    elseif value.type == "table" then
                        _G[key] = value.data
                    else
                        _G[key] = value
                    end
                else
                    _G[key] = value
                end
            end
            if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
            return true, "Success"
        end

                ExportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
                return
            end
            -- Removed "22S_V1_" prefix
            local encoded = base64encode(configJson)
            ExportBox.Text = encoded
            ExportBox:CaptureFocus()
            task.wait(0.05)
            ExportBox.SelectionStart = 1
            ExportBox.CursorPosition = #encoded + 1

            -- Copy to clipboard
            local clipboardFuncs = {setclipboard, toclipboard, set_clipboard, Clipboard and Clipboard.set, syn and syn.write_clipboard, fluxus and fluxus.write_clipboard, writeclipboard}
            local copied = false
            for _, func in ipairs(clipboardFuncs) do
                if func then
                    local success = pcall(function() func(encoded) end)
                    if success then copied = true break end
                end
            end

            if copied then
                ExportLabel.Text = "Copied to clipboard!"
                ExportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            else
                ExportLabel.Text = "Generated! Select & copy manually"
                ExportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100)
            end
            task.delay(3, function()
                ExportLabel.Text = "Your Config Code:"
                ExportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
            end)
        end)

                task.delay(2, function() ImportLabel.Text = "Import Config:" ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220) end)
                return
            end

            local success, decoded = pcall(function() return base64decode(configCode) end)
            if not success then
                ImportLabel.Text = "Invalid Base64"
                ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
                task.delay(3, function() ImportLabel.Text = "Import Config:" ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220) end)
                return
            end

            local loadSuccess, msg = deserializeConfig(decoded)
            if loadSuccess then
                ImportBox.Text = ""
                ImportLabel.Text = "Config loaded!"
                ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            else
                ImportLabel.Text = "Failed: " .. (msg or "Unknown error")
                ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
            end
            task.delay(3, function()
                ImportLabel.Text = "Import Config:"
                ImportLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
            end)
        end)

        ColorPickerPopup.BorderSizePixel = 0
        ColorPickerPopup.Visible = false

        ColorGrid.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, isMobile and 36 or 42)

        for i, color in ipairs(colorPalette) do
            local ColorOption = Instance.new("TextButton", ColorGrid)
            ColorOption.BackgroundColor3 = color
            ColorOption.BorderSizePixel = 0
            ColorOption.Text = ""
            ColorOption.ZIndex = 3002
            ColorOption.LayoutOrder = i

            Instance.new("UICorner", ColorOption).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)


            ColorOption.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            end)

            ColorOption.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            end)

            ColorOption.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                ColorPreview.BackgroundColor3 = color
                ColorPickerPopup.Visible = false

                for _, descendant in pairs(dxhubGui:GetDescendants()) do
                    if descendant:IsA("UIStroke") then
                        pcall(function()
                            if descendant.Thickness >= 1.5 or descendant.Parent.Name:find("Panel") or descendant.Parent.Name:find("Frame") then
                                descendant.Color = color
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                end

                local panelsToUpdate = {
                    "AdminPanel", "CooldownPanel", "AutoStealPanel", "MovementPanel",
                    "PlayerControlsPanel", "ProximityPanel", "KeybindsActivePanel",
                    "MainFrame", "Bar", "BaseHubPanel"
                }

                for _, panelName in ipairs(panelsToUpdate) do
                    pcall(function()
                        local panel = dxhubGui:FindFirstChild(panelName, true)
                        if panel then
                            local stroke = panel:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
                            if stroke then
                                stroke.Color = color
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end

                pcall(function()
                end)

                pcall(function()
                    if _G.BAR_BORDER_GLOW then
                        _G.BAR_BORDER_GLOW.Color = color
                    end
                end)

                pcall(function()
                    if _G.BASE_HUB_BUTTON_GLOWS then
                        for _, buttonGlow in ipairs(_G.BASE_HUB_BUTTON_GLOWS) do
                            buttonGlow.Color = color
                        end
                    end
                end)

                _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR = color
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.SWITCH_TRACKS then
                        for _, switchData in ipairs(_G.SWITCH_TRACKS) do
                            if switchData.getState() then
                                TweenService:Create(switchData.track, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
                                    BackgroundColor3 = color
                                }):Play()
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)

                pcall(function()
                    if _G.STEAL_MODE_TOGGLES and _G.STEAL_MODE then
                        local activeToggle = _G.STEAL_MODE_TOGGLES[_G.STEAL_MODE]
                        if activeToggle then
                            TweenService:Create(activeToggle.track, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
                                BackgroundColor3 = color
                            }):Play()
                        end
                    end
                end)

            end)
        end

        ColorButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            ColorPickerPopup.Visible = not ColorPickerPopup.Visible
        end)

        _G.UI_LOCKED = _G.UI_LOCKED or false

        _G.createdxhubToggle(configPanel, "Lock All UIs", _G.UI_LOCKED, function(enabled)
            _G.UI_LOCKED = enabled

            local panelNames = {
                "AdminPanel", "CooldownPanel", "AutoStealPanel", "MovementPanel",
                "PlayerControlsPanel", "ProximityPanel", "KeybindsActivePanel",
                "BaseHubPanel", "MainFrame", "Bar"
            }

            for _, child in ipairs(dxhubGui:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Frame") then
                    local header = child:FindFirstChild("Header") or child:FindFirstChildOfClass("Frame")
                    if header then
                        header.Active = not enabled
                    end
                    child.Active = not enabled
                end
            end

            _G.DRAG_DISABLED = enabled

        end)

        _G.createdxhubToggle(configPanel, "Close UI on load", _G.AutoCloseGUI, function(enabled)
            _G.AutoCloseGUI = enabled
        end)
    end
