        speedLevelKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        speedLevelKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", speedLevelKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local speedLevelDragging = false
        speedLevelKnob.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                speedLevelDragging = true
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                speedLevelDragging = false
            end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if speedLevelDragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
                local trackAbsPos = speedLevelTrack.AbsolutePosition.X
                local trackAbsSize = speedLevelTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
                local relX = math.clamp((input.Position.X - trackAbsPos) / trackAbsSize, 0, 1)
                local newVal = math.clamp(math.floor(relX * 4 + 0.5), 0, 4)
                _G.TeleportSpeedLevel = newVal
                speedLevelLabel.Text = "Speed Level: " .. tostring(newVal)
                local pct = newVal / 4
                speedLevelFill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
                speedLevelKnob.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -5, 0.5, -5)
                if _G.savedBinds then _G.savedBinds.TeleportSpeedLevel = newVal end
                if _G.saveKeybinds then task.defer(pcall, _G.saveKeybinds) end
            end
        end)

            riseFirstInput.Text = tostring(tpDefaults.TPRisePowerFloor1)

                _G.savedBinds.TeleportMinimum = tpDefaults.TeleportMinimum

    local dragging = false
    local dragInput, dragStart, startPos

    local function update(input)
        local delta = input.Position - dragStart
        MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(
            startPos.X.Scale,
            startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
            startPos.Y.Scale,
            startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
        )
    end

    HeaderBar.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if _G.DRAG_DISABLED then return end -- Check if dragging is locked
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            dragStart = input.Position
            startPos = MainFrame.Position

            input.Changed:Connect(function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    dragging = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end)

    HeaderBar.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragInput = input
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input == dragInput and dragging then
            update(input)
        end
    end)

    _G.dxhub_GUI_TOGGLE_KEY = _G.OpenGUIKey or _G.dxhub_GUI_TOGGLE_KEY or Enum.KeyCode.RightControl

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        if input.KeyCode == _G.dxhub_GUI_TOGGLE_KEY then
            MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
        end
    end)

    local playerEntryCache = {}
    local lastPositionUpdate = 0

    local function getStealingItemName(player)
        local stealingAnimalName = nil
        pcall(function()
            local char = player.Character
            if char then
                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    local playerPos = hrp.Position
                    local closestDist = 20
                    for _, obj in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if obj:IsA("TextLabel") and obj.Name == "Generation" then
                            local animalModel = obj:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
                            if animalModel then
                                local animalPos = nil
                                local billboard = obj:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("BillboardGui")
                                if billboard and billboard.Adornee then
                                    if billboard.Adornee:IsA("Attachment") then
                                        animalPos = billboard.Adornee.WorldPosition
                                    elseif billboard.Adornee:IsA("BasePart") then
                                        animalPos = billboard.Adornee.Position
                                    end
                                end
                                if not animalPos and animalModel.PrimaryPart then
                                    animalPos = animalModel.PrimaryPart.Position
                                elseif not animalPos then
                                    local part = animalModel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                                    if part then animalPos = part.Position end
                                end
                                if animalPos then
                                    local dist = (animalPos - playerPos).Magnitude
                                    if dist < closestDist then
                                        closestDist = dist
                                        stealingAnimalName = animalModel.Name
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        return stealingAnimalName
    end

    local function isBaseOwner(player)
        local isOwner = false
        pcall(function()
            local char = player.Character
            if not char then return end
            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end

            local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not plotsFolder then return end

            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local dist = (plotSign.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
                    if dist < 100 then -- Within plot range
                        local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                        if surfaceGui then
                            for _, desc in ipairs(surfaceGui:GetDescendants()) do
                                if desc:IsA("TextLabel") and desc.Text == player.Name then
                                    isOwner = true
                                    return
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        return isOwner
    end

    local function createPlayerEntry(player, isStealing, itemName, isOwner)
        local entryHeight = isMobile and 50 or 60
        if isStealing then
            entryHeight = isMobile and 72 or 84
        elseif isOwner then
            entryHeight = isMobile and 58 or 68
        end

        local Entry = Instance.new("Frame")
        Entry.Name = "Entry_" .. player.UserId
        Entry.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, entryHeight)
        Entry.BackgroundColor3 = isStealing and Color3.fromRGB(18, 12, 12) or Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
        Entry.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
        Entry.BorderSizePixel = 0

        Instance.new("UICorner", Entry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        -- Stealing glow border
        if isStealing then
            local stealStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", Entry)
            stealStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 60, 60)
            stealStroke.Thickness = 1.5
            stealStroke.Transparency = 0.3
        end

        local Avatar = Instance.new("ImageLabel", Entry)
        Avatar.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 34 or 42, 0, isMobile and 34 or 42)
        Avatar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6)
        Avatar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)
        Avatar.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Avatar.Image = "rbxthumb://type=AvatarHeadShot&id=" .. player.UserId .. "&w=150&h=150"
        Instance.new("UICorner", Avatar).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        -- Avatar ring for stealing
        if isStealing then
            local avatarStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", Avatar)
            avatarStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            avatarStroke.Thickness = 2
            avatarStroke.Transparency = 0.1
        elseif isOwner then
            local avatarStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", Avatar)
            avatarStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 50)
            avatarStroke.Thickness = 1.5
            avatarStroke.Transparency = 0.3
        end

        local textX = isMobile and 44 or 54

        local Username = Instance.new("TextLabel", Entry)
        Username.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(textX + 4), 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)
        Username.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, 6)
        Username.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Username.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Username.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
        Username.TextColor3 = isStealing and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or (isOwner and Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 80) or Color3.fromRGB(220, 225, 240))
        Username.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Username.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        Username.Text = player.Name

        -- Status badge
        if isStealing then
            local stealBadge = Instance.new("Frame", Entry)
            stealBadge.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(textX + 8), 0, isMobile and 18 or 22)
            stealBadge.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, isMobile and 22 or 26)
            stealBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 15, 15)
            stealBadge.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
            stealBadge.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", stealBadge).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)

            local stealIcon = Instance.new("TextLabel", stealBadge)
            stealIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 14 or 18, 1, 0)
            stealIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 0)
            stealIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            stealIcon.Text = "🚨"
            stealIcon.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            stealIcon.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11

            local stealText = Instance.new("TextLabel", stealBadge)
            stealText.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 20 or 24), 1, 0)
            stealText.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 18 or 22, 0, 0)
            stealText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            stealText.Text = "STEALING — " .. (itemName or "Unknown")
            stealText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            stealText.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 10
            stealText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
            stealText.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            stealText.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        elseif isOwner then
            local ownerBadge = Instance.new("Frame", Entry)
            ownerBadge.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 80 or 95, 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)
            ownerBadge.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, isMobile and 22 or 26)
            ownerBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 40, 10)
            ownerBadge.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
            ownerBadge.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", ownerBadge).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

            local ownerText = Instance.new("TextLabel", ownerBadge)
            ownerText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            ownerText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            ownerText.Text = "👑 Base Owner"
            ownerText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            ownerText.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 9
            ownerText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 80)
        end

        -- Command buttons
        local btnY = isStealing and (isMobile and 46 or 54) or (isOwner and (isMobile and 40 or 46) or (isMobile and 24 or 30))

        local ButtonContainer = Instance.new("Frame", Entry)
        ButtonContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(textX + 8), 0, isMobile and 18 or 22)
        ButtonContainer.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, btnY)
        ButtonContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        local ButtonLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", ButtonContainer)
        ButtonLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
        ButtonLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 3)

        local commands = {
            {label = "💀", cmd = "ragdoll", tip = "Ragdoll"},
            {label = "🚀", cmd = "rocket", tip = "Rocket"},
            {label = "🔒", cmd = "jail", tip = "Jail"},
            {label = "🎈", cmd = "balloon", tip = "Balloon"},
            {label = "🔄", cmd = "inverse", tip = "Inverse"},
            {label = "🐜", cmd = "tiny", tip = "Tiny"},
            {label = "👻", cmd = "morph", tip = "Morph"},
        }

        for _, cmd in ipairs(commands) do
            local CmdBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", ButtonContainer)
            CmdBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 22 or 26, 1, 0)
            CmdBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)
            CmdBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
            CmdBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
            CmdBtn.Text = cmd.label
            CmdBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            CmdBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
            CmdBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 215)

            Instance.new("UICorner", CmdBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            CmdBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(CmdBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0, BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 48, 58)}):Play()
            end)
            CmdBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(CmdBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.2, BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)}):Play()
            end)

            CmdBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                task.spawn(function()
                    if _G.setCommandCooldown then _G.setCommandCooldown(cmd.cmd) end
                    executeAdmin(player, cmd.cmd)
                end)
            end)
        end

        -- Admin All button (click whole entry)
        local HoverBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", Entry)
        HoverBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        HoverBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        HoverBtn.Text = ""
        HoverBtn.ZIndex = 0

        HoverBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(Entry, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
        end)
        HoverBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            TweenService:Create(Entry, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.1}):Play()
        end)

        HoverBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            task.spawn(function()
                local adminCommands = {"ragdoll", "rocket", "jail", "balloon", "inverse", "tiny", "morph"}
                for _, cmd in ipairs(adminCommands) do
                    task.spawn(function()
                        if _G.setCommandCooldown then _G.setCommandCooldown(cmd) end
                        executeAdmin(player, cmd)
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.15)
                end
                pcall(function()
                    game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                        Title = "Admin Spam",
                        Text = "You've Admined \"" .. player.Name .. "\" Successfully",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end)
            end)
        end)

        return Entry
    end

    local function updatePlayerList(forcePositionUpdate)
        if not AdminPanel.Visible then return end

        local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
        local localPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        local currentTime = tick()

        local shouldUpdatePositions = forcePositionUpdate or (currentTime - lastPositionUpdate >= 10)
        if shouldUpdatePositions then
            lastPositionUpdate = currentTime
        end

        local localHRP = nil
        if localPlayer.Character then
            localHRP = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        end

        local playerData = {}
        for _, player in ipairs(players) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local isStealing = player:GetAttribute("Stealing") or false
                local itemName = nil
                local isOwner = false

                if isStealing then
                    itemName = getStealingItemName(player)
                else
                    isOwner = isBaseOwner(player)
                end

                local distance = math.huge
                if localHRP and player.Character then
                    local pHRP = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if pHRP then
                        distance = (pHRP.Position - localHRP.Position).Magnitude
                    end
                end

                table.insert(playerData, {
                    player = player,
                    isStealing = isStealing,
                    itemName = itemName,
                    isOwner = isOwner,
                    distance = distance
                })
            end
        end

        table.sort(playerData, function(a, b)
            return a.distance < b.distance
        end)

        local existingEntries = {}
        for _, child in ipairs(PlayerList:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Frame") then
                existingEntries[child.Name] = child
            end
        end

        for i, data in ipairs(playerData) do
            local entryName = "Entry_" .. data.player.UserId
            local existingEntry = existingEntries[entryName]

            if existingEntry then
                existingEntry:Destroy()
            end

            local entry = createPlayerEntry(data.player, data.isStealing, data.itemName, data.isOwner)
            entry.LayoutOrder = i
            entry.Parent = PlayerList

            existingEntries[entryName] = nil -- Mark as processed
        end

        for name, entry in pairs(existingEntries) do
            entry:Destroy()
        end
    end

    local isHoveringAdminPanel = false

    AdminPanel.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        isHoveringAdminPanel = true
    end)

    AdminPanel.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        isHoveringAdminPanel = false
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        while _loopFlags.running do
            task.wait(0.5)
            if AdminPanel.Visible and not isHoveringAdminPanel then
                pcall(updatePlayerList)
            end
        end
    end)

    AdminPanel:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Visible"):Connect(function()
        if AdminPanel.Visible then
            task.spawn(function()
                updatePlayerList(true) -- Force position update on open
            end)
        end
    end)

    local function syncToggleOff(panelName)
        if contentPanels["Misc"] then
            task.spawn(function()
                task.wait(0.1)
                for _, child in ipairs(contentPanels["Misc"]:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("Frame") and child:FindFirstChild("TextLabel") then
                        local label = child:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                        if label.Text == panelName then
                            for _, descendant in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                                if descendant:IsA("Frame") and descendant.Parent:IsA("Frame") and descendant.Size == UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 36 or 42, 0, isMobile and 18 or 22) then
                                    local toggleBG = descendant
                                    local circle = toggleBG:FindFirstChildOfClass("Frame")
                                    if circle then
                                        TweenService:Create(toggleBG, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 75)}):Play()
                                        TweenService:Create(circle, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
                                            Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9)),
                                            BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 160, 170)
                                        }):Play()
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local commandExecutionTimes = {
        ragdoll = 30,
        inverse = 60,
        jail = 60,
        tiny = 60,
        morph = 60,
        rocket = 120,
        jumpscare = 60,
        balloon = 30,

    _G.commandCooldowns = _G.commandCooldowns or {}

    local function commandOnCooldown(cmd)
        return _G.commandCooldowns[cmd] and tick() < _G.commandCooldowns[cmd]
    end
    _G.commandOnCooldown = commandOnCooldown

    local function setCommandCooldown(cmd)
        local execTime = commandExecutionTimes[cmd:lower()] or 30
        _G.commandCooldowns[cmd:lower()] = tick() + execTime
    end
    _G.setCommandCooldown = setCommandCooldown

                    data.entry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)

    local stealModeToggles = {}
    _G.STEAL_MODE_TOGGLES = stealModeToggles

    local function createStealModeEntry(parent, label, mode)
        local entry = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        entry.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 30 or 36)
        entry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        entry.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
        entry.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", entry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", entry)
        lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
        lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1; lbl.Text = label
        lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lbl.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
        lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220); lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        local isActive = _G.STEAL_MODE == mode and _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled

        local track = Instance.new("Frame", entry)
        track.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 32 or 38, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
        track.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 38 or 44), 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9))
        track.BackgroundColor3 = isActive and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)
        track.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local knob = Instance.new("Frame", track)
        knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 8 or 10, 0, isMobile and 8 or 10)
        knob.Position = isActive and UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 10 or 12), 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5))
        knob.BackgroundColor3 = isActive and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)
        knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", knob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        stealModeToggles[mode] = {track = track, knob = knob, active = isActive, entry = entry}

        entry.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                local cur = stealModeToggles[mode]
                if cur.active then
                    TweenService:Create(cur.knob, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(cur.track, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)}):Play()
                    cur.active = false; _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled = false; _G.STEAL_MODE = nil
                    -- Sync teleport type
                    _G.AutoStealHighestEnabled = false
                    _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = false
                    _G.AutoStealNearestEnabled = false
                else
                    for m, t in pairs(stealModeToggles) do
                        if m ~= mode then
                            TweenService:Create(t.knob, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)}):Play()
                            TweenService:Create(t.track, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)}):Play()
                            t.active = false
                        end
                    end
                    TweenService:Create(cur.knob, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 10 or 12), 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(cur.track, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
                    cur.active = true; _G.STEAL_MODE = mode; _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled = true
                    -- Sync teleport type based on steal mode
                    _G.AutoStealHighestEnabled = (mode == "Highest")
                    _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = (mode == "Priority")
                    _G.AutoStealNearestEnabled = (mode == "Nearest")
                    if mode == "Priority" then
                        _G.TeleportType = "Priority Config"
                    else
                        _G.TeleportType = "Highest Value"
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        return entry
    end

    createStealModeEntry(ASContent, "Steal Highest", "Highest")
    createStealModeEntry(ASContent, "Steal Priority", "Priority")
    createStealModeEntry(ASContent, "Steal Nearest", "Nearest")

        optBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()

                _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled = false

            if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
        end)
    end

        tpOptFrame.Visible = not tpOptFrame.Visible

            tpDropContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, (isMobile and 56 or 66) + #tpOptions * (isMobile and 24 or 28))

        end
    end)
    MvHeader.InputChanged:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then mvDragIn = input end end)
    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input == mvDragIn and mvDrag then local d = input.Position - mvDragSt; MovementPanel.Position = UDim2.new(mvStPos.X.Scale, mvStPos.X.Offset + d.X, mvStPos.Y.Scale, mvStPos.Y.Offset + d.Y) end
    end)

    local function createBlackSectionHeader(parent, text)

    local function createBlackToggle(parent, label, globalVar, callback)
        local entry = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        entry.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 30 or 36)
        entry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0); entry.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5; entry.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", entry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", entry)
        lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
        lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1; lbl.Text = label
        lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lbl.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
        lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220); lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        local track = Instance.new("Frame", entry)
        track.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 32 or 38, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
        track.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 38 or 44), 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9))
        track.BackgroundColor3 = _G[globalVar] and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)
        track.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local knob = Instance.new("Frame", track)
        knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 8 or 10, 0, isMobile and 8 or 10)
        knob.Position = _G[globalVar] and UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 10 or 12), 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5))
        knob.BackgroundColor3 = _G[globalVar] and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)
        knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", knob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local function updateVisual(enabled)
            if enabled then
                TweenService:Create(knob, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 10 or 12), 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(track, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
            else
                TweenService:Create(knob, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)), BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(track, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)}):Play()
            end
        end

        entry.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                _G[globalVar] = not _G[globalVar]; updateVisual(_G[globalVar])
                if callback then callback(_G[globalVar]) end
            end
        end)
        return entry, updateVisual
    end

    local function createBlackSlider(parent, label, globalVar, minVal, maxVal, callback, showLock, step)
        step = step or 1
        local entry = Instance.new("Frame", parent)
        entry.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 42 or 50)
        entry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0); entry.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5; entry.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", entry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local currentVal = _G[globalVar] or minVal
        local fmt = step < 1 and "%.1f" or "%d"

        local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", entry)
        lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, showLock and -50 or -10, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
        lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 2); lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        lbl.Text = label .. ": " .. string.format(fmt, currentVal)
        lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lbl.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
        lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220); lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

        if showLock then
            local lockBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", entry)
            lockBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 20 or 24, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
            lockBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 28 or 32), 0, 2)
            lockBtn.BackgroundColor3 = _G.DepthLocked and Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100) or Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 75)
            lockBtn.Text = "L"; lockBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold; lockBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 10
            lockBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255); lockBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", lockBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            lockBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                _G.DepthLocked = not _G.DepthLocked
                lockBtn.BackgroundColor3 = _G.DepthLocked and Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100) or Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 75)
            end)
        end

        local sTrack = Instance.new("Frame", entry)
        sTrack.Size = UDim2.new(1, -16, 0, isMobile and 4 or 5)
        sTrack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, isMobile and 22 or 28)
        sTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 42, 48); sTrack.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", sTrack).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local iPct = math.clamp((currentVal - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal), 0, 1)
        local fill = Instance.new("Frame", sTrack)
        fill.Size = UDim2.new(iPct, 0, 1, 0)
        fill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255); fill.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", fill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local sKnob = Instance.new("Frame", sTrack)
        sKnob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 10 or 12, 0, isMobile and 10 or 12)
        sKnob.Position = UDim2.new(iPct, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
        sKnob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255); sKnob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", sKnob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local dragging = false
        local function updateSlider(inputPos)
            if showLock and _G.DepthLocked then return end
            local tPos = sTrack.AbsolutePosition.X; local tW = sTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
            local pct = math.clamp((inputPos.X - tPos) / tW, 0, 1)
            local raw = minVal + pct * (maxVal - minVal)
            local val = math.clamp(math.floor(raw / step + 0.5) * step, minVal, maxVal)
            _G[globalVar] = val; lbl.Text = label .. ": " .. string.format(fmt, val)
            local ap = (val - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal)
            fill.Size = UDim2.new(ap, 0, 1, 0)
            sKnob.Position = UDim2.new(ap, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
            if callback then callback(val) end
        end
        sTrack.InputBegan:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then dragging = true; updateSlider(input.Position) end end)
        sTrack.InputEnded:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then dragging = false end end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input) if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then updateSlider(input.Position) end end)
        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then dragging = false end end)
        return entry
    end

    createBlackSectionHeader(MvContent, "INVISIBLE STEAL")

    local rotEntry = Instance.new("Frame", MvContent)

    _G.updateRotationSliderUI = function(angle)
        _G.InvisStealAngle = angle
        local p = math.clamp((angle - 1) / 359, 0, 1)
        rotationLabel.Text = "Rotation: " .. tostring(math.floor(angle)) .. "°"
        rotFill.Size = UDim2.new(p, 0, 1, 0)
        rotKnob.Position = UDim2.new(p, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
    end

    local rotDragging = false
    local function updateRotSlider(pos)
        if _G.AutoRotateInvis then return end
        local tP = rotTrack.AbsolutePosition.X; local tW = rotTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
        local p = math.clamp((pos.X - tP) / tW, 0, 1)
        local v = math.floor(1 + p * 359 + 0.5)
        _G.InvisStealAngle = v; rotationLabel.Text = "Rotation: " .. tostring(v) .. "°"
        rotFill.Size = UDim2.new(p, 0, 1, 0); rotKnob.Position = UDim2.new(p, -(isMobile and 5 or 6), 0.5, -(isMobile and 5 or 6))
    end
    rotTrack.InputBegan:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then rotDragging = true; updateRotSlider(input.Position) end end)
    rotTrack.InputEnded:Connect(function(input) if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then rotDragging = false end end)
    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input) if rotDragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then updateRotSlider(input.Position) end end)

    local arEntry = Instance.new("Frame", MvContent)

    Instance.new("UICorner", arEntry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local arBox = Instance.new("Frame", arEntry)
    arBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 14 or 18, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
    arBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9))
    arBox.BackgroundColor3 = _G.AutoRotateInvis and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(40, 42, 48)
    arBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
    Instance.new("UICorner", arBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
    local arCheck = Instance.new("TextLabel", arBox)
    arCheck.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0); arCheck.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    arCheck.Text = _G.AutoRotateInvis and "✓" or ""

                if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end

                end

                if MainFrame then
                    MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
                end
            end
        end)

    ProxToggleCircle.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 14 or 18, 0, isMobile and 14 or 18)
    ProxToggleCircle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9))
    ProxToggleCircle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 130, 140)

    local proxEnabled = false
    local proxConnection = nil

    local ProxToggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", ProxToggleContainer)
    ProxToggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    ProxToggleBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    ProxToggleBtn.Text = ""

    local playersInProximity = {}
    local proximityCheckInterval = 0.5
    local lastProximityCheck = 0

    local proximityCommands = {"ragdoll", "balloon", "inverse", "jail", "morph", "rocket", "tiny"}

    local function checkProximity()
        if not proxEnabled then
            playersInProximity = {}
            return
        end

        local currentTime = tick()
        if currentTime - lastProximityCheck < proximityCheckInterval then return end
        lastProximityCheck = currentTime

        local char = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if not (char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
            playersInProximity = {}
            return
        end

        local hrp = char.HumanoidRootPart
        local dist = _G.ProximityDistance or 25

        for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if plr ~= Players.LocalPlayer and plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local targetHrp = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                local horizontalDistance = math.sqrt(
                    (hrp.Position.X - targetHrp.Position.X)^2 +
                    (hrp.Position.Z - targetHrp.Position.Z)^2
                )

                if horizontalDistance <= dist then
                    if not playersInProximity[plr] then
                        playersInProximity[plr] = true
                        task.spawn(function()
                            for _, cmd in ipairs(proximityCommands) do
                                if not proxEnabled then break end
                                if plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    local targetPos = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                                    local currentDist = math.sqrt(
                                        (hrp.Position.X - targetPos.X)^2 +
                                        (hrp.Position.Z - targetPos.Z)^2
                                    )
                                    if currentDist > dist then break end
                                else
                                    break
                                end
                                if not _G.commandCooldowns or not _G.commandCooldowns[cmd] or tick() > _G.commandCooldowns[cmd] then
                                    pcall(function()
                                        executeAdmin(plr, cmd)
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(0.1)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                else
                    playersInProximity[plr] = nil
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function doProximityToggle()
        proxEnabled = not proxEnabled
        _G.ProximityEnabled = proxEnabled
        _G.AutoProximityEnabled = proxEnabled

        if proxEnabled then
            TweenService:Create(ProxToggleBG, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
            TweenService:Create(ProxToggleCircle, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
                Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 16 or 20), 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9)),
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            }):Play()

            proxConnection = _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if proxEnabled then
                    checkProximity()
                end
            end))
        else
            TweenService:Create(ProxToggleBG, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 35, 42)}):Play()
            TweenService:Create(ProxToggleCircle, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
                Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 7 or 9)),
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 130, 140)
            }):Play()

            if proxConnection then
                proxConnection:Disconnect()
                proxConnection = nil
            end
        end
    end

    ProxToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(doProximityToggle)

    _G.toggleProximity = doProximityToggle

    local SpamBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", ProxContent)
    SpamBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 38 or 44)
    SpamBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    SpamBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    SpamBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
    SpamBtn.Text = "Spam Base Owner"
    SpamBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    SpamBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 13
    SpamBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

    Instance.new("UICorner", SpamBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)


    SpamBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()

        local char = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if not char or not char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            task.wait(0.2)
            TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
            return
        end

        local plots = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots") or workspace:FindFirstChild("plots")
        if not plots then
            task.wait(0.2)
            TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
            return
        end

        local closestPlot, minDist = nil, math.huge
        for _, plot in pairs(plots:GetChildren()) do
            local pos = nil
            pcall(function() pos = plot:GetPivot().Position end)
            if not pos then
                local p = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign") or plot:FindFirstChild("Base") or plot:FindFirstChild("Floor")
                if p and p:IsA("BasePart") then pos = p.Position end
            end
            if pos then
                local d = (char.HumanoidRootPart.Position - pos).Magnitude
                if d < minDist then closestPlot, minDist = plot, d end
            end
        end

        if not closestPlot then
            task.wait(0.2)
            TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
            return
        end

        local ownerName = nil
        local sign = closestPlot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
        if sign then
            local sg = sign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
            if sg then
                local lbl = sg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                if lbl and lbl.Text then
                    ownerName = lbl.Text:match("([^']+)'s") or lbl.Text
                    ownerName = ownerName:gsub("^%s+", ""):gsub("%s+$", "")
                end
            end
        end

        if not ownerName then
            task.wait(0.2)
            TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
            return
        end

        local target = nil
        for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p.DisplayName:lower() == ownerName:lower() or p.Name:lower() == ownerName:lower() then
                target = p
                break
            end
        end
        if not target then
            for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if p.DisplayName:lower():find(ownerName:lower(), 1, true) or p.Name:lower():find(ownerName:lower(), 1, true) then
                    target = p
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if not target or target == Players.LocalPlayer then
            task.wait(0.2)
            TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
            return
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            for _, cmd in ipairs({'jail','rocket','inverse','ragdoll','jumpscare','tiny','balloon','morph'}) do
                if not (_G.commandOnCooldown and _G.commandOnCooldown(cmd)) then
                    if executeAdmin then
                        task.spawn(function()
                            executeAdmin(target, cmd)
                        end)
                    end
                    if _G.setCommandCooldown then
                        _G.setCommandCooldown(cmd)
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        task.wait(0.2)
        TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)}):Play()
    end)

    SpamBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.3}):Play()
    end)

    SpamBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(SpamBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.5}):Play()
    end)

    local SliderContainer = Instance.new("Frame", ProxContent)

    local SliderLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", SliderContainer)

    SliderBar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 1, -(isMobile and 16 or 20))
    SliderBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 45, 55)
    SliderBar.BorderSizePixel = 0

    SliderFill.BorderSizePixel = 0

    Instance.new("UICorner", SliderFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local SliderButton = Instance.new("TextButton", SliderBar)
    SliderButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 16 or 20, 0, isMobile and 16 or 20)
    SliderButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -(isMobile and 8 or 10), 0.5, -(isMobile and 8 or 10))
    SliderButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    SliderButton.Text = ""

    Instance.new("UICorner", SliderButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local draggingSlider = false
    local distanceValue = 25

    SliderButton.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            draggingSlider = true
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            draggingSlider = false
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if draggingSlider and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
            local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
            local sliderPos = SliderBar.AbsolutePosition
            local sliderSize = SliderBar.AbsoluteSize

            local relativePos = math.clamp((mousePos.X - sliderPos.X) / sliderSize.X, 0, 1)
            distanceValue = math.floor(1 + (relativePos * 49))

            _G.ProximityDistance = distanceValue

            SliderFill.Size = UDim2.new(relativePos, 0, 1, 0)
            SliderButton.Position = UDim2.new(relativePos, -(isMobile and 8 or 10), 0.5, -(isMobile and 8 or 10))
            SliderLabel.Text = "Distance: " .. distanceValue .. " studs"
        end
    end)

        task.wait(0.5)
        if _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES then
            if _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.PlayerControls and PlayerControlsPanel then PlayerControlsPanel.Visible = true; _G.dxhub_PANELS.PlayerControls = true end
            if _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.Proximity and ProximityPanel then ProximityPanel.Visible = true; _G.dxhub_PANELS.Proximity = true end
        end
    end)

    local ROW_HEIGHT = isMobile and 62 or 72
    local VP_SIZE = isMobile and 50 or 58

    local function formatTargetValue(value)
        if not value or value == 0 then return "?" end
        if value >= 1e12 then return string.format("%.1fT/s", value / 1e12)
        elseif value >= 1e9 then return string.format("%.1fB/s", value / 1e9)
        elseif value >= 1e6 then return string.format("%.0fM/s", value / 1e6)
        elseif value >= 1e3 then return string.format("%.0fK/s", value / 1e3)
        else return string.format("%.0f/s", value) end
    end

    local function getFloorName(yPos)
        if yPos > 23.15 then return "3F"
        elseif yPos >= 11 and yPos <= 23.15 then return "2F"
        else return "1F" end
    end

    local function refreshTargetPanel()
        for _, child in ipairs(TPanelScroll:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
        end

        local allItems = {}
        if _G.scanDebrisForSteal then
            allItems = _G.scanDebrisForSteal() or {}
        else
            allItems = findAllBrainrots() or {}
        end

        table.sort(allItems, function(a, b)
            return (a.genValue or a.value or 0) > (b.genValue or b.value or 0)
        end)

        TPanelCount.Text = tostring(#allItems)

        if #allItems == 0 then
            local emptyLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", TPanelScroll)
            emptyLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
            emptyLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            emptyLabel.Text = "No brainrots found..."
            emptyLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
            emptyLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
            emptyLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 80)
            return
        end

        for idx, item in ipairs(allItems) do
            local itemName = item.name or "Unknown"
            local itemValue = item.genValue or item.value or 0
            local itemPos = item.position or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            local floorLabel = getFloorName(itemPos.Y)

            -- Check if priority item
            local isPriority = false
            if nameInfo and nameInfo[itemName:lower()] then
                isPriority = true
            end

            local row = Instance.new("Frame", TPanelScroll)
            row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, ROW_HEIGHT)
            row.BackgroundColor3 = idx == 1 and Color3.fromRGB(20, 28, 20) or Color3.fromRGB(18, 19, 24)
            row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
            row.BorderSizePixel = 0
            row.LayoutOrder = idx
            Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

            -- #1 glow
            if idx == 1 then
                local glow = Instance.new("UIStroke", row)
                glow.Color = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
                glow.Thickness = 1.5
                glow.Transparency = 0.4
            end

            -- Rank number
            local rankLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            rankLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 16 or 20, 0, isMobile and 16 or 20)
            rankLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 4)
            rankLabel.BackgroundColor3 = idx <= 3 and Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 50) or Color3.fromRGB(40, 42, 50)
            rankLabel.BackgroundTransparency = idx <= 3 and 0.2 or 0.5
            rankLabel.BorderSizePixel = 0
            rankLabel.Text = tostring(idx)
            rankLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            rankLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 9
            rankLabel.TextColor3 = idx <= 3 and Color3.fromRGB(40, 30, 0) or Color3.fromRGB(150, 155, 170)
            Instance.new("UICorner", rankLabel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

            -- Viewport
            local vpBox = Instance.new("Frame", row)
            vpBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, VP_SIZE, 0, VP_SIZE)
            vpBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 6 or 8, 0.5, -(VP_SIZE / 2))
            vpBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(8, 9, 12)
            vpBox.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            vpBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", vpBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            if idx == 1 then
                local vpStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", vpBox)
                vpStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
                vpStroke.Thickness = 1.5
                vpStroke.Transparency = 0.3
            end

            makeVP(vpBox, itemName, 0.78)

            -- Text area
            local textX = VP_SIZE + (isMobile and 14 or 16)
            local rightSpace = isMobile and 50 or 60

            -- Name
            local nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(textX + rightSpace), 0, isMobile and 16 or 20)
            nameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, isMobile and 6 or 8)
            nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            nameLabel.Text = itemName
            nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            nameLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
            nameLabel.TextColor3 = isPriority and Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 50) or Color3.fromRGB(220, 225, 240)
            nameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            nameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd

            -- Value
            local valueLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
            valueLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -(textX + rightSpace), 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)
            valueLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 0, isMobile and 23 or 28)
            valueLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            valueLabel.Text = "$" .. formatTargetValue(itemValue)
            valueLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            valueLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
            valueLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 220, 100)
            valueLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

            -- Floor badge
            local floorBadge = Instance.new("Frame", row)
            floorBadge.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 22 or 26, 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)
            floorBadge.Position = UDim2.new(0, textX, 1, -(isMobile and 18 or 22))
            floorBadge.BackgroundColor3 = floorLabel == "3F" and Color3.fromRGB(60, 20, 60) or (floorLabel == "2F" and Color3.fromRGB(20, 40, 60) or Color3.fromRGB(20, 50, 20))
            floorBadge.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
            floorBadge.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Instance.new("UICorner", floorBadge).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

            local floorText = Instance.new("TextLabel", floorBadge)
            floorText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            floorText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            floorText.Text = floorLabel
            floorText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            floorText.TextSize = isMobile and 8 or 9
            floorText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 190, 210)

            -- TP button
            local tpBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", row)
            tpBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 38 or 46, 0, isMobile and 28 or 34)
            tpBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 44 or 52), 0.5, -(isMobile and 14 or 17))
            tpBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 80, 30)
            tpBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
            tpBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
            tpBtn.Text = "TP"
            tpBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            tpBtn.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
            tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            Instance.new("UICorner", tpBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

            tpBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(tpBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0, BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 120, 50)}):Play()
            end)
            tpBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(tpBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.2, BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 80, 30)}):Play()
            end)

            local capturedItem = item
            tpBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if _G.isTeleporting then return end

                -- Verify it still exists
                if not capturedItem.part or not capturedItem.part.Parent then
                    tpBtn.Text = "Gone"
                    tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
                    task.delay(1, function()
                        if tpBtn and tpBtn.Parent then
                            tpBtn.Text = "TP"
                            tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
                        end
                    end)
                    return
                end

                tpBtn.Text = "..."
                tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 100)

                -- Set as selected steal target so TeleportToHighest uses it
                _G.SelectedStealTarget = {
                    part = capturedItem.part,
                    name = capturedItem.name or "Unknown",
                    value = capturedItem.genValue or capturedItem.value or 0,
                    genValue = capturedItem.genValue or capturedItem.value or 0,
                    position = capturedItem.position,
                }

                task.spawn(function()
                    if _G.TeleportToHighest then
                        local ok, err = pcall(_G.TeleportToHighest, true)
                        if not ok then
                            warn("[dxhub] Target Panel TP error: " .. tostring(err))
                            _G.isTeleporting = false
                        end
                        task.delay(3, function()
                            _G.isTeleporting = false
                            _G.SelectedStealTarget = nil
                        end)
                    end
                    if tpBtn and tpBtn.Parent then
                        tpBtn.Text = "TP"
                        tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
                    end
                end)
            end)

            -- Hover effect on whole row
            row.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
            end)
            row.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.1}):Play()
            end)
        end
    end

    TPanelRefreshBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(TPanelRefreshBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 120, 255)}):Play()
        task.delay(0.2, function()
            TweenService:Create(TPanelRefreshBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 30, 36)}):Play()
        end)
        refreshTargetPanel()
    end)

    -- Auto-refresh when panel becomes visible
    TargetPanel:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Visible"):Connect(function()
        if TargetPanel.Visible then
            task.spawn(refreshTargetPanel)
        end
    end)

    -- Auto-refresh loop every 3 seconds while visible
    task.spawn(function()
        while _loopFlags.running do
            task.wait(3)
            if TargetPanel.Visible then
                pcall(refreshTargetPanel)
            end
        end
    end)

    -- Restore visibility from saved state
    task.defer(function()
        task.wait(0.5)
        if _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES and _G.SAVED_PANEL_STATES.TargetPanel then
            TargetPanel.Visible = true
            _G.dxhub_PANELS.TargetPanel = true
        end
    end)
    end) -- end Target Panel scope

        }

        _G.QUICK_PANEL_FEATURES = _G.QUICK_PANEL_FEATURES or {}

        local QuickPanel = Instance.new("Frame")
        QuickPanel.Name = "QuickPanel"
        QuickPanel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 160 or 200, 0, isMobile and 50 or 60)
        if _G.SAVED_UI_POSITIONS and _G.SAVED_UI_POSITIONS.QuickPanel then
            local pos = _G.SAVED_UI_POSITIONS.QuickPanel
            QuickPanel.Position = UDim2.new(pos.XScale, pos.XOffset, pos.YScale, pos.YOffset)
        else

        QAddBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 14 or 16, 0, isMobile and 14 or 16)

        local qDrag, qDragIn, qDragSt, qStPos = false, nil, nil, nil
        QHeader.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if _G.DRAG_DISABLED then return end
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                qDrag = true; qDragSt = input.Position; qStPos = QuickPanel.Position
                input.Changed:Connect(function()
                    if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                        qDrag = false
                        if _G.autoSavePositions then pcall(_G.autoSavePositions) end
                    end

            end
        end)
        QHeader.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then qDragIn = input end
        end)
        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if input == qDragIn and qDrag then
                local d = input.Position - qDragSt
                QuickPanel.Position = UDim2.new(qStPos.X.Scale, qStPos.X.Offset + d.X, qStPos.Y.Scale, qStPos.Y.Offset + d.Y)
            end
        end)

        Qpad.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 2)
        Qpad.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 2)

        Qpad.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 2)

        local quickToggleRefs = {}

        local function getFeatureById(id)
            for _, f in ipairs(QUICK_FEATURES) do
                if f.id == id then return f end
            end
            return nil
        end

        local function rebuildQuickPanel()
            for _, child in ipairs(QScroll:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
            end
            quickToggleRefs = {}

            local activeFeatures = _G.QUICK_PANEL_FEATURES or {}
            local count = 0

            for _, featureId in ipairs(activeFeatures) do
                local feat = getFeatureById(featureId)
                if not feat then continue end
                count = count + 1

                local row = Instance.new("Frame", QScroll)
                row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
                row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 28)
                row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
                row.BorderSizePixel = 0
                row.LayoutOrder = count
                Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

                local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", row)
                lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -42, 1, 0)
                lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
                lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                lbl.Text = feat.label
                lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                lbl.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
                lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 220)
                lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

                local isOn = _G[feat.global] or false

                local track = Instance.new("Frame", row)
                track.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 28 or 32, 0, isMobile and 12 or 14)
                track.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 34 or 38), 0.5, -(isMobile and 6 or 7))
                track.BackgroundColor3 = isOn and (_G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)) or Color3.fromRGB(50, 52, 58)
                track.BorderSizePixel = 0
                Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

                local knob = Instance.new("Frame", track)
                knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 8 or 10, 0, isMobile and 8 or 10)
                knob.Position = isOn and UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 10 or 12), 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5)) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -(isMobile and 4 or 5))

_track(UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    if input.KeyCode == _G.CloneKey and _G.InstantCloneEnabled == true then
        QuantumClone()
    elseif input.KeyCode == _G.RagdollSelfKey then
        executeAdmin(player, "ragdoll")
    end
end))


for i = 1, _G.RING_SEGMENTS do
    local segment = Instance.new("Part")
    segment.Name = "ProximityRingSegment"
    segment.Anchored = true
    segment.CanCollide = false
    segment.CanQuery = false
    segment.CanTouch = false
    segment.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
    segment.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    segment.Transparency = 1
    segment.CastShadow = false
    segment.Size = Vector3.new(_G.RING_THICKNESS, _G.RING_THICKNESS, 1)
    segment.Parent = workspace
    table.insert(_G.ringParts, segment)
end

_G.updateRingVisuals = function()
    local root = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not _G.ProximityEnabled or not root or not root.Parent then
        for _, segment in ipairs(_G.ringParts) do
            segment.Transparency = 1
        end
        return
    end
    local radius = _G.ProximityDistance or 25
    local centerPos = Vector3.new(root.Position.X, root.Position.Y - 2.7, root.Position.Z)
    local segmentLength = (2 * math.pi * radius) / _G.RING_SEGMENTS * 1.05
    
    for i, segment in ipairs(_G.ringParts) do
        local angle = (i / _G.RING_SEGMENTS) * math.pi * 2
        local x = math.cos(angle) * radius
        local z = math.sin(angle) * radius
        segment.Size = Vector3.new(_G.RING_THICKNESS, _G.RING_THICKNESS, segmentLength)
        segment.CFrame = CFrame.new(centerPos + Vector3.new(x, 0, z)) * CFrame.Angles(0, angle + math.pi/2, 0)
        segment.Transparency = 0.3
        segment.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    end
end

RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if isStealing then return end
    local prompt = findNearestPrompt()
    --if prompt then executeSteal(prompt) end
end)

_track(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
    if _G.updateRingVisuals then
        _G.updateRingVisuals()
    end
end))

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.AutoProximityEnabled then
            local root = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if root and root.Parent then
                local maxdistance = _G.ProximityDistance or 25
                local target = getNearestPlayer(maxdistance)
                if target then
                    for cmdName, cooldownTime in pairs(CommandSettings) do
                        local lastUsed = GlobalCooldowns[cmdName] or 0
                        if tick() - lastUsed >= cooldownTime then
                            GlobalCooldowns[cmdName] = tick()
                            executeAdmin(target, cmdName)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local isCloning = false

    _G.instantClonerV2 = function()
        if not _G.InstantCloneEnabled then
            return
        end
        if isCloning then
            return
        end

        QuantumClone()

        if cloneSuccess and _G.TPDirectlyToPet then
            task.wait(0.35)
            local freshPos, freshHeight = nil, nil
            pcall(function()
                local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
                if not debrisFolder then return end
                local hrpRef = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                local hrpPos = hrpRef and hrpRef.Position or Vector3.zero
                local allItems = {}
                local priorityNames = _G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS or {
                    "strawberry elephant", "headless horseman", "meowl", "skibidi toilet",
                    "hydra dragon cannelloni", "dragon gingerini", "la supreme combinasion",
                    "dragon cannelloni", "ginger gerat", "cerberus", "capitano moby", "la casa boo",
                    "popcuru and fizzuru", "cooki and milki", "burguro and fryuro", "ketupat bros",
                    "reinito sleighito", "spooky and pumpky", "fragrama and chocrama", "festive 67",
                    "garama and madundung"
                }
                for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
                    if not obj:IsA("BasePart") then continue end
                    local dName, genLabel
                    for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                            for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                                if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                    if label.Name == "DisplayName" then dName = label.Text end
                                    if label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then genLabel = label.Text end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if dName and genLabel then
                        local gt = genLabel:lower()
                        local v = tonumber(gt:match("[%d%.]+")) or 0
                        if gt:find("t") then v = v * 1e12
                        elseif gt:find("b") then v = v * 1e9
                        elseif gt:find("m") then v = v * 1e6
                        elseif gt:find("k") then v = v * 1e3 end
                        if v >= 5000000 then
                            local pos = obj.Position - Vector3.new(0, 11, 0)
                            local dist = (obj.Position - hrpPos).Magnitude
                            local prio = 999
                            for i, pName in ipairs(priorityNames) do
                                if dName:lower():find(pName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                    prio = i
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            table.insert(allItems, {name = dName, value = v, position = pos, height = pos.Y, distance = dist, priority = prio})
                        end
                    end
                end
                if #allItems == 0 then return end
                local target = nil
                if _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled then
                    for _, item in ipairs(allItems) do
                        if item.priority < 999 then
                            if not target or item.priority < target.priority or (item.priority == target.priority and item.value > target.value) then
                                target = item
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if not target then
                    table.sort(allItems, function(a, b) return a.value > b.value end)
                    target = allItems[1]
                end
                if target then
                    freshPos = target.position
                    freshHeight = target.height
                end
            end)
            if freshPos then
                local newChar = player.Character
                local newHRP = newChar and newChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                local newHumanoid = newChar and newChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                local distMoved = newHRP and posBeforeClone and (newHRP.Position - posBeforeClone).Magnitude or 0
                if distMoved >= 0.3 and newHRP and newHumanoid then
                    local myY = newHRP.Position.Y
                    local myFloor = 0
                    if myY >= -6.9 and myY <= 8.9 then myFloor = 1
                    elseif myY >= 11 and myY <= 23.15 then myFloor = 2
                    elseif myY > 23.15 then myFloor = 3 end
                    local itemFloor = 0
                    if freshHeight then
                        if freshHeight >= -6.9 and freshHeight <= 8.9 then itemFloor = 1
                        elseif freshHeight >= 11 and freshHeight <= 23.15 then itemFloor = 2
                        elseif freshHeight > 23.15 then itemFloor = 3 end
                    end
                    local floorOk = (myFloor == itemFloor) or (myFloor == 2 and itemFloor == 3)
                    if floorOk then
                        local inPlotRadius = false
                        local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
                        if plotsFolder then
                            local pos = newHRP.Position
                            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                                pcall(function()
                                    local plotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                                    if math.abs(pos.X - plotPos.X) < 23 and math.abs(pos.Z - plotPos.Z) < 23 then
                                        inPlotRadius = true
                                    end
                                end)
                                if inPlotRadius then break end
                            end
                        end
                        if inPlotRadius then
                            pcall(function()
                                local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                                if backpack then
                                    local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                                    if carpet then newHumanoid:EquipTool(carpet) end
                                end
                            end)
                            local targetY = newHRP.Position.Y
                            if freshHeight then
                                if freshHeight > 23.15 then targetY = 21
                                elseif freshHeight >= 11 and freshHeight <= 23.15 then targetY = 14.5
                                elseif freshHeight >= -6.9 and freshHeight <= 8.9 then targetY = -4 end
                            end
                            newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            newHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            newHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(freshPos.X, targetY, freshPos.Z)
                            newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            newHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            if freshHeight and freshHeight > 23.15 then
                                pcall(function()
                                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                                    if backpack then
                                        local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                                        if carpet then newHumanoid:EquipTool(carpet) task.wait(0.1) end
                                    end
                                end)
                                newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                newHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(freshPos.X, 21, freshPos.Z)
                                newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                if _G.enableFloat then pcall(_G.enableFloat) end
                            end
                        elseif _G.autoCarpetPulloutEnabled and _G.TPSpeedItem then
                            local bp = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                            if bp then
                                local item = bp:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem)
                                if item then newHumanoid:EquipTool(item) end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif cloneSuccess then
            -- No TPDirectlyToPet, just equip carpet
            task.wait(0.1)
            pcall(function()
                local character2 = player.Character
                local humanoid2 = character2 and character2:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                local backpack2 = player.Backpack
                if humanoid2 and backpack2 then
                    local carpet = backpack2:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                    if carpet then humanoid2:EquipTool(carpet) end
                end
            end)
        end

        task.wait(0.05)
        isCloning = false
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()

    local walkspeedConnection = nil
    local lastWalkspeedPosition = nil
    local walkspeedPausedUntil = 0
    local lastWalkspeedTime = nil
    local lagbackThreshold = 15

    if _G.WalkspeedEnabled == nil then _G.WalkspeedEnabled = false end
    _G.currentWalkSpeed = _G.currentWalkSpeed or _G.WalkspeedValue or 27

    local function applyWalkspeed()
        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        if not character then return end
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not humanoid or not hrp then return end

        local currentTime = tick()
        local currentPosition = hrp.Position

        if currentTime < walkspeedPausedUntil then
            return
        end

        if lastWalkspeedPosition then
            local distance = (currentPosition - lastWalkspeedPosition).Magnitude
            local timeDelta = currentTime - (lastWalkspeedTime or currentTime)
            if distance > lagbackThreshold and timeDelta < 0.5 and not _G.isTeleporting then
                walkspeedPausedUntil = currentTime + 1
                lastWalkspeedPosition = currentPosition
                lastWalkspeedTime = currentTime
                return
            end
        end

        lastWalkspeedPosition = currentPosition
        lastWalkspeedTime = currentTime

        local moveDirection = humanoid.MoveDirection
        if moveDirection.Magnitude > 0 then
            local targetSpeed = _G.currentWalkSpeed or _G.WalkspeedValue or 27
            local targetVelocity = moveDirection * targetSpeed
            local currentYVelocity = hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Y
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(
                targetVelocity.X,
                currentYVelocity,
                targetVelocity.Z
            )
        end
    end

    _G.startWalkspeed = function()
        if walkspeedConnection then return end
        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = true
        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = true

        lastWalkspeedPosition = nil
