        walkspeedPausedUntil = 0
        lastWalkspeedTime = nil

        local walkspeedFrameCount = 0
        walkspeedConnection = _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
                walkspeedFrameCount = walkspeedFrameCount + 1
                if walkspeedFrameCount >= 2 then
                    walkspeedFrameCount = 0
                    pcall(applyWalkspeed)
                end
            end
        end))

        if _G.updateWalkspeedToggleVisual then
            pcall(_G.updateWalkspeedToggleVisual, true)
        end

    end

    _G.stopWalkspeed = function()
        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = false
        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = false

        if walkspeedConnection then
            walkspeedConnection:Disconnect()
            walkspeedConnection = nil
        end

        if _G.updateWalkspeedToggleVisual then
            pcall(_G.updateWalkspeedToggleVisual, false)
        end

    end

    _G.toggleWalkspeed = function()
        if _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
            _G.stopWalkspeed()
        else
            _G.startWalkspeed()
        end
        return _G.WalkspeedEnabled
    end

    _G.setWalkspeedValue = function(value)
        _G.currentWalkSpeed = math.clamp(value, 16, 29)
        _G.WalkspeedValue = _G.currentWalkSpeed
    end

    _track(LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        lastWalkspeedPosition = nil
        walkspeedPausedUntil = 0
        lastWalkspeedTime = nil

        if _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
            task.wait(0.1)
            if walkspeedConnection then
                walkspeedConnection:Disconnect()
            end
            local walkspeedFrameCount2 = 0
            walkspeedConnection = _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
                    walkspeedFrameCount2 = walkspeedFrameCount2 + 1
                    if walkspeedFrameCount2 >= 2 then
                        walkspeedFrameCount2 = 0
                        pcall(applyWalkspeed)
                    end
                end
            end))
        end
    end))

end)

task.spawn(function()

    local wasStealingForWalkspeed = false
    local walkspeedWasEnabledBefore = false

    task.wait(1)

    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(0.1) do
            if not _G.AutoWalkspeedAfterSteal and not _G.AutoWalkspeedOnSteal then
                wasStealingForWalkspeed = false
                continue
            end

            local isStealing = LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing")

            if isStealing and not wasStealingForWalkspeed then
                walkspeedWasEnabledBefore = _G.WalkspeedEnabled or false

                if _G.AfterStealWalkspeedValue then
                    _G.currentWalkSpeed = _G.AfterStealWalkspeedValue
                    _G.WalkspeedValue = _G.AfterStealWalkspeedValue
                end

                task.spawn(function()
                    task.wait(1) -- Wait 1 second after steal starts
                    if LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") and not _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
                        if _G.startWalkspeed then
                            pcall(_G.startWalkspeed)
                        end
                        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = true
                        _G.WalkspeedEnabled = true

                        if _G.updateWalkspeedPanelVisual then
                            pcall(_G.updateWalkspeedPanelVisual, true)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end

            if not isStealing and wasStealingForWalkspeed then
                if not walkspeedWasEnabledBefore and _G.WalkspeedEnabled then
                    if _G.stopWalkspeed then
                        pcall(_G.stopWalkspeed)
                    end
                    _G.WalkspeedEnabled = false
                    _G.WalkspeedEnabled = false

                    if _G.updateWalkspeedPanelVisual then
                        pcall(_G.updateWalkspeedPanelVisual, false)
                    end
                end
            end

            wasStealingForWalkspeed = isStealing
        end
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()

    local wasStealingForTurret = false
    local turretWasEnabledBefore = false

    task.wait(1)

    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(0.1) do
            if _G.isTeleporting then
                continue
            end

            if not _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal and not _G.AutoTurretOnSteal then
                wasStealingForTurret = false
                continue
            end

            local isStealing = LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing")

            if isStealing and not wasStealingForTurret then
                turretWasEnabledBefore = _G.autoTurretEnabled or false
                wasStealingForTurret = true

                _G.autoTurretEnabled = true
                if _G.scanExistingSentries then
                    pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                    task.delay(0.5, function()
                        if _G.autoTurretEnabled and _G.scanExistingSentries then
                            pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.delay(1.5, function()
                        if _G.autoTurretEnabled and _G.scanExistingSentries then
                            pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end

            if isStealing and wasStealingForTurret and _G.autoTurretEnabled then
                if _G.scanExistingSentries and math.random() < 0.1 then -- 10% chance each tick
                    pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                end
            end

            if not isStealing and wasStealingForTurret then
                wasStealingForTurret = false
                if not turretWasEnabledBefore then
                    _G.autoTurretEnabled = false
                end
            end
        end
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()

    local wasStealingForUnlock = false

    task.wait(1)

    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(0.1) do
            if not _G.AutoUnlockBaseAfterSteal and not _G.AutoUnlockDuringSteal then
                wasStealingForUnlock = false
                continue
            end

            local isStealing = LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing")

            if isStealing and not wasStealingForUnlock then
                task.spawn(function()
                    task.wait(0.5)
                    if LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") and _G.unlockCurrentBase then
                        pcall(_G.unlockCurrentBase)
                    end
                end)
            end

            wasStealingForUnlock = isStealing
        end
    end)
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local wasStealingForInvis = false
    local invisWasEnabledBefore = false

    task.wait(1)

    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(0.1) do
            if not _G.AutoInvisibleAfterSteal and not _G.AutoInvisDuringSteal then
                if wasStealingForInvis and _G.invisibleStealEnabled then
                    if _G.toggleInvisibleSteal then pcall(_G.toggleInvisibleSteal) end
                end
                wasStealingForInvis = false
                continue
            end

            local isStealing = LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing")

            if isStealing and not wasStealingForInvis then
                invisWasEnabledBefore = _G.invisibleStealEnabled or false
                wasStealingForInvis = true
            end

            if not isStealing and wasStealingForInvis then
                wasStealingForInvis = false
                invisWasEnabledBefore = false
                if _G.invisibleStealEnabled then
                    if _G.forceStopInvis then
                        pcall(_G.forceStopInvis)
                    end
                end
            end

if wasStealingForInvis and isStealing then
    if not _G.invisibleStealEnabled then
        task.spawn(function()
            task.wait(0.8)
            if _G.AutoInvisibleAfterSteal and not _G.invisibleStealEnabled and LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Stealing") and not _G.isTeleporting then
                pcall(_G.toggleInvisibleSteal)
            end
        end)
    end
end
        end
    end)
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local animDisableConnection = nil
    local originalAnimations = {}

    _G.startAnimDisable = function()
        if animDisableConnection then return end
        _G.AutoStealDisableAnimEnabled = true

        animDisableConnection = _track(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            local character = player.Character
            if not character then return end
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid then return end

            local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
            if animator then
                for _, track in ipairs(animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                    track:Stop(0)
                end
            end
        end))
    end

    _G.stopAnimDisable = function()
        _G.AutoStealDisableAnimEnabled = false
        if animDisableConnection then
            animDisableConnection:Disconnect()
            animDisableConnection = nil
        end
    end

    _G.toggleAnimDisable = function()
        if _G.AutoStealDisableAnimEnabled then
            _G.stopAnimDisable()
        else
            _G.startAnimDisable()
        end
    end

end)

_G.invisibleStealEnabled = false
_G.AutoRecoverLagback = true
_G.RecoveryInProgress = false
_G.InvisStealAngle = _G.InvisStealAngle or 180
if _G.AutoRotateInvis == nil then _G.AutoRotateInvis = false end
_G.SinkSliderValue = _G.SinkSliderValue or 5
_G.INVISIBLE_STEAL_KEY = _G.INVISIBLE_STEAL_KEY or Enum.KeyCode.U

task.spawn(function()
    local animPlaying = false
    local tracks = {}
    local clone, oldRoot, hip, connection, jumpConn
    local folderConnections = {}
    local SINK_AMOUNT = 5
    local serverGhosts = {}
    local ghostEnabled = true
    local lagbackCallCount = 0
    local lagbackWindowStart = 0
    local lastLagbackTime = 0
    local errorOrbActive = false
    local errorOrb = nil
    local errorOrbConnection = nil

    local function clearErrorOrb()
        if errorOrb and errorOrb.Parent then
            errorOrb:Destroy()
        end
        errorOrb = nil
        errorOrbActive = false
        if errorOrbConnection then
            errorOrbConnection:Disconnect()
            errorOrbConnection = nil
        end
    end

    local function createErrorOrb()
        if errorOrbActive then return end
        errorOrbActive = true
        for _, ghost in pairs(serverGhosts) do
            if ghost and ghost.Parent then
                ghost:Destroy()
            end
        end
        serverGhosts = {}
        local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        screenGui.Name = "ErrorOrbGui"
        screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        screenGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
        local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 500, 0, 60)
        frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -250, 0.3, 0)
        frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        frame.Parent = screenGui
        local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0)
        label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        label.Text = "ERROR CAUSED BY PLAYER DEATH"
        label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        label.TextScaled = true
        label.Parent = frame
        local label2 = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        label2.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0)
        label2.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
        label2.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        label2.Text = "MUST RESET TO FIX ERROR"
        label2.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        label2.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        label2.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        label2.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        label2.TextScaled = true
        label2.Parent = frame
        errorOrb = screenGui
    end

    local function createServerGhost(position)
        if not ghostEnabled then return end
        if errorOrbActive then return end
        local now = tick()
        if now - lastLagbackTime < 0.05 then
            return
        end
        lastLagbackTime = now
        if now - lagbackWindowStart > 1 then
            lagbackCallCount = 0
            lagbackWindowStart = now
        end
        lagbackCallCount = lagbackCallCount + 1
        if lagbackCallCount >= 7 then
            createErrorOrb()
            return
        end
        for _, g in pairs(serverGhosts) do
            if g and g.Parent then
                g:Destroy()
            end
        end
        serverGhosts = {}
        local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        screenGui.Name = "LagbackNotification"
        screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        screenGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
        local screenLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        screenLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 500, 0, 30)
        screenLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -250, 0.15, 0)
        screenLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        screenLabel.Text = "LAGBACK DETECTED"
        screenLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        screenLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        screenLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        screenLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        screenLabel.TextScaled = true
        screenLabel.Parent = screenGui
        local screenWarning = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        screenWarning.Size = UDim2.new(0, 650, 0, 25)
        screenWarning.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -325, 0.15, 32)
        screenWarning.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        screenWarning.Text = "DISABLE INVISIBLE STEAL NOW OR YOU WILL BE KILLED BY ANTICHEAT"
        screenWarning.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        screenWarning.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        screenWarning.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        screenWarning.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        screenWarning.TextScaled = true
        screenWarning.Parent = screenGui
        task.delay(1.5, function()
            if screenGui and screenGui.Parent then
                screenGui:Destroy()
            end
        end)
        local raisedPosition = position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
        local ghost = Instance.new("Part")
        ghost.Name = "LagbackGhost"
        ghost.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
        ghost.Size = Vector3.new(3, 3, 3)
        ghost.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        ghost.Material = Enum.Material.Glass
        ghost.Transparency = 0.3
        ghost.CanCollide = false
        ghost.Anchored = true
        ghost.CastShadow = false
        ghost.Position = raisedPosition
        ghost.Parent = Workspace.CurrentCamera
        local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
        billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 400, 0, 60)
        billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 4, 0)
        billboard.AlwaysOnTop = true
        billboard.Parent = ghost
        local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 25)
        label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        label.Text = "LAGBACK DETECTED"
        label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        label.TextScaled = true
        label.Parent = billboard
        local warning = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        warning.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 25)
        warning.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 25)
        warning.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        warning.Text = "DISABLE INVISIBLE STEAL NOW OR YOU WILL BE KILLED BY ANTICHEAT"
        warning.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        warning.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
        warning.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
        warning.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        warning.TextScaled = true
        warning.Parent = billboard
        table.insert(serverGhosts, ghost)
        return ghost
    end

    local function clearAllGhosts()
        for _, ghost in pairs(serverGhosts) do
            pcall(function()
                if ghost and ghost.Parent then
                    ghost:Destroy()
                end
            end)
        end
        serverGhosts = {}
        clearErrorOrb()
        lagbackCallCount = 0
        lastLagbackTime = 0
        pcall(function()
            local playerGui = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui")
            if playerGui then
                for _, gui in pairs(playerGui:GetChildren()) do
                    if gui.Name == "LagbackNotification" then
                        gui:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        pcall(function()
            if Workspace.CurrentCamera then
                for _, child in pairs(Workspace.CurrentCamera:GetChildren()) do
                    if child.Name == "LagbackGhost" then
                        child:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        pcall(function()
            for _, child in pairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                if child.Name == "LagbackGhost" then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    _G.clearAllLagbackGhosts = clearAllGhosts

    local function updateServerGhost(position)
        createServerGhost(position)
    end

    local function removeFolders()
        local playerName = player.Name
        local playerFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild(playerName)
        if not playerFolder then return end
        local doubleRig = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("DoubleRig")
        if doubleRig then
            local rigRoot = doubleRig:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or doubleRig:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
            if rigRoot and ghostEnabled then
                updateServerGhost(rigRoot.Position)
            end
            doubleRig:Destroy()
        end
        local constraints = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("Constraints")
        if constraints then constraints:Destroy() end
        local childAddedConn = playerFolder.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
            if child.Name == "DoubleRig" then
                task.defer(function()
                    local rigRoot = child:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or child:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                    if rigRoot and ghostEnabled then
                        updateServerGhost(rigRoot.Position)
                    end
                    child:Destroy()
                end)
            elseif child.Name == "Constraints" then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end)
        table.insert(folderConnections, childAddedConn)
    end

    local function doClone()
        local character = player.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
            hip = character.Humanoid.HipHeight
            oldRoot = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not oldRoot or not oldRoot.Parent then return false end
            for _, child in pairs(oldRoot:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Attachment") and (child.Name:find("Beam") or child.Name:find("Attach")) then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
            for _, child in pairs(oldRoot:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Beam") then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
            local tempParent = Instance.new("Model")
            tempParent.Parent = game
            character.Parent = tempParent
            clone = oldRoot:Clone()
            clone.Parent = character
            oldRoot.Parent = Workspace.CurrentCamera
            clone.CFrame = oldRoot.CFrame
            character.PrimaryPart = clone
            character.Parent = Workspace
            for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("Weld") or v:IsA("Motor6D") then
                    if v.Part0 == oldRoot then v.Part0 = clone end
                    if v.Part1 == oldRoot then v.Part1 = clone end
                end
            end
            tempParent:Destroy()
            return true
        end
        return false
    end

    local function revertClone()
        local character = player.Character
        if not oldRoot then return false end
        if not character then return false end
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 then return false end

        if not oldRoot.Parent then return false end

        pcall(function()
            local tempParent = Instance.new("Model")
            tempParent.Parent = game
            character.Parent = tempParent
            oldRoot.Parent = character
            character.PrimaryPart = oldRoot
            character.Parent = Workspace
            oldRoot.CanCollide = true
            for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("Weld") or v:IsA("Motor6D") then
                    if v.Part0 == clone then v.Part0 = oldRoot end
                    if v.Part1 == clone then v.Part1 = oldRoot end
                end
            end
            if clone then
                local oldPos = clone.CFrame
                clone:Destroy()
                clone = nil
                oldRoot.CFrame = oldPos
            end
            oldRoot = nil
            if character and humanoid then
                humanoid.HipHeight = hip
            end
            tempParent:Destroy()
        end)
        clearAllGhosts()
        return true
    end

    local function animationTrickery()
        local character = player.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
            local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
            anim.AnimationId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=18537363391"
            local humanoid = character.Humanoid
            local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") or Instance.new("Animator", humanoid)
            local animTrack = animator:LoadAnimation(anim)
            animTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
            animTrack:Play(0, 1, 0)
            anim:Destroy()
            table.insert(tracks, animTrack)
            animTrack.Stopped:Connect(function()
                if animPlaying then animationTrickery() end
            end)
            task.delay(0, function()
                animTrack.TimePosition = 0.7
                task.delay(0.3, function()
                    if animTrack then animTrack:AdjustSpeed(math.huge) end
                end)
            end)
        end
    end

    local function turnOff()
        clearAllGhosts()
        animPlaying = false
        _G.invisibleStealEnabled = false

        for _, track in pairs(tracks) do
            pcall(function() track:Stop(0) end)
        end
        tracks = {}

        if connection then pcall(function() connection:Disconnect() end) connection = nil end
        if jumpConn then pcall(function() jumpConn:Disconnect() end) jumpConn = nil end
        for _, conn in ipairs(folderConnections) do
            pcall(function() if conn then conn:Disconnect() end end)
        end
        folderConnections = {}

        pcall(revertClone)
        clearAllGhosts()

        -- force stop all animations and reset character state
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                pcall(function()
                    local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
                    if animator then
                        for _, track in pairs(animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                            track:Stop(0)
                        end
                    end
                end)
                pcall(function() humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp) end)
                pcall(function() humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running) end)
            end
            -- destroy any leftover cloned root parts in camera
            pcall(function()
                for _, child in pairs(workspace.CurrentCamera:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
                        child:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end)
            -- re-parent character properly if needed
            pcall(function()
                if character.Parent ~= workspace then
                    character.Parent = workspace
                end
            end)
        end

        if _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle then
            pcall(function() _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle(false) end)
        end
        if _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual then
            pcall(function() _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual(false) end)
        end
    end

    local function turnOn()
        if animPlaying then return end
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid then return end
        animPlaying = true
        _G.invisibleStealEnabled = true
        if _G.AutoStealDisableAnimEnabled then
            _G.AutoStealDisableAnimEnabled = false
            if _G.stopAnimDisable then pcall(_G.stopAnimDisable) end
            if _G.updateUnwalkPanelVisual then pcall(_G.updateUnwalkPanelVisual, false) end
        end
        if _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual then
            pcall(function() _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual(true) end)
        end
        tracks = {}
        removeFolders()
        local sinkAmount = (_G.SinkSliderValue or SINK_AMOUNT) * 0.5
        local success = doClone()
        if success then
            task.wait(0.05)
            animationTrickery()
            task.defer(function()
                if _G.resetBrainrotBeam then pcall(_G.resetBrainrotBeam) end
                if _G.resetPlotBeam then pcall(_G.resetPlotBeam) end
                task.wait(0.1)
                if _G.updateBrainrotBeam then pcall(_G.updateBrainrotBeam) end
                if _G.createPlotBeam then pcall(_G.createPlotBeam) end
            end)
            local function calculateAutoRotation()
                if not _G.AutoRotateInvis then return _G.InvisStealAngle or 180 end
                local char = player.Character
                if not char then return 180 end
                local minY, maxY = math.huge, -math.huge
                local maxHorizontal = 0
                for _, part in pairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and part ~= clone then
                        local size = part.Size
                        local pos = part.Position
                        minY = math.min(minY, pos.Y - size.Y/2)
                        maxY = math.max(maxY, pos.Y + size.Y/2)
                        maxHorizontal = math.max(maxHorizontal, size.X, size.Z)
                    end
                end
                local modelHeight = maxY - minY
                if modelHeight <= 0 then return 180 end
                local sinkAmount = (_G.SinkSliderValue or SINK_AMOUNT) * 0.5
                local angle
                if sinkAmount >= modelHeight then
                    angle = 180
                else
                    local ratio = math.min(1, sinkAmount / modelHeight)
                    angle = 180 + math.deg(math.asin(1 - ratio)) + 15
                    angle = math.clamp(angle, 180, 270)
                end
                if _G.updateRotationSliderUI then
                    pcall(_G.updateRotationSliderUI, angle)
                end
                return angle
            end
            local jumpHeld = false
            jumpConn = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
                if gameProcessed then return end
                if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
                    jumpHeld = true
                end
            end)
            local jumpEndConn = UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
                    jumpHeld = false
                end
            end)
            table.insert(folderConnections, jumpEndConn)
            local jumpLoopConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if jumpHeld and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    local root = character.PrimaryPart or character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if root then
                        root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.X, humanoid.JumpPower or 50, root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Z)
                    end
                end
            end)
            table.insert(folderConnections, jumpLoopConn)
            local lastSetPosition = nil
            local skipFrames = 5
            connection = RunService.PreSimulation:Connect(function(dt)
                if character and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and oldRoot then
                    local root = character.PrimaryPart or character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if root then
                        if skipFrames > 0 then
                            skipFrames = skipFrames - 1
                            lastSetPosition = nil
                        elseif lastSetPosition and ghostEnabled then
                            local currentPos = oldRoot.Position
                            local jumpDistance = (currentPos - lastSetPosition).Magnitude
                            if jumpDistance > 3 and not _G.RecoveryInProgress then
                                lastSetPosition = nil
                                createServerGhost(currentPos)
                                if _G.AutoRecoverLagback and _G.toggleInvisibleSteal then
                                    _G.RecoveryInProgress = true
                                    task.spawn(function()
                                        pcall(_G.toggleInvisibleSteal)
                                        task.wait(0.5)
                                        pcall(_G.toggleInvisibleSteal)
                                        _G.RecoveryInProgress = false
                                    end)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        if clone then
                            clone.CanCollide = false
                        end
                        if oldRoot then
                            for _, child in pairs(oldRoot:GetChildren()) do
                                if child:IsA("Attachment") or child:IsA("Beam") then
                                    child:Destroy()
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        if not oldRoot then return end

                        local rotationAngle = _G.AutoRotateInvis and calculateAutoRotation() or (_G.InvisStealAngle or 180)
                        local defaultDepth = character.Humanoid.HipHeight + (root.Size.Y / 2) - 1 + 0.09
                        local sinkAmount = (_G.SinkSliderValue or 5) * 0.5
                        local cf = root.CFrame - Vector3.new(0, sinkAmount, 0)
                        oldRoot.CFrame = cf * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(rotationAngle), 0, 0)
                        oldRoot.Velocity = root.Velocity
                        oldRoot.CanCollide = false
                        lastSetPosition = oldRoot.Position
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        if _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle then
            pcall(function() _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle(true) end)
        end
    end

    _G.toggleInvisibleSteal = function()
        if animPlaying then
            turnOff()
        else
            if not player:GetAttribute("Stealing") then return end
            turnOn()
        end
    end

    _G.forceStopInvis = function()
        if animPlaying then
            turnOff()
        end
    end

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        if UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() then return end
        if input.KeyCode == (_G.INVISIBLE_STEAL_KEY or Enum.KeyCode.U) then
            pcall(_G.toggleInvisibleSteal)
            if _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual then
                pcall(_G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual, _G.invisibleStealEnabled or false)
            end
        end
    end)

    local function onCharacterAdded(newChar)
        clearErrorOrb()
        clearAllGhosts()
        lagbackCallCount = 0
        pcall(function()
            for _, child in pairs(Workspace.CurrentCamera:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end)
        if oldRoot then
            pcall(function() oldRoot:Destroy() end)
            oldRoot = nil
        end
        if clone then
            pcall(function() clone:Destroy() end)
            clone = nil
        end
        animPlaying = false
        _G.invisibleStealEnabled = false
        if _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual then
            pcall(function() _G.updateMovementPanelInvisVisual(false) end)
        end
        if _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle then
            pcall(function() _G.updateStealPanelInvisToggle(false) end)
        end
        task.wait(0.2)
        local camera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
        if camera and newChar then
            local newHumanoid = newChar:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if newHumanoid then
                camera.CameraSubject = newHumanoid
                camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
            end
        end
    end
    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(onCharacterAdded)

    local function setupDeathListener()
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                    clearErrorOrb()
                    clearAllGhosts()
                    lagbackCallCount = 0
                end)
            end
        end
    end
    setupDeathListener()
    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        task.wait(0.1)
        setupDeathListener()
    end)

end)

if _G.STEAL_MODE == nil then _G.STEAL_MODE = nil end
if _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled == nil then _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled = false end
_G.PreFireDistance = _G.PreFireDistance or 20
_G.PREDICTION_LOOKAHEAD = _G.PREDICTION_LOOKAHEAD or 1.6

if _G.AutoWalkspeedAfterSteal == nil then _G.AutoWalkspeedAfterSteal = false end
if _G.autoKickEnabled == nil then _G.autoKickEnabled = false end
if _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal == nil then _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal = false end
if _G.AutoUnlockBaseAfterSteal == nil then _G.AutoUnlockBaseAfterSteal = false end

local function isPathBlocked(player, targetPart)
	local character = player.Character
	if not character then return true end

	local humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if not humanoidRootPart then return true end

	local origin = humanoidRootPart.Position
	local direction = targetPart.Position - origin
	local remainingDistance = direction.Magnitude
	local unitDirection = direction.Unit

	local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
	raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
	raycastParams.IgnoreWater = true

	local ignoreList = {character}

	while remainingDistance > 0 do
		raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = ignoreList

		local raycastResult = workspace:Raycast(origin, unitDirection * remainingDistance, raycastParams)

		if not raycastResult then
			return false
		end

		if raycastResult.Instance == targetPart then
			return false
		end

		local hit = raycastResult.Instance

		if hit.Name == "StealHitbox"
			or hit.Name == "Hitbox"
            or hit.Name == "DeliveryHitbox"
			or (hit.Name == "structure base home" and hit.Size.Z == 2)
			or string.find(hit:GetFullName(), "AnimalPodiums")
            or string.find(hit:GetFullName(), "Decorations")
		then
			table.insert(ignoreList, hit)
			origin = raycastResult.Position + unitDirection * 0.01
			remainingDistance = (targetPart.Position - origin).Magnitude
		else
			print(hit.Name)
			print(hit:GetFullName())
			return true
		end
	end

	return false
end

player:GetAttributeChangedSignal("StealingIndex"):Connect(function()
	local currentValue = player:GetAttribute("StealingIndex")

    if previousValue ~= nil and currentValue == nil and _G.AutoTpBackAfterHit == true then
        print(isPathBlocked(player, CurrentRoot))
        if not isPathBlocked(player, CurrentRoot) then
            TeleportBack()
        end
	end

	previousValue = currentValue
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local LastPlayerPosition = nil
    local PlayerVelocity = Vector3.zero
    local InternalStealCache = {}
    local StealInProgress = false

    local debrisScanCache = {}
    local debrisScanCacheTime = 0

    local function getHRP()
        local c = player.Character
        if not c then return nil end
        return c:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    end

    local function scanDebrisForSteal()
        local currentTime = tick()
        if (currentTime - debrisScanCacheTime) < 0.05 and #debrisScanCache > 0 then
            local validCache = true
            for _, item in ipairs(debrisScanCache) do
                if not item.part or not item.part.Parent then
                    validCache = false
                    break
                end
            end
            if validCache then return debrisScanCache end
        end
        local results = {}
        local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
        if not debrisFolder then
            debrisScanCache = results
            debrisScanCacheTime = currentTime
            return results
        end
        local myPlot = nil
        local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
        if plotsFolder then
            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local gui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                    if gui then
                        local lbl = gui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                        if lbl and lbl.Text then
                            local t = lbl.Text:lower()
                            if t:find(player.Name:lower(), 1, true) or t:find(player.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                myPlot = plot
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        local plotOwners = {}
        if plotsFolder then
            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local gui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                    if gui then
                        local lbl = gui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                        if lbl and lbl.Text then
                            local ownerInGame = false
                            for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                                if lbl.Text:lower():find(p.Name:lower(), 1, true) or
                                lbl.Text:lower():find(p.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                    ownerInGame = true
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            plotOwners[plot] = {
                                position = plot:GetPivot().Position,
                                ownerInGame = ownerInGame,
                                isMyPlot = (plot == myPlot)
                            }
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        local hrp = getHRP()
        local playerPos = hrp and hrp.Position or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                local distFromPlayer = (obj.Position - playerPos).Magnitude
                if distFromPlayer > 350 then continue end
                local closestPlot, closestPlotDist = nil, math.huge
                for plot, data in pairs(plotOwners) do
                    local dx = obj.Position.X - data.position.X
                    local dz = obj.Position.Z - data.position.Z
                    local dist = math.sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                    if dist < closestPlotDist then
                        closestPlotDist = dist
                        closestPlot = plot
                    end
                end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and plotOwners[closestPlot].isMyPlot then continue end
                if closestPlotDist > 300 then continue end
                if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and not plotOwners[closestPlot].ownerInGame then continue end
                local displayNameLabel, generationLabel = nil, nil
                for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                        for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                            if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                if label.Name == "DisplayName" then displayNameLabel = label
                                elseif label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then generationLabel = label end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if displayNameLabel and generationLabel then
                    local genText = string.lower(generationLabel.Text or "0")
                    local petValue = parsePetValue(genText)
                    table.insert(results, {
                        part = obj,
                        name = displayNameLabel.Text or "Unknown",
                        genValue = petValue,
                        value = petValue,
                        position = obj.Position - Vector3.new(0, 11, 0),
                        closestPlot = closestPlot,
                        cachedPrompt = nil
                    })
                end
            end
        end
        debrisScanCache = results
        debrisScanCacheTime = tick()
        return results
    end

    _G.scanDebrisForSteal = scanDebrisForSteal

    local function findPromptAndInfo(position, targetData)
        if targetData and targetData.directPrompt and targetData.directPrompt.Parent then
            return targetData.directPrompt, nil, nil
        end
        if targetData and targetData.cachedPrompt and targetData.cachedPrompt.Parent then
            return targetData.cachedPrompt, nil, nil
        end
        local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
        local closestPrompt, closestPlotName, closestSlot = nil, nil, nil
        local closestDist = 15
        if plotsFolder then
            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local podiums = plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums")
                if podiums then
                    for _, podium in ipairs(podiums:GetChildren()) do
                        local podiumPos = podium:GetPivot().Position
                        local dist = (podiumPos - position).Magnitude
                        if dist < closestDist then
                            local base = podium:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                local spawn = base:FindFirstChild("Spawn")
                                if spawn then
                                    local attach = spawn:FindFirstChild("PromptAttachment")
                                    if attach then
                                        for _, p in ipairs(attach:GetChildren()) do
                                            if p:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                                closestPrompt = p
                                                closestPlotName = plot.Name
                                                closestSlot = tonumber(podium.Name)
                                                closestDist = dist
                                                if targetData then targetData.cachedPrompt = p end
                                                break
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
        if debrisFolder and not closestPrompt then
            for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local objPos = obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Position or (obj:IsA("Model") and obj:GetPivot().Position or nil)
                if objPos then
                    local dist = (objPos - position).Magnitude
                    if dist < closestDist then
                        for _, desc in ipairs(obj:GetDescendants()) do
                            if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                closestPrompt = desc
                                closestDist = dist
                                closestPlotName = nil
                                closestSlot = nil
                                if targetData then targetData.cachedPrompt = desc end
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        return closestPrompt, closestPlotName, closestSlot
    end
    
    local function getBestTarget()
        local debrisPets = scanDebrisForSteal()
        local stealMode = _G.STEAL_MODE
        local hrp = getHRP()

        if not hrp then return nil end
        if #debrisPets == 0 then return nil end
        if not stealMode then return nil end

        if stealMode == "Nearest" then
            local bestNearest, bestNearestDist = nil, math.huge
            for _, petData in ipairs(debrisPets) do
                if petData.part and petData.part.Parent then
                    local dist = (hrp.Position - petData.position).Magnitude
                    if dist < bestNearestDist then
                        bestNearest = petData
                        bestNearestDist = dist
                    end
                end
            end
            return bestNearest

        elseif stealMode == "Priority" then
            local priorityList = _G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS or {}
            if #priorityList == 0 then return nil end

            local bestPriority, bestPriorityLevel, bestPriorityValue = nil, 999, 0
            for _, petData in ipairs(debrisPets) do
                local lowerName = (petData.name or ""):lower()
                for idx, priorityName in ipairs(priorityList) do
                    if lowerName:find(priorityName:lower(), 1, true) then
                        if idx < bestPriorityLevel then
                            bestPriority = petData
                            bestPriorityLevel = idx
                            bestPriorityValue = petData.genValue
                        elseif idx == bestPriorityLevel and petData.genValue > bestPriorityValue then
                            bestPriority = petData
                            bestPriorityValue = petData.genValue
                        end
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            if bestPriority then return bestPriority end
            -- Fallback to highest if no priority match
            local bestHighest, bestHighestValue = nil, 0
            for _, petData in ipairs(debrisPets) do
                if petData.genValue > bestHighestValue then
                    bestHighest = petData
                    bestHighestValue = petData.genValue
                end
            end
            return bestHighest

        elseif stealMode == "Highest" then
            -- XenHub approach: find all matching highest, pick closest in prefire range
            if #debrisPets == 0 then return nil end
            table.sort(debrisPets, function(a, b) return a.genValue > b.genValue end)
            local highestValue = debrisPets[1].genValue
            if highestValue <= 0 then return nil end
            local matchingAnimals = {}
            for _, petData in ipairs(debrisPets) do
                if petData.genValue == highestValue and petData.part and petData.part.Parent then
                    table.insert(matchingAnimals, petData)
                end
            end
            if #matchingAnimals == 0 then return nil end
            if #matchingAnimals == 1 then return matchingAnimals[1] end
            -- Pick closest one
            local bestTarget, bestDist = nil, math.huge
            for _, petData in ipairs(matchingAnimals) do
                local dist = (hrp.Position - petData.position).Magnitude
                if dist < bestDist then
                    bestDist = dist
                    bestTarget = petData
                end
            end
            return bestTarget
        end

        return nil
    end

    _G.getBestStealTarget = getBestTarget

    local function buildCallbacks(prompt)
        if callbackCache[prompt] then return callbackCache[prompt] end
        local data = { hold = {}, holdEnd = {}, trig = {} }
        pcall(function()
            for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(prompt.PromptButtonHoldBegan)) do
                if type(c.Function) == "function" then
                    table.insert(data.hold, c.Function)
                end
            end
        end)
        pcall(function()
            for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(prompt.PromptButtonHoldEnded)) do
                if type(c.Function) == "function" then
                    table.insert(data.holdEnd, c.Function)
                end
            end
        end)
        pcall(function()
            for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(prompt.Triggered)) do
                if type(c.Function) == "function" then
                    table.insert(data.trig, c.Function)
                end
            end
        end)
        callbackCache[prompt] = data
        return data
    end

local StealData = {}

    local function executeSteal(prompt, name, distance)
        if isStealing then return end
        if not StealData[prompt] then
            StealData[prompt] = {hold = {}, trigger = {}, ready = true}
            pcall(function()
                if getconnections then
                    for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(prompt.PromptButtonHoldBegan)) do
                        if c.Function then table.insert(StealData[prompt].hold, c.Function) end
                    end
                    for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(prompt.Triggered)) do
                        if c.Function then table.insert(StealData[prompt].trigger, c.Function) end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        local data = StealData[prompt]
        if not data.ready then return end
        data.ready = false
        isStealing = true
        task.spawn(function()
            for _, f in ipairs(data.hold) do task.spawn(f) end
            task.wait(1.3)
            for _, f in ipairs(data.trigger) do task.spawn(f) end
            data.ready = true
            isStealing = false
        end)
    end


    -- Pre-cache steal callbacks in background (xen approach)
    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait(0.05) do
            if _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled or _G.STEAL_MODE then
                local debrisPets = scanDebrisForSteal()
                for _, petData in ipairs(debrisPets) do
                    if petData.part and petData.part.Parent then
                        local prompt = findPromptAndInfo(petData.position, petData)
                        if prompt and prompt.Parent then
                            buildCallbacks(prompt)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end)

    local hiddenPrompts = {}
    local lastAutoStealUpdate = 0

    --[[
    _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not _G.AutoInstantStealEnabled then
            -- Restore hidden prompts when auto steal is off
            for prompt, _ in pairs(hiddenPrompts) do
                if prompt and prompt.Parent then
                    prompt.Enabled = true
                end
            end
            hiddenPrompts = {}
            _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget = nil
            if not StealInProgress and _G.hideStealProgress then
                pcall(_G.hideStealProgress)
            end
            PreFireSent = false
            PreFireTarget = nil
            return
        end

        if StealInProgress then return end

        local hrp = getHRP()
        if not hrp then _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget = nil return end

        -- Handle pre-selected steal target
        local selectedStealTarget = _G.SelectedStealTarget
        local target = nil

        if selectedStealTarget and selectedStealTarget.part and selectedStealTarget.part.Parent then
            target = selectedStealTarget
        else
            target = getBestTarget()
        end

        if not target then
            _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget = nil
            if not StealInProgress and _G.hideStealProgress then
                pcall(_G.hideStealProgress)
            end
            return
        end

        _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget = target

        local prompt = findPromptAndInfo(target.position, target)
        if prompt then
            prompt.Enabled = false
            hiddenPrompts[prompt] = true
        end

        local dist = (hrp.Position - target.position).Magnitude
        if dist <= RADIUS and prompt then
            CurrentRoot = prompt.Parent.Parent
             executeSteal(prompt, target.name, dist)
        end
    end))
    ]]
    local stealConnection = nil
    local lastTargetCheck = 0
    local checkInterval = 0.02
    local function startLoop()
        if stealConnection then stealConnection:Disconnect() end
        stealConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            local currentTime = tick()
            if currentTime - lastTargetCheck < checkInterval then return end
            lastTargetCheck = currentTime
            local selectedStealTarget = _G.SelectedStealTarget
            local target = nil
            local hrp = getHRP()
            if not hrp then return end
            if selectedStealTarget and selectedStealTarget.part and selectedStealTarget.part.Parent then
                target = selectedStealTarget
            else
                target = getBestTarget()
            end
            if not target or not target.position then return end
            local dist = (hrp.Position - target.position).Magnitude
            if dist > 65 then return end
            local prompt = findPromptAndInfo(target.position, target)
            if prompt then
                prompt.Enabled = false
                hiddenPrompts[prompt] = true
            end
            if prompt and dist <= RADIUS then
                CurrentRoot = prompt.Parent.Parent
                executeSteal(prompt, target.name, dist)
            end
        end)
    end
    startLoop()

    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(1)
            if not stealConnection or not stealConnection.Connected then
                pcall(startLoop)
            end
        end
    end)
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while _loopFlags.running do
        pcall(function()
            local character = player.Character
            if character then
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    if humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                        humanoid.Health = humanoid.MaxHealth
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        task.wait(0.1)
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local currentConnection = nil

    local function setupAntiDie()
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid then return end
        if currentConnection then
            pcall(function() currentConnection:Disconnect() end)
        end
        currentConnection = humanoid:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Health"):Connect(function()
            if humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                humanoid.Health = humanoid.MaxHealth
            end
        end)
    end

    setupAntiDie()
    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
        task.wait(0.1)
        setupAntiDie()
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()
    local function getClosestPlot()
        local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
        if not plotsFolder then return nil end

        local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not hrp then return nil end

        local closestPlot, closestDist = nil, math.huge
        for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
            local pos = plot:GetPivot().Position
            local dist = (hrp.Position - pos).Magnitude
            if dist < closestDist then
                closestDist = dist
                closestPlot = plot
            end
        end
        return closestPlot
    end

    local function findPromptsRecursive(instance, found)
        for _, child in pairs(instance:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                table.insert(found, child)
            end
            findPromptsRecursive(child, found)
        end
    end

    _G.unlockFloor = function(floorNumber)
        local success, err = pcall(function()
            local targetPlot = getClosestPlot()
            if not targetPlot then
                return
            end
            local unlockFolder = targetPlot:FindFirstChild("Unlock")
            if not unlockFolder then
                return
            end
            local unlockItems = {}
            for _, item in pairs(unlockFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local pos = nil
                if item:IsA("Model") then
                    pcall(function()
                        pos = item:GetPivot().Position
                    end)
                elseif item:IsA("BasePart") then
                    pos = item.Position
                end
                if pos then
                    table.insert(unlockItems, {
                        Object = item,
                        Height = pos.Y
                    })
                end
            end
            table.sort(unlockItems, function(a, b)
                return a.Height < b.Height
            end)
            if floorNumber > #unlockItems then
                return
            end
            local targetFloor = unlockItems[floorNumber].Object
            local prompts = {}
            findPromptsRecursive(targetFloor, prompts)
            if #prompts == 0 then
                return
            end
            for _, prompt in pairs(prompts) do
                if fireproximityprompt then
                    fireproximityprompt(prompt)
                end
            end
        end)
        if not success then
        end
    end

end)

task.spawn(function()
    local STEAL_HOLD_DURATION = 0.55
    local StealProgressActive = false
    local StealStartTime = 0

    _G.StealProgressGui = nil
    _G.StealProgressFrame = nil
    _G.StealProgressFill = nil
    _G.StealProgressText = nil
    _G.StealProgressItemName = nil
    _G.StealProgressBarEnabled = true

    local function createStealProgressBar()
        local existingGui = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("StealProgressGui") or game:GetService("CoreGui"):FindFirstChild("StealProgressGui")
        if existingGui then existingGui:Destroy() end

        local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        ScreenGui.Name = "StealProgressGui"
        ScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        ScreenGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
        ScreenGui.DisplayOrder = 100
        ScreenGui.Parent = game:GetService("CoreGui")
        _G.StealProgressGui = ScreenGui

        local containerWidth = isMobile and 180 or 250
        local containerHeight = isMobile and 38 or 50
        local barHeight = isMobile and 10 or 14
        local fontSize = isMobile and 10 or 13
        local nameLabelHeight = isMobile and 12 or 16
        local barYPos = isMobile and 22 or 28

        local Container = Instance.new("Frame")
        Container.Name = "ProgressContainer"
        Container.Size = UDim2.new(0, containerWidth, 0, containerHeight)
        Container.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -containerWidth/2, 1, -200)
        Container.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 25)
        Container.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15
        Container.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Container.Visible = false
        Container.Parent = ScreenGui
        _G.StealProgressFrame = Container

        Instance.new("UICorner", Container).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)


        local ItemNameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", Container)
        ItemNameLabel.Name = "ItemNameLabel"
        ItemNameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, nameLabelHeight)
        ItemNameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 5)
        ItemNameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        ItemNameLabel.Text = ""
        ItemNameLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        ItemNameLabel.TextSize = fontSize
        ItemNameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        ItemNameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        _G.StealProgressItemName = ItemNameLabel

        local BarTrack = Instance.new("Frame", Container)
        BarTrack.Name = "BarTrack"
        BarTrack.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, barHeight)
        BarTrack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, barYPos)
        BarTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)
        BarTrack.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Instance.new("UICorner", BarTrack).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local BarFill = Instance.new("Frame", BarTrack)
        BarFill.Name = "BarFill"
        BarFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
        BarFill.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        BarFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        BarFill.BorderSizePixel = 0
        _G.StealProgressFill = BarFill
        Instance.new("UICorner", BarFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

        local FillGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient", BarFill)
        local themeColor = _G.CURRENT_UI_COLOR or Color3.fromRGB(99, 102, 241)
        local themeR, themeG, themeB = themeColor.R * 255, themeColor.G * 255, themeColor.B * 255
        FillGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(math.min(themeR * 1.2, 255), math.min(themeG * 1.2, 255), math.min(themeB * 1.2, 255))),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, themeColor),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(themeR * 0.7, themeG * 0.7, themeB * 0.7))
        })
        FillGradient.Rotation = 90

        local PercentText = Instance.new("TextLabel", BarTrack)
        PercentText.Name = "PercentText"
        PercentText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        PercentText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        PercentText.Text = "0%"
        PercentText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        PercentText.TextSize = 14
        PercentText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        PercentText.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
        PercentText.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        PercentText.ZIndex = 2
        _G.StealProgressText = PercentText

        return ScreenGui
    end

    local function formatStealValue(num)
        if not num or num == 0 then return "" end
        if num >= 1e12 then return string.format("%.1fT", num/1e12)
        elseif num >= 1e9 then return string.format("%.1fB", num/1e9)
        elseif num >= 1e6 then return string.format("%.1fM", num/1e6)
        elseif num >= 1e3 then return string.format("%.1fK", num/1e3) end
        return tostring(math.floor(num))
    end

    _G.showStealProgress = function(itemName, itemValue)
        if _G.StealProgressBarEnabled == false then return end
        if not _G.StealProgressFrame then
            createStealProgressBar()
        end
        StealProgressActive = true
        StealStartTime = tick()
        _G.StealProgressFrame.Visible = true
        if _G.StealProgressFill then
            _G.StealProgressFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
        end
        if _G.StealProgressText then
            _G.StealProgressText.Text = "0%"
        end
        if _G.StealProgressItemName then
            local valueStr = formatStealValue(itemValue)
            if valueStr ~= "" then
                _G.StealProgressItemName.Text = (itemName or "Unknown") .. " - " .. valueStr .. "/s"
            else
                _G.StealProgressItemName.Text = itemName or "Unknown"
            end
        end
    end

    _G.hideStealProgress = function()
        StealProgressActive = false
        if _G.StealProgressFrame then
            _G.StealProgressFrame.Visible = false
        end
    end

    local function updateStealProgress()
        if not StealProgressActive then return end
        if not _G.StealProgressFill or not _G.StealProgressText then return end
        local elapsed = tick() - StealStartTime
        local progress = math.clamp(elapsed / STEAL_HOLD_DURATION, 0, 1)
        local percent = math.floor(progress * 100)
        _G.StealProgressFill.Size = UDim2.new(progress, 0, 1, 0)
        _G.StealProgressText.Text = percent .. "%"
        if progress >= 1 then
            task.delay(0.15, function()
                if StealProgressActive and (tick() - StealStartTime) >= STEAL_HOLD_DURATION then
                    _G.hideStealProgress()
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    _track(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(updateStealProgress))
    task.defer(createStealProgressBar)

    -- Auto Turret Indicator
    -- Auto turret indicator removed (was floating at top of screen)
    -- Turret state still tracked internally via _G.autoTurretEnabled

end)

_G.autoKickEnabledTime = tick()

task.spawn(function()
    local playerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui", 10)
    if not playerGui then return end
    local kickTriggered = false

    local function checkTextForSteal(gui)
        if not gui:IsA("TextLabel") and not gui:IsA("TextButton") then return end
        if not gui.Text or gui.Text == "" then return end
        local text = gui.Text:lower()
        if text:find("you%s+stole%s+") then
            -- Debounce per GUI instance: mark it so we don't process same element twice
            if gui:GetAttribute("_stealProcessed") then return end
            pcall(function() gui:SetAttribute("_stealProcessed", true) end)

            local stolenName = gui.Text:match("[Yy]ou%s+stole%s+(.+)") or "something"
            stolenName = stolenName:gsub("<[^>]+>", "")
            stolenName = stolenName:gsub("%s*%([Ee]rror%s+[Cc]ode:?%s*%d+%)%s*", "")
            stolenName = stolenName:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")

            -- Feed steal tracker
            if _G.StealLoggerEnabled and _G.addStolenItemEntry then
                _G.addStolenItemEntry(stolenName, os.time())
            end

            -- Auto kick after steal
            if not kickTriggered and _G.autoKickEnabled then
                local textAppearTime = tick()
                if textAppearTime > _G.autoKickEnabledTime then
                    kickTriggered = true
                    _G.KICK_IN_PROGRESS = true
                    task.wait(0.1)
                    player:Kick("You have successfully stolen " .. stolenName)
                    pcall(function()
                        if not isMobile then
                            game:Shutdown()
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function hookTextChanged(gui)
        if gui:IsA("TextLabel") or gui:IsA("TextButton") then
            pcall(function()
                _track(gui:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
                    -- Reset processed flag so text changes get re-evaluated
                    pcall(function() gui:SetAttribute("_stealProcessed", nil) end)
                    pcall(function() checkTextForSteal(gui) end)
                end))
            end)
        end
    end

    for _, gui in ipairs(playerGui:GetDescendants()) do
        hookTextChanged(gui)
    end

    _track(playerGui.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(gui)
        pcall(function() checkTextForSteal(gui) end)
        hookTextChanged(gui)
    end))
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(30) do
        table.clear(_espCache.brainrot)
        table.clear(_cacheTimestamps)
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    _G.SPEEDBOOST_KEY = _G.CarpetSpeedKey or Enum.KeyCode.Q
    local SpeedBoostEnabled = false
    _G.SpeedBoostEnabled = false
    local SpeedBoostConnection = nil

    local function toggleSpeedBoost()
        SpeedBoostEnabled = not SpeedBoostEnabled
        _G.SpeedBoostEnabled = SpeedBoostEnabled
        _G.CarpetSpeedEnabled = SpeedBoostEnabled

        if SpeedBoostEnabled then
            task.spawn(function()
                local character = player.Character
                if character then
                    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")
                    if humanoid and backpack then
                        local carpet = character:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                        if not carpet then
                            carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                        end

                        if carpet and carpet:IsA("Tool") and carpet.Parent == backpack then
                            humanoid:EquipTool(carpet)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)

            if SpeedBoostConnection then SpeedBoostConnection:Disconnect() SpeedBoostConnection = nil end
            SpeedBoostConnection = _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not SpeedBoostEnabled then return end
                local character = player.Character
                if not character then return end
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end

                local carpet = character:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")

                if not carpet then
                    SpeedBoostEnabled = false
                    _G.SpeedBoostEnabled = false
                    _G.CarpetSpeedEnabled = false
                    SpeedBoostConnection:Disconnect()
                    SpeedBoostConnection = nil
                    return
                end
                local moveDirection = humanoid.MoveDirection
                if moveDirection.Magnitude > 0 then
                    rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(
                        moveDirection.X * _G.CarpetSpeedValue,
                        rootPart.Velocity.Y,
                        moveDirection.Z * _G.CarpetSpeedValue
                    )
                else
                    rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, rootPart.Velocity.Y, 0)
                end
            end))
        else
            if SpeedBoostConnection then
                SpeedBoostConnection:Disconnect()
                SpeedBoostConnection = nil
            end
        end
    end

    _G.toggleCarpetSpeed = toggleSpeedBoost

    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
        SpeedBoostEnabled = false
        _G.SpeedBoostEnabled = false
        if SpeedBoostConnection then
            SpeedBoostConnection:Disconnect()
            SpeedBoostConnection = nil
        end
    end)

    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
        character.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
            if child:IsA("Tool") and child.Name ~= (_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet") then
                if SpeedBoostEnabled then
                    SpeedBoostEnabled = false
                    _G.SpeedBoostEnabled = false
                    if SpeedBoostConnection then
                        SpeedBoostConnection:Disconnect()
                        SpeedBoostConnection = nil
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()
    local antiRagdollConnections = {}
    local antiRagdollCharacter, antiRagdollHumanoid, antiRagdollRootPart, antiRagdollAnimator
    local lastVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    local velocityChangeThreshold = 40
    local velocityMagnitudeThreshold = 25
    local maxVelocity = 15

    local function isFlyingCarpetActive()
        if not antiRagdollCharacter then return false end
        local tool = antiRagdollCharacter:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool")
        if not tool then return false end
        local hrp = antiRagdollCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if hrp then
            for _, obj in ipairs(hrp:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("BodyVelocity") or obj:IsA("BodyPosition") or obj:IsA("BodyGyro") then
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
        return false
    end

    local function isRagdolled()
        if not antiRagdollHumanoid then return false end
        local state = antiRagdollHumanoid:GetState()
        return state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics or state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll or state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.FallingDown or state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp
    end

    local function enableAntiRagdollControls()
        pcall(function()
            local PlayerModule = player:WaitForChild("PlayerScripts"):WaitForChild("PlayerModule", 10)
            require(PlayerModule):GetControls():Enable()
        end)
    end

    local function cleanupRagdoll()
        if not antiRagdollCharacter then return end
        local carpetEquipped = isFlyingCarpetActive()

        local function processChildren(parent)
            for _, obj in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("BallSocketConstraint") or obj:IsA("NoCollisionConstraint") or obj:IsA("HingeConstraint") or (obj:IsA("Attachment") and (obj.Name == "A" or obj.Name == "B")) then
                    obj:Destroy()
                elseif obj:IsA("BodyVelocity") or obj:IsA("BodyPosition") or obj:IsA("BodyGyro") then
                    if not carpetEquipped then obj:Destroy() end
                elseif obj:IsA("Motor6D") then
                    obj.Enabled = true
                elseif obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                    for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("BallSocketConstraint") or child:IsA("NoCollisionConstraint") or child:IsA("HingeConstraint") or child:IsA("Motor6D") then
                            if child:IsA("Motor6D") then child.Enabled = true else child:Destroy() end
                        elseif child:IsA("Attachment") and (child.Name == "A" or child.Name == "B") then
                            child:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        pcall(function() processChildren(antiRagdollCharacter) end)

        if antiRagdollAnimator then
            for _, track in pairs(antiRagdollAnimator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                local animName = track.Animation and track.Animation.Name:lower() or ""
                if animName:find("rag") or animName:find("fall") or animName:find("hurt") or animName:find("down") then
                    track:Stop(0)
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function setupAntiRagdollCharacter(char)
        antiRagdollCharacter = char
        antiRagdollHumanoid = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
        antiRagdollRootPart = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
        antiRagdollAnimator = antiRagdollHumanoid and antiRagdollHumanoid:WaitForChild("Animator", 10)
        lastVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    end

    local function clearAntiRagdollConnections()
        for _, connection in pairs(antiRagdollConnections) do
            pcall(function() connection:Disconnect() end)
        end
        antiRagdollConnections = {}
    end

    local function setupAntiRagdollConnections()
        clearAntiRagdollConnections()
        if not antiRagdollHumanoid or not antiRagdollRootPart then return end

        table.insert(antiRagdollConnections, antiRagdollHumanoid.StateChanged:Connect(function()
            if (_G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled) and isRagdolled() then
                if not isFlyingCarpetActive() then
                    antiRagdollHumanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
                end
                cleanupRagdoll()
                workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = antiRagdollHumanoid
                enableAntiRagdollControls()
            end
        end))

        pcall(function()
            local impulsePath = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Packages")
            if impulsePath then
                impulsePath = impulsePath:FindFirstChild("Net")
                if impulsePath then
                    impulsePath = impulsePath:FindFirstChild("RE/CombatService/ApplyImpulse")
                    if impulsePath then
                        table.insert(antiRagdollConnections, impulsePath.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
                            if (_G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled) and isRagdolled() then
                                antiRagdollRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                            end
                        end))
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        table.insert(antiRagdollConnections, antiRagdollCharacter.DescendantAdded:Connect(function()
            if (_G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled) and isRagdolled() then
                cleanupRagdoll()
            end
        end))

        table.insert(antiRagdollConnections, RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if (_G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled) and isRagdolled() then
