                cleanupRagdoll()
                local velocity = antiRagdollRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity
                if (velocity - lastVelocity).Magnitude > velocityChangeThreshold and velocity.Magnitude > velocityMagnitudeThreshold then
                    antiRagdollRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = velocity.Unit * math.min(velocity.Magnitude, maxVelocity)
                end
                lastVelocity = velocity
            end
        end))

        enableAntiRagdollControls()
        cleanupRagdoll()
    end

    _G.toggleAntiRagdoll = function(enabled)
        _G.AntiRagdollEnabled = enabled
        _G.antiKnockbackEnabled = enabled
        if enabled then
            if player.Character then
                setupAntiRagdollCharacter(player.Character)
                setupAntiRagdollConnections()
            end
        else
            clearAntiRagdollConnections()
        end
    end

    _G.enableAntiKnockback = function()
        _G.AntiRagdollEnabled = true
        _G.antiKnockbackEnabled = true
        if player.Character then
            setupAntiRagdollCharacter(player.Character)
            setupAntiRagdollConnections()
        end
    end

    _G.disableAntiKnockback = function()
        _G.AntiRagdollEnabled = false
        _G.antiKnockbackEnabled = false
        clearAntiRagdollConnections()
    end

    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        clearAntiRagdollConnections()
        antiRagdollCharacter = nil
        antiRagdollHumanoid = nil
        antiRagdollRootPart = nil
        antiRagdollAnimator = nil
        local humanoid = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
        local rootPart = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
        if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end
        task.wait(0.2)
        setupAntiRagdollCharacter(char)
        if _G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled then
            _G.AntiRagdollEnabled = true
            _G.antiKnockbackEnabled = true
            setupAntiRagdollConnections()
        end
    end)

    if player.Character then
        setupAntiRagdollCharacter(player.Character)
        if _G.AntiRagdollEnabled or _G.antiKnockbackEnabled then
            setupAntiRagdollConnections()
        end
    end

end)

task.spawn(function()
    task.wait(1) -- Wait for other systems to initialize

    local lastRejoinAttempt = 0
    local REJOIN_COOLDOWN = 3 -- seconds

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
        if processed then return end
        if UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() then return end
        if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end

        local keyCode = input.KeyCode

        if keyCode == (_G.RejoinCurrentServerKey or Enum.KeyCode.Semicolon) then
            if tick() - lastRejoinAttempt < REJOIN_COOLDOWN then
                return
            end
            lastRejoinAttempt = tick()

            if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
            local _ts = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            --pcall(function() _ts:SetTeleportData({Keybinds = _G.savedBinds}) end)
            --pcall(function() _ts:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, player) end)
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.RejoinPrivateServerKey or Enum.KeyCode.K) then
            if tick() - lastRejoinAttempt < REJOIN_COOLDOWN then
                return
            end
            lastRejoinAttempt = tick()

            if _G.saveKeybinds then pcall(_G.saveKeybinds) end
            if _G.autoSavePositions then pcall(_G.autoSavePositions) end
            local teleportInfo = {Keybinds = _G.savedBinds}

            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function()
                --TeleportService:SetTeleportData(teleportInfo)
                TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, player)
            end)

            if not success then
                pcall(function()
                    TeleportService:Teleport(game.PlaceId, player, teleportInfo)
                end)
            end
        end

if keyCode == (_G.ResetCharacterKey or Enum.KeyCode.X) then
            if _G.instantReset then
                _G.instantReset()
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.FloatKey or Enum.KeyCode.B) then
            if _G.toggleFloat then
                pcall(_G.toggleFloat)
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.WalkspeedKey or Enum.KeyCode.V) then
            if _G.toggleWalkspeed then
                pcall(_G.toggleWalkspeed)
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.dxhub_GUI_TOGGLE_KEY or _G.OpenGUIKey or Enum.KeyCode.RightControl) then
            local dxhubGui = nil
                pcall(function() dxhubGui = cloneref(game:GetService("CoreGui")):FindFirstChild("22SHubGui") end)
                if not dxhubGui then dxhubGui = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("22SHubGui") end
                if not dxhubGui then dxhubGui = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("22SHub") end
            if dxhubGui then
                local mainFrame = dxhubGui:FindFirstChild("MainFrame")
                if mainFrame then
                    mainFrame.Visible = not mainFrame.Visible
                end
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.ProximityKey or Enum.KeyCode.P) then
            if _G.toggleProximity then
                pcall(_G.toggleProximity)
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.ManualTPKey or Enum.KeyCode.O) then
            warn("[dxhub] Manual TP key pressed. TeleportToHighest=" .. tostring(_G.TeleportToHighest ~= nil) .. " isTeleporting=" .. tostring(_G.isTeleporting))
            if _G.TeleportToHighest and not _G.isTeleporting then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local ok, err = pcall(_G.TeleportToHighest, true)
                    if not ok then
                        warn("[dxhub] TeleportToHighest error: " .. tostring(err))
                        _G.isTeleporting = false
                    end
                end)
                task.delay(3, function()
                    _G.isTeleporting = false
                end)
            end
        end


        if keyCode == (_G.AutoTurretKey or Enum.KeyCode.G) then
            if not _G.isTeleporting then
                _G.autoTurretEnabled = not _G.autoTurretEnabled
                _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal = _G.autoTurretEnabled
                if _G.autoTurretEnabled and _G.scanExistingSentries then
                    pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                end
            end
        end

        if keyCode == (_G.CarpetSpeedKey or Enum.KeyCode.Q) then
            if _G.toggleCarpetSpeed then
                pcall(_G.toggleCarpetSpeed)
            end
        end
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()
    if _G.dxhub_InfJumpActive then return end
    _G.dxhub_InfJumpActive = true

    if _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled == nil then _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled = true end


    local JUMP_POWER = 52
    local JUMP_COOLDOWN = 0.1
    local VELOCITY_BLEND = 0.35
    local FALLING_BOOST = 1.3
    local MAX_VELOCITY = 75

    local isHoldingSpace = false
    local lastJumpTime = 0
    local cachedCharacter = nil
    local cachedHumanoid = nil
    local cachedRootPart = nil

    local function updateCache()
        cachedCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
        if cachedCharacter then
            cachedHumanoid = cachedCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            cachedRootPart = cachedCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        else
            cachedHumanoid = nil
            cachedRootPart = nil
        end
    end

    local function performSmoothJump()
        if _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled == false then return end
        if not cachedHumanoid or not cachedRootPart then
            updateCache()
            if not cachedHumanoid or not cachedRootPart then return end
        end
        if not cachedRootPart.Parent then
            updateCache()
            return
        end

        local currentTime = tick()
        if currentTime - lastJumpTime < JUMP_COOLDOWN then
            return
        end

        if cachedHumanoid.Health <= 0 then return end

        local state = cachedHumanoid:GetState()
        if state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead or
           state == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics then
            return
        end

        local currentVelocity = cachedRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity
        local currentY = currentVelocity.Y
        local targetPower = JUMP_POWER

        if currentY < -10 then
            targetPower = JUMP_POWER * FALLING_BOOST
        elseif currentY < 0 then
            targetPower = JUMP_POWER * (1 + (FALLING_BOOST - 1) * (math.abs(currentY) / 10))
        end

        local blendedY
        if currentY > 0 then
            blendedY = currentY * VELOCITY_BLEND + targetPower * (1 - VELOCITY_BLEND)
        else
            blendedY = targetPower
        end

        blendedY = math.min(blendedY, MAX_VELOCITY)
        cachedRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(currentVelocity.X, blendedY, currentVelocity.Z)
        lastJumpTime = currentTime
    end

    local frameCounter = 0
    local framesPerJump = 6

    _track(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not isHoldingSpace then
            frameCounter = 0
            return
        end
        frameCounter = frameCounter + 1
        if frameCounter >= framesPerJump then
            frameCounter = 0
            performSmoothJump()
        end
    end))

    _track(UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
        if processed then return end
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
            isHoldingSpace = true
            performSmoothJump()
        end
    end))

    UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input, processed)
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
            isHoldingSpace = false
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.JumpRequest:Connect(function()
        if _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled == false then return end
        performSmoothJump()
    end)

    local function setupInfiniteJump()
        updateCache()
        if not cachedHumanoid then return end
        pcall(function()
            cachedHumanoid.Jumping:Connect(function()
                if isHoldingSpace then
                    task.defer(performSmoothJump)
                end
            end)
        end)
    end

    task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(0.1)
        while _loopFlags.running do
            if isHoldingSpace then
                performSmoothJump()
            end
            task.wait(0.12)
        end
    end)

    if LocalPlayer.Character then
        setupInfiniteJump()
    end

    LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
        char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
        task.wait(0.1)
        updateCache()
        setupInfiniteJump()
    end)

    _G.toggleInfiniteJump = function()
        _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled = not _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled
        return _G.InfiniteJumpEnabled
    end

end)

task.defer(function()
    warn("[dxhub] TP task.spawn starting...")
    local workspace = workspace

    if _G.autoTPButtonEnabled == nil then _G.autoTPButtonEnabled = false end
    if _G.AutoCloneAfterTP == nil then _G.AutoCloneAfterTP = false end
    if _G.AutoTpBackAfterHit == nil then _G.AutoTpBackAfterHit = false end
    if _G.TPDirectlyToPet == nil then _G.TPDirectlyToPet = true end
    if _G.AutoFloatThirdFloor == nil then _G.AutoFloatThirdFloor = true end
    _G.AutoTPClosestPlayer = _G.AutoTPClosestPlayer or false
    _G.AutoTPOwnerOnly = _G.AutoTPOwnerOnly or false
    _G.TPSpeedItem = _G.TeleportSpeedItem or _G.TPSpeedItem or "Santa's Sleigh"
    if _G.autoCarpetPulloutEnabled == nil then _G.autoCarpetPulloutEnabled = true end
    _G.AutoTPTargetPosition = nil
    _G.AutoTPTargetPlotSign = nil
    _G.skipAutoCloneAfterTP = false
    _G.insideBaseTPHandledSpawn = false

    _G.getAutoTPState = function() return _G.autoTPButtonEnabled or false end
    _G.setAutoTPState = function(enabled)
        _G.autoTPButtonEnabled = enabled
        _G.AutoTeleportEnabled = enabled
    end

    local ParseGenerationValue = parsePetValue -- use top-level utility function

    local function findAncestorOfClass(instance, className)
        local parent = instance.Parent
        while parent and parent ~= game do
            if parent:IsA(className) then
                return parent
            end
            parent = parent.Parent
        end
        return nil
    end


    local function TeleportToHighest(isManualTP)
        if _G.isTeleporting == true then return end

        _G.isTeleporting = true
        warn("[dxhub] TeleportToHighest called, isManual=" .. tostring(isManualTP))
        local success, err = pcall(function()
        local function getCharacter()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                return char, char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            end
            return nil, nil
        end
        local character, hrp = getCharacter()
        if not character or not hrp then warn("[dxhub] TP abort: no character/hrp") _G.isTeleporting = false return end

local speedLevel = math.clamp(_G.TeleportSpeedLevel or 4, 0, 4)
local waitMultipliers = {3, 2, 1.5, 1, 0.7}
        local waitMult = waitMultipliers[speedLevel + 1]
        local powerMultipliers = {0.5, 0.75, 1, 1.5, 2.1}
        local powerMult = powerMultipliers[speedLevel + 1]


        local function TPWait(seconds)
            task.wait(seconds * waitMult)
        end

        local playerGui = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
        local teleportMsg = nil
        local msgLabel = nil
        if playerGui then
            local oldMsg = playerGui:FindFirstChild("TeleportMessage")
            if oldMsg then oldMsg:Destroy() end
        end
        local function createMessageBox()
            if teleportMsg or not playerGui then return end
            teleportMsg = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
            teleportMsg.Name = "TeleportMessage"
            teleportMsg.ResetOnSpawn = false
            teleportMsg.Parent = playerGui
            msgLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            msgLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 400, 0, 80)
            msgLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -200, 0.08, 0)
            msgLabel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
            msgLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            msgLabel.Text = ""
            msgLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(170, 0, 255)
            msgLabel.TextTransparency = 1
            msgLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 1
            msgLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            msgLabel.TextSize = 24
            msgLabel.Parent = teleportMsg
            local msgCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
            msgCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            msgCorner.Parent = msgLabel
        end
        local function fadeIn()
            if not msgLabel then return end
            for i = 1, 5 do
                msgLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 - (i * 0.14)
                msgLabel.TextTransparency = 1 - (i * 0.2)
                msgLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 1 - (i * 0.1)
                task.wait(0.01)
            end
        end
        local function fadeOutAndDestroy()
            if not msgLabel then return end
            for i = 1, 5 do
                msgLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 + (i * 0.14)
                msgLabel.TextTransparency = i * 0.2
                msgLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5 + (i * 0.1)
                task.wait(0.01)
            end
            if teleportMsg and teleportMsg.Parent then
                teleportMsg:Destroy()
            end
        end

        local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
        local debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")

        local debrisWait = 0
        while debrisWait < 0.5 do
            local debris = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
            if debris and #debris:GetChildren() > 0 then break end
            task.wait(0.1)
            debrisWait = debrisWait + 0.1
        end

        local myPlotSign = nil
        local myPlot = nil
        debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
        warn("[dxhub] Plots: " .. tostring(plotsFolder ~= nil) .. ", Debris: " .. tostring(debrisFolder ~= nil) .. " children: " .. tostring(debrisFolder and #debrisFolder:GetChildren() or 0))
        if plotsFolder then
            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                    if surfaceGui then
                        local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                        if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                            local text = textLabel.Text:lower()
                            if (LocalPlayer.Name and text:find(LocalPlayer.Name:lower(), 1, true)) or
                               (LocalPlayer.DisplayName and text:find(LocalPlayer.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true)) then
                                myPlotSign = plotSign
                                myPlot = plot
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local plotOwners = {}
        if plotsFolder then
            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local plotPos = plot:GetPivot().Position
                    local surfaceGui = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceGui", true)
                    if surfaceGui then
                        local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
                        if textLabel and textLabel.Text then
                            local ownerText = textLabel.Text
                            local ownerInGame = false
                            for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                                if ownerText:lower():find(player.Name:lower(), 1, true) or
                                   ownerText:lower():find(player.DisplayName:lower(), 1, true) then
                                    ownerInGame = true
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            plotOwners[plot] = {
                                position = plotPos,
                                ownerInGame = ownerInGame,
                                isMyPlot = (plot == myPlot)
                            }
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

local FENCE_POSITIONS = {
            Vector3.new(-411.4, -5.5, -137.6), Vector3.new(-411.9, -5.5, -123.4),
            Vector3.new(-412.4, -5.5, -106.2), Vector3.new(-412.9, -5.5, -89.3),
            Vector3.new(-412.4, -5.5, -72.1), Vector3.new(-411.8, -5.5, -55),
            Vector3.new(-411.6, -5.5, -37.8), Vector3.new(-411.4, -5.5, -20.8),
            Vector3.new(-411.2, -5.5, -3.7), Vector3.new(-410.9, -5.5, 13.4),
            Vector3.new(-410.7, -5.5, 30.4), Vector3.new(-410.8, -5.5, 47.6),
            Vector3.new(-410.9, -5.5, 64.7), Vector3.new(-411, -5.5, 81.9),
            Vector3.new(-411.1, -5.5, 98.9), Vector3.new(-411.2, -5.5, 115.9),
            Vector3.new(-411.3, -5.5, 132.9), Vector3.new(-411.4, -5.5, 150.1),
            Vector3.new(-411.5, -5.5, 167.3), Vector3.new(-411.6, -5.5, 184.3),
            Vector3.new(-411.7, -5.5, 201.4), Vector3.new(-411.8, -5.5, 218.6),
            Vector3.new(-411.9, -5.5, 235.6), Vector3.new(-412, -5.5, 252.8),
        }

        local function isNearFence(position)
            for _, fencePos in ipairs(FENCE_POSITIONS) do
                if (Vector3.new(position.X, -5.5, position.Z) - Vector3.new(fencePos.X, -5.5, fencePos.Z)).Magnitude <= 20 then
                    return true
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local itemsList = {}
        local allDetectedItems = {}
        local minimumValue = (_G.TeleportMinimum or 5) * 1000000 -- 5M minimum default

        debrisFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
        if debrisFolder then
            for _, obj in ipairs(debrisFolder:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                    local closestPlot = nil
                    local closestPlotDist = math.huge
                    if plotsFolder then
                        for plot, plotData in pairs(plotOwners) do
                            local dx = obj.Position.X - plotData.position.X
                            local dz = obj.Position.Z - plotData.position.Z
                            local dist = math.sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                            if dist < closestPlotDist then
                                closestPlotDist = dist
                                closestPlot = plot
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and plotOwners[closestPlot].isMyPlot then
                        continue
                    end
                    if closestPlotDist > 300 then
                        continue
                    end
                    if closestPlot and plotOwners[closestPlot] and not plotOwners[closestPlot].ownerInGame then
                        continue
                    end

                    local displayNameLabel = nil
                    local generationLabel = nil
                    for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                        if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                            for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                                if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                    if label.Name == "DisplayName" then
                                        displayNameLabel = label
                                    elseif label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then
                                        generationLabel = label
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    if displayNameLabel and generationLabel then
                        local displayName = displayNameLabel.Text or "Unknown"
                        local genText = string.lower(generationLabel.Text or "0")
                        local petValue = parsePetValue(genText)

                        -- Track all detected items for message display (before ProximityPrompt filter)
                        if petValue >= minimumValue then
                            table.insert(allDetectedItems, {
                                value = petValue,
                                name = displayName
                            })
                        end

                        local hasDirectPrompt = false
                        for _, desc in ipairs(obj:GetDescendants()) do
                            if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                hasDirectPrompt = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        if hasDirectPrompt then continue end

                        if petValue >= minimumValue then
                            table.insert(itemsList, {
                                value = petValue,
                                position = obj.Position - Vector3.new(0, 11, 0),
                                name = displayName,
                                priorityLevel = 999
                            })
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if #itemsList == 0 then
            for _, d in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                if d:IsA("TextLabel") and d.Name == "Generation" then
                    local ok, val = pcall(ParseGenerationValue, d.Text)
                    val = ok and val or 0
                    if val >= minimumValue then
                        local attachment = findAncestorOfClass(d, "Attachment")
                        if not attachment then
                            local adorn = findAncestorOfClass(d, "BillboardGui")
                            if adorn and adorn.Adornee and adorn.Adornee:IsA("Attachment") then
                                attachment = adorn.Adornee
                            end
                        end
                        if attachment then
                            local hasDirectPrompt = false
                            local parentModel = attachment.Parent
                            while parentModel and parentModel ~= workspace do
                                for _, desc in ipairs(parentModel:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                        hasDirectPrompt = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                                if hasDirectPrompt then break end
                                parentModel = parentModel.Parent
                            end
                            if not hasDirectPrompt then
                                table.insert(itemsList, {
                                    value = val,
                                    position = attachment.WorldCFrame.Position,
                                    label = d
                                })
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if #itemsList == 0 then
            _G.isTeleporting = false
            return
        end

        warn("[dxhub] Items found: " .. #itemsList .. ", allDetected: " .. #allDetectedItems .. ", minimumValue: " .. minimumValue)
        table.sort(itemsList, function(a, b) return a.value > b.value end)

        local priorityItems = _G.PRIORITY_ANIMALS or {
            "strawberry elephant", "headless horseman", "meowl", "skibidi toilet",
            "hydra dragon cannelloni", "dragon gingerini", "la supreme combinasion",
            "dragon cannelloni", "cerberus", "capitano moby", "la casa boo",
            "cooki and milki", "burguro and fryuro", "ketupat bros", "reinito sleighito",
            "ginger gerat", "spooky and pumpky", "fragrama and chocrama",
            "festive 67", "garama and madundung"
        }

        local function getItemPriority(item)
            if item.priorityLevel and item.priorityLevel < 999 then
                return item.priorityLevel
            end
            if item.name then
                local itemNameLower = item.name:lower()
                for priorityIndex, priorityName in ipairs(priorityItems) do
                    if itemNameLower:find(priorityName, 1, true) then
                        return priorityIndex
                    end
                end
            end
            return 999
        end

        local function getFloorLevel(yPosition)
            if yPosition >= -3.95 and yPosition <= 6.11 then
                return 1
            elseif yPosition >= 11 and yPosition <= 23.15 then
                return 2
            elseif yPosition > 23.15 then
                return 3
            else
                return 0
            end
        end

        local bestOverallItem = nil
        local bestOverallPlotSign = nil
        local bestOverallPriority = 999
        local bestOverallFloor = 0
        local bestOverallValue = 0
        local myPosition = hrp and hrp.Position or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)

local usePriorityMode = _G.TeleportType == "Priority Config" or _G.AutoStealPriorityEnabled or (_G.StealType == "Priority Config")
        local priorityTargetFound = false

        if usePriorityMode and _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget and _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.part and _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget.part.Parent then
            local ct = _G.CurrentAutoStealTarget
            local ctPos = ct.position or (ct.part.Position - Vector3.new(0, 11, 0))
            local closestSign, closestDist = nil, math.huge
            if plotsFolder then
                for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                    local ps = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                    if ps and ps ~= myPlotSign then
                        local d = (ps.Position - ctPos).Magnitude
                        if d < closestDist then closestDist = d; closestSign = ps end
                    end
                end
            end
            if closestSign then
                bestOverallItem = {position = ctPos, value = ct.genValue or ct.value or 0, name = ct.name or "Unknown"}
                bestOverallPlotSign = closestSign
                bestOverallValue = bestOverallItem.value
                priorityTargetFound = true
            end
        end

        if not priorityTargetFound then
        for _, item in ipairs(itemsList) do
            local itemPosition = item.position
            local closestPlotSign = nil
            local closestDistance = math.huge

            if plotsFolder then
                for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                    local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                    if plotSign then
                        local distance = (plotSign.Position - itemPosition).Magnitude
                        if distance < closestDistance then
                            closestDistance = distance
                            closestPlotSign = plotSign
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            if closestPlotSign and closestPlotSign ~= myPlotSign then
                local itemPriority = getItemPriority(item)
                local itemFloor = getFloorLevel(itemPosition.Y)
                local itemValue = item.value

                local shouldSelect = false
                if usePriorityMode then
                    if itemPriority < bestOverallPriority then
                        shouldSelect = true
                    elseif itemPriority == bestOverallPriority then
                        if itemValue > bestOverallValue then
                            shouldSelect = true
                        elseif itemValue == bestOverallValue then
                            if itemFloor > bestOverallFloor then
                                shouldSelect = true
                            end
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if itemValue > bestOverallValue then
                        shouldSelect = true
                    elseif itemValue == bestOverallValue then
                        if itemPriority < bestOverallPriority then
                            shouldSelect = true
                        elseif itemPriority == bestOverallPriority then
                            if itemFloor > bestOverallFloor then
                                shouldSelect = true
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                if shouldSelect then
                    bestOverallItem = item
                    bestOverallPlotSign = closestPlotSign
                    bestOverallPriority = itemPriority
                    bestOverallFloor = itemFloor
                    bestOverallValue = itemValue
                end
            end
        end
        end -- end if not priorityTargetFound

        -- Handle pre-selected steal target (from auto steal panel click)
        local useSelectedTarget = false
        local selectedTargetItem = nil
        local selectedTargetPlotSign = nil
        if _G.SelectedStealTarget and _G.SelectedStealTarget.part and _G.SelectedStealTarget.part.Parent then
            if _G.SelectedStealTarget.directPrompt then
                _G.isTeleporting = false
                return
            else
                local selectedPart = _G.SelectedStealTarget.part
                local selectedPosition = _G.SelectedStealTarget.position or (selectedPart.Position - Vector3.new(0, 11, 0))
                local selectedValue = _G.SelectedStealTarget.value or 0
                local selectedName = _G.SelectedStealTarget.name or "Unknown"
                local closestDistance = math.huge
                if plotsFolder then
                    for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                        local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                        if plotSign then
                            local distance = (plotSign.Position - selectedPosition).Magnitude
                            if distance < closestDistance then
                                closestDistance = distance
                                selectedTargetPlotSign = plotSign
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if selectedTargetPlotSign and selectedTargetPlotSign ~= myPlotSign then
                    useSelectedTarget = true
                    selectedTargetItem = {
                        position = selectedPosition,
                        value = selectedValue,
                        name = selectedName
                    }
                end
            end
        end

        if bestOverallItem then
            _G.AutoTPTargetPosition = bestOverallItem.position
            _G.AutoTPTargetPlotSign = bestOverallPlotSign
        end

        local targetItem, targetPlotSign, bestValue
        if useSelectedTarget and selectedTargetItem and selectedTargetPlotSign then
            targetItem = selectedTargetItem
            targetPlotSign = selectedTargetPlotSign
            bestValue = selectedTargetItem.value
            _G.AutoTPTargetPosition = selectedTargetItem.position
            _G.AutoTPTargetPlotSign = selectedTargetPlotSign
        else
            targetItem = bestOverallItem
            targetPlotSign = bestOverallPlotSign
            bestValue = bestOverallValue
        end

if not targetPlotSign then
            _G.isTeleporting = false
            return
        end

        local nearFence = targetItem and isNearFence(targetItem.position)
        if nearFence then
            warn("[dxhub] Target near fence, doing direct hop TP")
            local fenceHopChar = LocalPlayer.Character
            local fenceHopHRP = fenceHopChar and fenceHopChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local fenceHopHum = fenceHopChar and fenceHopChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            if fenceHopHRP and fenceHopHum then
                pcall(function()
                    local bp = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                    if bp then
                        local carpet = bp:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                        if carpet then fenceHopHum:EquipTool(carpet) end
                    end
                end)

                local directPos = targetItem.position
                local travelSpeed = _G.TPTravelSpeed or 140
                local totalRise = 25
                local startY = fenceHopHRP.Position.Y
                local peakY = startY + totalRise
                local landingY = directPos.Y + 3
                local startHPos = Vector3.new(fenceHopHRP.Position.X, 0, fenceHopHRP.Position.Z)
                local endHPos = Vector3.new(directPos.X, 0, directPos.Z)
                local hDist = (endHPos - startHPos).Magnitude
                local hUnit = hDist > 0.1 and (endHPos - startHPos).Unit or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                local reachedPeak = false
                local startTime = os.clock()
                local lastY = startY

                while fenceHopHRP.Parent do
                    pcall(function()
                        local h = fenceHopChar:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        if h then h.Health = h.MaxHealth end
                    end)

                    local currentPos = fenceHopHRP.Position
                    local currentHPos = Vector3.new(currentPos.X, 0, currentPos.Z)
                    local hDistLeft = (endHPos - currentHPos).Magnitude

                    if hDistLeft < 2 and reachedPeak and math.abs(currentPos.Y - landingY) < 3 then
                        fenceHopHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        break
                    end

                    local dot = hUnit:Dot((endHPos - currentHPos).Unit)
                    if dot < 0 and reachedPeak then
                        fenceHopHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        break
                    end

                    local vVel = 0
                    local hFraction = hDist > 0.1 and math.clamp(1 - (hDistLeft / hDist), 0, 1) or 1

                    if not reachedPeak then
                        if currentPos.Y >= peakY then
                            reachedPeak = true
                            vVel = 0
                        else
                            local remaining = peakY - currentPos.Y
                            vVel = remaining < 5 and math.min(50, remaining * 10) or 80
                            if math.abs(currentPos.Y - lastY) < 0.05 then
                                fenceHopHRP.CFrame = fenceHopHRP.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    if reachedPeak or hFraction >= 0.45 then
                        reachedPeak = true
                        local distDown = currentPos.Y - landingY
                        if distDown > 0.5 then
                            vVel = -math.clamp(distDown * 2.0, 6, 50)
                        elseif distDown < -0.5 then
                            vVel = math.clamp(-distDown * 2.0, 6, 50)
                        else
                            vVel = 0
                        end
                    end

                    lastY = currentPos.Y

                    fenceHopHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(
                        hUnit.X * travelSpeed,
                        vVel,
                        hUnit.Z * travelSpeed
                    )

                    if os.clock() - startTime > 15 then break end
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end

                fenceHopHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                fenceHopHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                fenceHopHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(directPos.X, landingY, directPos.Z)
                fenceHopHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                task.delay(1.5, function() _G.isTeleporting = false end)
            else
                _G.isTeleporting = false
            end
            return
        end
        if (bestValue or 0) < minimumValue then
            _G.isTeleporting = false
            return
        end

        -- Verify target still exists in Debris before committing to TP
        local targetStillExists = false
        pcall(function()

                                    if label:IsA("TextLabel") and label.Name == "DisplayName" then
                                        dName = label.Text
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            if dName then break end

                        if dName and targetItem.name and dName:lower() == targetItem.name:lower() then
                            local dist = (obj.Position - (targetItem.position + Vector3.new(0, 11, 0))).Magnitude
                            if dist < 5 then
                                targetStillExists = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        if not targetStillExists then
            warn("[dxhub] Target no longer exists in Debris, aborting TP")
            _G.isTeleporting = false
            return
        end

        -- Track current steal target info for steal progress display
        if targetItem and targetItem.name then
            _G.CurrentStealingItemName = targetItem.name
            _G.CurrentStealingItemPosition = targetItem.position
            _G.CurrentStealingItemValue = targetItem.value
        end

        -- Show teleport target message
        createMessageBox()
        if msgLabel and targetItem then
            msgLabel.Text = "TP at’ " .. (targetItem.name or "Unknown")
            msgLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            fadeIn()
            task.delay(2, function()
                pcall(fadeOutAndDestroy)
            end)
        end

        local itemPos = targetItem.position
        local itemHeight = targetItem.position.Y
        local signPos = targetPlotSign.Position
        local targetCFrame = targetPlotSign.CFrame

        local isFirstFloor = (itemHeight <= 8.9)
        local isSecondFloor = (itemHeight >= 11 and itemHeight <= 23.15)
        local isThirdFloor = (itemHeight > 23.15)

            local forwardOffset = Vector3.new(directionFromItem.X * 3, 0, directionFromItem.Z * 3)
            local randomZ1 = math.random(-9, 9)
            finalPosition = Vector3.new(signPos.X + forwardOffset.X, -4, signPos.Z + forwardOffset.Z + randomZ1)
        else

            local randomZ1 = math.random(-9, 9)
            finalPosition = targetPlotSign.Position + forwardOffset + Vector3.new(0, 6, randomZ1)

        local facingDirection

            facingDirection = Vector3.new(1, 0, 0)
        else

        if hrp then
            _G.isTeleporting = true
            local autoTurretWasEnabled = _G.autoTurretEnabled
            _G.autoTurretEnabled = false
           warn("[dxhub] Executing TP to: " .. tostring(targetItem and targetItem.name) .. " value=" .. tostring(bestValue))

                local h = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

            local startTime = os.clock()
            local timeout = 15

                        hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero

                hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(finalPosition, finalPosition + facingDirection)

            else

                        local h = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            local hUnit = hDist > 0.1 and (endHPos - startHPos).Unit or Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)

if hDistLeft < 2 and reachedPeak then

                                local playerY = newHRP.Position.Y

                                if playerY <= 35 then
                                    newHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(itemPos.X, 21, itemPos.Z)
                                    newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                    newHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                    TPWait(0.05)
                                    
                                    if (_G.AutoFloatThirdFloor ~= false) and _G.enableFloat then
                                        pcall(function()
                                            local h = newChar:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                            if h then h.Health = h.MaxHealth end
                                        end)

                                        if isInsidePlot(getNearestPlot()) then
                                            -- Step 1: Enable float to rise to 3rd floor
                                            pcall(_G.enableFloat)
                                            
                                            -- Step 2: Wait until we reach 3rd floor height
                                            local floatStartTime = os.clock()
                                            local targetFloatY = itemHeight - 2
                                            while newHRP and newHRP.Parent and os.clock() - floatStartTime < 5 do
                                                if newHRP.Position.Y >= targetFloatY then
                                                    break
                                                end
                                                task.wait(0.05)
                                            end
                                            
                                            -- Step 3: Stop the float
                                            if _G.disableFloat then
                                                pcall(_G.disableFloat)
                                            end
                                            
                                            -- Step 4: Position precisely and anchor in place
                                            pcall(function()
                                                newHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                                newHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                                                newHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(itemPos.X, newHRP.Position.Y, itemPos.Z)
                                                newHRP.Anchored = true
                                            end)

                                            -- Allow jump to cancel anchor
                                            local _anchorJumpConn
                                            _anchorJumpConn = UserInputService.JumpRequest:Connect(function()
                                                if newHRP then newHRP.Anchored = false end
                                                if _anchorJumpConn then _anchorJumpConn:Disconnect(); _anchorJumpConn = nil end
                                            end)

                                            if _G.invisibleStealEnabled and _G.forceStopInvis then
                                                pcall(_G.forceStopInvis)
                                                task.wait(0.1)
                                            end

                                            -- Step 5: Wait until stealing starts, then drop
                                            repeat
                                                if newHRP then newHRP.Anchored = true end
                                                task.wait()
                                            until player:GetAttribute("Stealing") or not newHRP or not newHRP.Parent or (newHRP and not newHRP.Anchored)
                                            
                                            -- Step 6: Unanchor to drop down
                                            if newHRP and newHRP.Parent then
                                                newHRP.Anchored = false
                                            end
                                            if _anchorJumpConn then _anchorJumpConn:Disconnect(); _anchorJumpConn = nil end
                                        else
                                            warn("[dxhub] Float skipped - not inside plot bounds")
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end -- cloner
            end -- cloneChar

            -- ============================================================
            -- After clone: float for third floor ONLY (never second floor)
            -- ============================================================
            if cloneSucceeded and isThirdFloor and itemHeight and itemHeight > 23.15 and _G.TPDirectlyToPet then
                local floatChar = LocalPlayer.Character
                if floatChar then
                    local floatHRP = floatChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    local floatHumanoid = floatChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                    local playerY = floatHRP and floatHRP.Position.Y or 0
                    local onFloor2 = playerY >= 10 and playerY <= 25
                    if floatHRP and floatHumanoid and onFloor2 then
                        pcall(function()
                            local backpack = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                            if backpack then
                                local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.TPSpeedItem or "Flying Carpet")
                                if carpet then
                                    floatHumanoid:EquipTool(carpet)
                                    warn(83)
                                    task.wait(_G.TPCloneWait or 0.1)
                                end
                            end
                        end)

                        floatHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        floatHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        pcall(function()
                            warn(81)
                            floatHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(itemPos.X, 21, itemPos.Z)
                            floatHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            floatHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.05)
                        if (_G.AutoFloatThirdFloor ~= false) and _G.enableFloat then
                            pcall(_G.enableFloat)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            -- ============================================================
            -- LAGBACK PREVENTION (XenHub-style 3 retries)
            -- ============================================================
            local savedFinalPos = finalPosition
            task.spawn(function()
                task.wait(0.15)
                local character = LocalPlayer.Character
                if not character then return end
                local currentHRP = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not currentHRP then return end

                local currentPos = currentHRP.Position
                local distanceFromTarget = (Vector3.new(currentPos.X, 0, currentPos.Z) - Vector3.new(savedFinalPos.X, 0, savedFinalPos.Z)).Magnitude
                local spawnArea = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                local midpointArea = Vector3.new(-381, 27, 86)
                local distanceFromSpawn = (currentPos - spawnArea).Magnitude
                local distanceFromMidpoint = (currentPos - midpointArea).Magnitude

                if distanceFromTarget > 30 and (distanceFromSpawn < 50 or distanceFromMidpoint < 20) then
                    warn("[dxhub] Lagback detected, retrying TP...")
                    _G.skipAutoCloneAfterTP = true
                    pcall(function()
                        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        if humanoid then
                            humanoid:MoveTo(currentHRP.Position)
                            currentHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.2)
                    for retryAttempt = 1, 3 do
                        pcall(function()
                            currentHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            currentHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            currentHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(savedFinalPos)
                            currentHRP.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
                            currentHRP.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.15)
                        local newPos = currentHRP.Position
                        local newDistFromTarget = (Vector3.new(newPos.X, 0, newPos.Z) - Vector3.new(savedFinalPos.X, 0, savedFinalPos.Z)).Magnitude
                        if newDistFromTarget < 30 then
                            _G.skipAutoCloneAfterTP = false
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
            local hasTurretAtPlot = false
            local savedTargetPlotSign = targetPlotSign
            pcall(function()
                if savedTargetPlotSign and savedTargetPlotSign.Parent then
                    local targetPlot = savedTargetPlotSign.Parent
                    for _, descendant in pairs(targetPlot:GetDescendants()) do
                        if descendant.Name and descendant.Name:find("Sentry") then
                            hasTurretAtPlot = true
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    if not hasTurretAtPlot then
                        local plotPos = savedTargetPlotSign.Position
                        for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                            if obj.Name and obj.Name:find("Sentry") then
                                    local sentryPos = nil
                                    pcall(function()
                                        if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                                            sentryPos = obj.Position
                                        elseif obj:IsA("Model") and obj.PrimaryPart then
                                            sentryPos = obj.PrimaryPart.Position
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    if sentryPos and (sentryPos - plotPos).Magnitude < 100 then
                                        hasTurretAtPlot = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                    end
                end
            end)

            --[[if _G.autoCarpetPulloutEnabled then
                task.spawn(function()
                    task.wait(0.05)
                    tryCarpetEquip(5)
                end)
            end]]
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            task.wait(1.5)
            _G.isTeleporting = false
            if autoTurretWasEnabled and _G.AutoDestroyTurretAfterSteal then
                _G.autoTurretEnabled = true
                if _G.scanExistingSentries then
                    pcall(_G.scanExistingSentries)
                end
            end
        end)

        task.delay(3, function()
            _G.usedInsideBaseTP = false
            _G.skipAutoCloneAfterTP = false
        end)
    end) -- end pcall wrapper
        if not success then
            warn("[dxhub] TeleportToHighest error: " .. tostring(err))
            _G.isTeleporting = false
        end
    end

    _G.TeleportToHighest = TeleportToHighest
    warn("[dxhub] TeleportToHighest defined successfully")

local function setupAutoTPOnSpawn(char)
        if not _G.autoTPButtonEnabled then return end
        if _G.skipAutoTPAfterReset then return end  -- vino de insta reset, no hacer TP
        if _G.AutoTPClosestPlayer and _G.insideBaseTPHandledSpawn then return end
        if _G.usedInsideBaseTP then return end

        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

        local hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
        local hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
        if not hrp or not hum then return end

        if not char:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
            char.AncestryChanged:Wait()
        end



if hum:GetState() == Enum.HumanoidStateType.None then
            hum.StateChanged:Wait()
        end
        repeat task.wait(0.01) until hrp and hrp.Parent and hum.Health > 0
        task.wait(0.05)

        for i = 1, 100 do
            if _G.TeleportToHighest then break end
            task.wait(0.01)
        end

        -- Wait until we find at least one valuable brainrot in Debris before TPing
local foundBrainrot = false
        for attempt = 1, 3 do
            local debris = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
            if debris then
                for _, obj in ipairs(debris:GetChildren()) do
                    if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                        for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
                            if child:IsA("BillboardGui") or child:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
                                for _, label in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if label:IsA("TextLabel") and label.Name == "Generation" and (label.Text or ""):find("/s") then
                                        local gt = label.Text:lower()
                                        local v = tonumber(gt:match("[%d%.]+")) or 0
                                        if gt:find("t") then v = v * 1e12
                                        elseif gt:find("b") then v = v * 1e9
                                        elseif gt:find("m") then v = v * 1e6
                                        elseif gt:find("k") then v = v * 1e3 end
                                        if v >= 5000000 then
                                            foundBrainrot = true
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            if foundBrainrot then break end
                        end
                    end
                    if foundBrainrot then break end
                end
            end
            if foundBrainrot then break end
task.wait(0.05)
        end

        if not foundBrainrot then
            warn("[dxhub] No valuable brainrot found after scanning, skipping auto TP")
        end

        warn("[dxhub] Valuable brainrot detected, starting auto TP")

        if not _G.autoTPButtonEnabled then return end
        if _G.AutoTPClosestPlayer and _G.insideBaseTPHandledSpawn then return end
        if _G.usedInsideBaseTP then return end

        if _G.TeleportToHighest and hum.Health > 0 then
            local ok, err = pcall(function()
                repeat task.wait(0.01) until game:IsLoaded()
                _G.TeleportToHighest()
            end)
            if not ok then
                warn("[dxhub] Auto TP on spawn error: " .. tostring(err))
                _G.isTeleporting = false
            end
            task.delay(3, function()
                _G.isTeleporting = false
            end)
        end
    end

LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        task.spawn(function()
            local hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
            local hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
            if not hrp or not hum then return end
repeat task.wait(0.05) until hum.Health > 0 and hum:GetState() ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead and char:IsDescendantOf(workspace)
            task.wait(0.2)
-- Wait for min 40 fps before TPing
            local fpsWait = 0
            repeat
                task.wait(0.03)
                fpsWait = fpsWait + 0.03
                local t = tick()
                RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                local fps = 1 / (tick() - t)
                if fps >= 40 then break end
            until fpsWait >= 5
            -- Force full health before TP
            pcall(function() hum.Health = hum.MaxHealth end)
            setupAutoTPOnSpawn(char)
        end)
    end)

    if LocalPlayer.Character and _G.autoTPButtonEnabled then
        task.spawn(function()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
            local hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
            if not hrp or not hum then return end
            repeat task.wait(0.05) until hum.Health > 0 and hum:GetState() ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead and char:IsDescendantOf(workspace)
            task.wait(0.2)
-- Wait for min 40 fps before TPing
            local fpsWait = 0
            repeat
                task.wait(0.03)
                fpsWait = fpsWait + 0.03
                local t = tick()
                RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                local fps = 1 / (tick() - t)
                if fps >= 40 then break end
            until fpsWait >= 5
            -- Force full health before TP
            pcall(function() hum.Health = hum.MaxHealth end)
            setupAutoTPOnSpawn(char)
        end)
    end

    _G.toggleAutoTP = function()
        _G.autoTPButtonEnabled = not _G.autoTPButtonEnabled
        _G.AutoTeleportEnabled = _G.autoTPButtonEnabled
        if _G.autoTPButtonEnabled and LocalPlayer.Character then
            local hum = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if hum and hum.Health > 0 then
                task.spawn(function()
                    tryCarpetEquip(5)
                    if _G.TeleportToHighest then
                        local ok, err = pcall(_G.TeleportToHighest)
                        if not ok then
                            warn("[dxhub] Toggle auto TP error: " .. tostring(err))
                            _G.isTeleporting = false
                        end
                        task.delay(3, function()
                            _G.isTeleporting = false
                        end)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
        return _G.autoTPButtonEnabled
    end

end)

task.spawn(function()

    if game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("22SJobIDSpammer") then
        game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("22SJobIDSpammer"):Destroy()
    end

    local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    ScreenGui.Name = "22SJobIDSpammer"
    ScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    ScreenGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
    ScreenGui.Parent = game.CoreGui

    local MainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    MainFrame.Name = "MainFrame"
    MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 340 or 450, 0, isMobile and 45 or 50)
    MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -(isMobile and 170 or 225), 1, -(isMobile and 200 or 260))
    MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 14, 16)
    MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.1
    MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    MainFrame.Active = true
    MainFrame.Visible = false
    MainFrame.Parent = ScreenGui

    Instance.new("UICorner", MainFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)


    local dragging = false
    local dragStart, startPos

    MainFrame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            dragStart = input.Position
            startPos = MainFrame.Position

            input.Changed:Connect(function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    dragging = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
            local delta = input.Position - dragStart
            MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        if input.KeyCode == (_G.JobIDSpammerKey or Enum.KeyCode.J) then
            MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
        end
    end)

    _G.toggleJobIDSpammer = function()
        MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
        return MainFrame.Visible
    end

    local JoinButton = Instance.new("TextButton", MainFrame)
    JoinButton.Name = "JoinButton"
    JoinButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 45 or 55, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
    JoinButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
    JoinButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
    JoinButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
    JoinButton.Text = "Join"
    JoinButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    JoinButton.TextSize = isMobile and 11 or 14
    JoinButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    Instance.new("UICorner", JoinButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local JobIDBox = Instance.new("TextBox", MainFrame)
    JobIDBox.Name = "JobIDBox"
    JobIDBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 100 or 120, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
    JobIDBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 60 or 75, 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
    JobIDBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
    JobIDBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
    JobIDBox.Text = ""
    JobIDBox.PlaceholderText = "Job ID..."
    JobIDBox.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)
    JobIDBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    JobIDBox.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 13
    JobIDBox.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    JobIDBox.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
    JobIDBox.ClipsDescendants = true
    JobIDBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    Instance.new("UICorner", JobIDBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local JobIDPadding = Instance.new("UIPadding", JobIDBox)
    JobIDPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 6)
    JobIDPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local ClearButton = Instance.new("TextButton", MainFrame)
    ClearButton.Name = "ClearButton"
    ClearButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 45 or 55, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
    ClearButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 165 or 200, 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
    ClearButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
    ClearButton.BorderSizePixel = 0

    Instance.new("UICorner", ClearButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    ClearButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        JobIDBox.Text = ""
    end)

    local AttemptsLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", MainFrame)
    AttemptsLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 45 or 55, 0, 12)
    AttemptsLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 215 or 258, 0, 4)
    AttemptsLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    AttemptsLabel.Text = "Attempts"
    AttemptsLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)
    AttemptsLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
    AttemptsLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    AttemptsLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center

    local AttemptsBox = Instance.new("TextBox", MainFrame)
    AttemptsBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 45 or 55, 0, isMobile and 20 or 22)
    AttemptsBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 215 or 258, 0, isMobile and 18 or 22)
    AttemptsBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
    AttemptsBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
    AttemptsBox.Text = "2000"
    AttemptsBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    AttemptsBox.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
    AttemptsBox.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    AttemptsBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    Instance.new("UICorner", AttemptsBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local DelayLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", MainFrame)
    DelayLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 40 or 55, 0, 12)
    DelayLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 265 or 320, 0, 4)
    DelayLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    DelayLabel.Text = "Delay"
    DelayLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 195)
    DelayLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
    DelayLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    DelayLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center

    local DelayBox = Instance.new("TextBox", MainFrame)
    DelayBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 40 or 55, 0, isMobile and 20 or 22)
    DelayBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 265 or 320, 0, isMobile and 18 or 22)
    DelayBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
    DelayBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
    DelayBox.Text = "0.01"
    DelayBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    DelayBox.TextSize = isMobile and 10 or 12
    DelayBox.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    DelayBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    Instance.new("UICorner", DelayBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local StatusLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", MainFrame)
    StatusLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, isMobile and 55 or 70, 0, isMobile and 26 or 30)
    StatusLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -(isMobile and 60 or 75), 0.5, -(isMobile and 13 or 15))
    StatusLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    StatusLabel.Text = ""
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 205, 215)
    StatusLabel.TextSize = isMobile and 9 or 11
    StatusLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    StatusLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right

    local isSpamming = false

    local function joinServer(jobId)
        pcall(function() if _G.saveKeybinds then _G.saveKeybinds() end end)
        pcall(function() if _G.autoSavePositions then _G.autoSavePositions() end end)
        local success = pcall(function()
            --pcall(function() TeleportService:SetTeleportData({Keybinds = _G.savedBinds or savedBinds}) end)
            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, jobId, LocalPlayer)
        end)
        return success
    end

    JoinButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if isSpamming then
            isSpamming = false
            JoinButton.Text = "Join"
            JoinButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
            StatusLabel.Text = ""
            return
        end

        local jobId = JobIDBox.Text
        local attempts = tonumber(AttemptsBox.Text) or 2000
        local delay = tonumber(DelayBox.Text) or 0.01

        if jobId == "" then
            TweenService:Create(JobIDBox, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 30, 30)}):Play()
            task.wait(0.1)
            TweenService:Create(JobIDBox, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)}):Play()
            return
        end

        isSpamming = true
        JoinButton.Text = "Stop"
        JoinButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 40, 40)

        task.spawn(function()
            for i = 1, attempts do
                if not isSpamming then break end
                StatusLabel.Text = i .. "/" .. attempts
                joinServer(jobId)
                task.wait(delay)
            end
            isSpamming = false
            JoinButton.Text = "Join"
            JoinButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)
            StatusLabel.Text = "Done"
            task.wait(1)
            if StatusLabel.Text == "Done" then
                StatusLabel.Text = ""
            end
        end)
    end)

    JoinButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if not isSpamming then
            TweenService:Create(JoinButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 38, 48)}):Play()
        end
    end)
    JoinButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if not isSpamming then
            TweenService:Create(JoinButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)}):Play()
        else
            JoinButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 40, 40)
        end
    end)

    ClearButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(ClearButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 38, 48)}):Play()
    end)
    ClearButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(ClearButton, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 26, 32)}):Play()
    end)

end)

task.spawn(function()
    local setFFlag = setfflag or SetFastFlag or setfastflag or SetFFlag
    if not setFFlag then _G.FastFlagsApplied = false return end

    local success = pcall(function()
        -- Telemetry
        for _, name in ipairs({"FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryEphemeralCounter","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryEphemeralStat","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryEventIngest","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryPoint","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryV2Counter","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryV2Event","FFlagDebugDisableTelemetryV2Stat"}) do
            setFFlag(name, "True")
        end
        setFFlag("DFFlagDebugAnalyticsSendUserId", "False")
        -- Rendering
        setFFlag("DFIntTaskSchedulerTargetFps", "9999")
        setFFlag("FFlagEnableInGameMenuChrome", "False")
        setFFlag("FFlagDisablePostFx", "True")
        setFFlag("DFIntMaxFrameBufferSize", "4")
        setFFlag("FIntRenderGrassDetailStrands", "0")
        setFFlag("DFIntDebugFRMQualityLevelOverride", "1")
        setFFlag("FIntRenderShadowIntensity", "0")

        ["FIntMaxParticlesPerEmitter"] = "0",

        ["FIntWaterDetailLevel"] = "0",

        ["FFlagEnableFacialAnimation"] = "False",
        ["DFFlagEnableLipSync"] = "False",
        ["DFIntAnimatorThrottleMaxDistance"] = "0",
        ["DFIntAnimatorThrottleMinDistance"] = "0",
        ["FFlagAnimatorThrottling"] = "True",
        ["FFlagEnableFRM"] = "False",
        ["FIntFRMQuality"] = "0",
        ["FFlagEnableVoiceChat"] = "False",
        ["FFlagVoiceChatEnabled"] = "False",
        ["DFIntMemoryMaxMB"] = "2048",
        ["FFlagEnablePhysicsOptimizations"] = "True",
        ["DFIntPhysicsStepRate"] = "240",
        ["DFIntHttpMaxConnections"] = "32",
        ["DFIntRenderThreadCount"] = "4",
        ["FFlagEnableMultithreadedRendering"] = "True",
        ["DFIntRenderJobsCount"] = "4",
        ["DFIntStreamingRadius"] = "256",
        ["DFIntStreamingTargetRadius"] = "384",
        ["DFIntCPUThrottlePercent"] = "0",
        ["FFlagDisableCPUThrottle"] = "True",
        ["DFIntGPUThrottlePercent"] = "0",
        ["FFlagDisableGPUThrottle"] = "True",
        ["FFlagEnableMicroProfiler"] = "False",
        ["FFlagEnableDebugStats"] = "False"
