    local setFFlag = setfflag or SetFastFlag or setfastflag or SetFFlag
    if setFFlag then
        for flag, value in pairs(fflags) do
            pcall(function()
                setFFlag(flag, value)
            end)
        end
    end

    pcall(function() rconsoleclose() end)
    pcall(function() clearconsole() end)
    pcall(function() game:GetService("LogService"):ClearOutput() end)

    local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
    local players = game:GetService("Players")
    local terrain = workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain")

    local processedModels = {}

    local function applyLighting()
        pcall(function()
            lighting.GlobalShadows = false
            lighting.FogEnd = 9e9
            lighting.Brightness = 3
            lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.ShadowSoftness = 0
            lighting.ClockTime = 0
            lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0
            lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 0
            lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        end)
    end

    local function stopAnimations(model)
        if not model or processedModels[model] then return end
        processedModels[model] = true
        for _, v in pairs(model:GetDescendants()) do
            pcall(function()
                if v:IsA("Animator") then
                    for _, track in pairs(v:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                        track:Stop()
                        track:Destroy()
                    end
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("Animation") or v:IsA("AnimationController") then
                    v:Destroy()
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local function stripCharacter(character)
        if not character then return end
        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            pcall(function()
                if v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("ShirtGraphic") or v:IsA("Accessory") then
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("Decal") and v.Name == "face" then
                    v:Destroy()
                elseif v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                    v.TextureID = ""
                elseif v:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                    v.TextureId = ""
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    local function cleanObject(v)
        if protectedBeamNames[v.Name] then return end
        if v:IsA("Beam") and v.Parent and v.Parent.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then return end
        if v:IsA("Attachment") and v.Parent and v.Parent.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then return end

        pcall(function()
            if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or v:IsA("Trail") or v:IsA("Smoke") or v:IsA("Fire") or v:IsA("Sparkles") then
                v.Enabled = false
            elseif v:IsA("Beam") then
                v.Enabled = false
            elseif v:IsA("Decal") or v:IsA("Texture") then
                v:Destroy()
            elseif v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                v.Reflectance = 0
                v.TextureID = ""
            elseif v:IsA("Part") or v:IsA("BasePart") then
                v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                v.Reflectance = 0
            elseif v:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                v.TextureId = ""
            elseif v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("ShirtGraphic") then
                v:Destroy()
            end
        end)
    end

    for _, child in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Atmosphere") or child:IsA("Clouds") or child:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or child:IsA("BlurEffect") or child:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or child:IsA("BloomEffect") or child:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
            pcall(function() child:Destroy() end)
        end
    end

    applyLighting()

    lighting.Changed:Connect(applyLighting)

    task.spawn(function()
        while _G.FPSBoostEnabled and task.wait(1) do
            applyLighting()
        end
    end)

    if terrain then
        pcall(function()
            terrain.WaterWaveSize = 0
            terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
            terrain.WaterReflectance = 0
            terrain.WaterTransparency = 0
            terrain.Decoration = false
        end)
    end

    pcall(function() settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 1 end)
    pcall(function() sethiddenproperty(lighting, "Technology", 2) end)

    -- Batched processing: yield every 200 objects to prevent massive frame drop on load-in
    task.spawn(function()
        local descendants = workspace:GetDescendants()
        local BATCH_SIZE = 200
        for i = 1, #descendants, BATCH_SIZE do
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then break end
            local batchEnd = math.min(i + BATCH_SIZE - 1, #descendants)
            for j = i, batchEnd do
                local v = descendants[j]
                if v and v.Parent then
                    cleanObject(v)
                    if v:IsA("Model") then
                        stopAnimations(v)
                    end
                end
            end
            if i + BATCH_SIZE <= #descendants then
                task.wait() -- Yield to let frames render between batches
            end
        end
    end)

    workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(v)
        if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
        task.wait()
        cleanObject(v)
        if v:IsA("Model") then
            stopAnimations(v)
        end
    end)

    for _, player in pairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character then
            stripCharacter(player.Character)
        end
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
            task.wait(1)
            stripCharacter(character)
        end)
    end

    players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
            if not _G.FPSBoostEnabled then return end
            task.wait(1)
            stripCharacter(character)
        end)
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        while _G.FPSBoostEnabled and task.wait(3) do
            for _, player in pairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    stripCharacter(player.Character)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end
]]
task.spawn(function()
    local Player = Players.LocalPlayer

    if not Player then return end

    local activeSentryConnections = {}

    local function handleSentry(child, immediate)
        if not child or not child.Parent then return end
        if not child.Name or not child.Name:find("Sentry") then return end
        if _G.isTeleporting then return end
        if not _G.autoTurretEnabled then return end

        if activeSentryConnections[child] then return end

        local sentry_owner_id = child.Name:match("Sentry_(%d+)")
        if sentry_owner_id and tonumber(sentry_owner_id) == Player.UserId then return end

        if not immediate then
            local setupReady = child:FindFirstChild("SetupReady")
            if not setupReady then
                local waitTime = 0
                while not setupReady and child.Parent and waitTime < 5 do
                    task.wait(0.1)
                    setupReady = child:FindFirstChild("SetupReady")
                    waitTime = waitTime + 0.1
                end
                if not child.Parent then return end
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end

        local sentryPart = nil
        if child:IsA("BasePart") then
            sentryPart = child
        elseif child:IsA("Model") then
            sentryPart = child.PrimaryPart or child:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
            if not sentryPart then
                for _, desc in ipairs(child:GetDescendants()) do
                    if desc:IsA("BasePart") then
                        sentryPart = desc
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if not sentryPart then return end

        pcall(function()
            sentryPart.CanCollide = false
            sentryPart.Transparency = 1
            sentryPart.Size = Vector3.new(10, 10, 10)
        end)

        local previouslyEquippedTool = nil
        if Player.Character then
            for _, item in pairs(Player.Character:GetChildren()) do
                if item:IsA("Tool") then
                    previouslyEquippedTool = item
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        local last_attack = 0
        local equipAttempts = 0

        local heartbeat_conn
        heartbeat_conn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if _G.isTeleporting or not _G.autoTurretEnabled or not child or not child.Parent then
                if heartbeat_conn then
                    heartbeat_conn:Disconnect()
                    activeSentryConnections[child] = nil
                end
                if not child.Parent and Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                    pcall(function()
                        Player.Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
                        if previouslyEquippedTool then
                            local toolToEquip = Player.Backpack:FindFirstChild(previouslyEquippedTool.Name)
                            if toolToEquip then
                                Player.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(toolToEquip)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return
            end

            local now = tick()
            if now - last_attack < 0.008 then return end
            last_attack = now

            if Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local hrp = Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                local targetCFrame = hrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -2)

                pcall(function()
                    if child:IsA("Model") and child.PrimaryPart then
                        child:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(targetCFrame)
                    elseif sentryPart then
                        sentryPart.CFrame = targetCFrame
                    end
                end)

                local bat = Player.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Bat") or (Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Bat"))
                if bat then
                    if bat.Parent == Player.Backpack then
                        equipAttempts = equipAttempts + 1
                        if equipAttempts <= 5 then
                            pcall(function()
                                Player.Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
                                Player.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(bat)
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                    if bat.Parent == Player.Character then
                        equipAttempts = 0
                        pcall(function()
                            bat:Activate()
                            bat:Activate()
                            bat:Activate()
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        activeSentryConnections[child] = heartbeat_conn
    end

    local function scanExistingSentries()
        if _G.isTeleporting then return end

        task.spawn(function()
            local sentryFolders = {}
            local plotsF = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if plotsF then table.insert(sentryFolders, plotsF) end
            local debrisF = workspace:FindFirstChild("Debris")
            if debrisF then table.insert(sentryFolders, debrisF) end

            for attempt = 1, 3 do
                for _, folder in ipairs(sentryFolders) do
                    pcall(function()
                        for _, child in pairs(folder:GetDescendants()) do
                            if child and child.Name and child.Name:find("Sentry") then
                                task.spawn(function()
                                    handleSentry(child, true)
                                end)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
                if attempt < 3 then task.wait(0.3) end
            end
        end)
    end

    _G.scanExistingSentries = scanExistingSentries

    _G.toggleAutoTurret = function()
        _G.autoTurretEnabled = not _G.autoTurretEnabled
        if _G.autoTurretEnabled then
            scanExistingSentries()
        end
        return _G.autoTurretEnabled
    end

    workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child and child.Name and child.Name:find("Sentry") then
            task.spawn(function()
                handleSentry(child, false)
            end)
        end
    end)

    if _G.autoTurretEnabled then
        scanExistingSentries()
    end

end)

task.spawn(function()

    _G.unlockCurrentBase = function()
        pcall(function()
            local plotsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
            if not plotsFolder then return end

            local character = LocalPlayer.Character
            if not character then return end
            local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end

            local closestPlot = nil
            local closestDist = math.huge

            for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
                local plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign")
                if plotSign then
                    local dist = (plotSign.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
                    if dist < closestDist then
                        closestDist = dist
                        closestPlot = plot
                    end
                end
            end

            if closestPlot and closestDist < 150 then
                for _, desc in ipairs(closestPlot:GetDescendants()) do
                    if desc:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                        local promptText = (desc.ObjectText or ""):lower()
                        local actionText = (desc.ActionText or ""):lower()
                        if promptText:find("door") or promptText:find("unlock") or actionText:find("open") or actionText:find("unlock") then
                            pcall(function()
                                fireproximityprompt(desc)
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
    end
end)


task.spawn(function()
    local plr = Players.LocalPlayer
    if not plr then return end

    _G.FloatEnabled = _G.FloatEnabled or false
    local floatPlatform = nil
    local function getHRP()
        local c = plr.Character; if not c then return end
        return c:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    end
    local stopFloat
    local function startFloat()
        if floatPlatform then floatPlatform:Destroy() end
        floatPlatform = Instance.new("Part")
        floatPlatform.Size = Vector3.new(6, 1, 6)
        floatPlatform.Anchored = true
        floatPlatform.CanCollide = true
        floatPlatform.Transparency = 1
        floatPlatform.Parent = workspace
        task.spawn(function()
            while _G.FloatEnabled and floatPlatform do
                local isStealing = plr:GetAttribute("Stealing")

                if isStealing then
                    stopFloat()
                    break
                end

                local hrp = getHRP()
                if hrp then
                    local targetPos = hrp.Position - Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                    floatPlatform.Position = floatPlatform.Position:Lerp(targetPos, 0.5)
                end

                RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
            end
        end)
    end
    stopFloat = function()
        _G.FloatEnabled = false
        if floatPlatform then floatPlatform:Destroy(); floatPlatform = nil end
    end
    _G.enableFloat = function()
        local char = plr.Character
        if not char then return end
        local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not hum or hum.Health <= 0 then return end
        _G.FloatEnabled = true
        startFloat()
    end
    _G.disableFloat = function() stopFloat() end
    _G.toggleFloat = function()
        if _G.FloatEnabled then _G.disableFloat() else _G.enableFloat() end
        return _G.FloatEnabled
    end
    plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
        stopFloat()
        _G.FloatEnabled = false
    end)
    if isMobile then
        UserInputService.JumpRequest:Connect(function()
            if _G.FloatEnabled then stopFloat() end
        end)
    end

end)

task.spawn(function()
    task.wait(0.1)
    local GuiService = game:GetService("GuiService")
    local frameCount = 0

    _track(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        frameCount = frameCount + 1
        if frameCount >= 90 then
            frameCount = 0
            if not _G.KICK_IN_PROGRESS and _G.ClearErrorEnabled ~= false then
                pcall(GuiService.ClearError, GuiService)
            end
        end
    end))
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local CoreGui = game:GetService("CoreGui")

    local function hideErrorGuis()
        if _G.ClearErrorEnabled == false then return end

        pcall(function()
            local promptGui = CoreGui:FindFirstChild("RobloxPromptGui")
            if promptGui then
                for _, child in pairs(promptGui:GetDescendants()) do
                    if child:IsA("Frame") or child:IsA("TextLabel") or child:IsA("ImageLabel") then
                        child.Visible = false
                    end
                end
            end

            local errorGui = CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ErrorGui")
            if errorGui then
                errorGui.Enabled = false
            end

            local purchasePrompt = CoreGui:FindFirstChild("PurchasePromptApp")
            if purchasePrompt and purchasePrompt:FindFirstChild("ErrorFrame") then
                purchasePrompt.ErrorFrame.Visible = false
            end
        end)
    end

    local _hideErrorCounter = 0
    _track(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        if _G.ClearErrorEnabled ~= false then
            _hideErrorCounter = _hideErrorCounter + 1
            if _hideErrorCounter >= 120 then -- ~2 seconds at 60fps
                _hideErrorCounter = 0
                hideErrorGuis()
            end
        end
    end))

    _track(CoreGui.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(descendant)
        if _G.ClearErrorEnabled ~= false then
            task.wait()
            hideErrorGuis()
        end
    end))

end)

task.spawn(function()
    while _loopFlags.running do
        pcall(function()
            local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if character then
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
                    if animator then
local tracks = animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
                        if #tracks > 50 then
                            for i = 1, #tracks - 30 do
                                pcall(function() tracks[i]:Stop(0) end)
                            end
end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        task.wait(2)
    end
end)
